### [Sessão Paralela: Tech Leader]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V12 Core - Arquitetura Técnica

## 1. Architecture Decision Record - ADR-001: Estratégia de Refatoração V12

**ADR-001: Refatoração Incremental com Modo Hive**
**Data:** 2024-01-15
**Status:** Aceita
**Autores:** Tech Lead V12

### CONTEXTO:
O DIYAPP atual possui código legado com:
- Acoplamento excessivo entre módulos
- Dívida técnica acumulada (testes < 60%)
- Performance degradada em operações batch
- Manutenção custosa para novas features

Forças em jogo:
- Necessidade de manter sistema 100% operacional durante transição
- Time distribuído trabalhando em paralelo
- Requisito de estabilidade autônoma
- Prazo de 6 meses para completa migração

### DECISÃO:
Adotar estratégia de **Refatoração Incremental com Modo Hive**:
1. Dividir sistema em "colmeias" (hives) independentes
2. Cada hive opera em paralelo com isolamento completo
3. Gateway de roteamento inteligente (HiveRouter)
4. Migração gradual por domínio de negócio
5. Rollback automático por hive

### OPÇÕES CONSIDERADAS:
- **Opção A: Big Bang Rewrite** — Prós: Arquitetura limpa desde início. Contras: Risco extremo, downtime prolongado, paralização do negócio.
- **Opção B: Refatoração Incremental Tradicional** — Prós: Baixo risco. Contras: Lento, dependências bloqueiam progresso.
- **Opção C: Modo Hive (escolhida)** — Prós: Paralelismo máximo, isolamento de falhas, rollback granular. Contras: Complexidade inicial do router.

### CONSEQUÊNCIAS:
**Positivas:**
- 100% uptime garantido durante migração
- Times podem trabalhar independentemente
- Testes A/B por feature flag
- Rollback por módulo específico

**Negativas:**
- Overhead inicial de 15% para infra do HiveRouter
- Duplicação temporária de código
- Complexidade de deploy aumentada

**Riscos:**
- Configuração incorreta do router → Mitigação: testes E2E automatizados
- Inconsistência de dados entre hives → Mitigação: Sincronização bidirecional
- Performance do gateway → Mitigação: Load testing contínuo

**REVISÃO:** 2024-04-15 (após 3 meses)

---

## 2. Engineering Standards V12

```javascript
// engineering-standards-v12.md
# DIYAPP V12 - Engineering Standards

## 1. Estrutura de Projeto
```
src/
├── hives/                    # Colmeias independentes
│   ├── hive-auth/           # Autenticação V12
│   ├── hive-payments/       # Pagamentos V12  
│   └── hive-legacy/         # Código legado encapsulado
├── shared/
│   ├── types/               # TypeScript definitions
│   ├── utils/               # Utilitários cross-hive
│   └── contracts/           # Contratos de API
├── gateway/                 # HiveRouter
└── monitoring/              # APM e observabilidade
```

## 2. Padrões de Código
### 2.1 TypeScript Strict
```typescript
// tsconfig.json
{
  "compilerOptions": {
    "strict": true,
    "noImplicitAny": true,
    "strictNullChecks": true,
    "strictFunctionTypes": true,
    "noUnusedLocals": true,
    "noUnusedParameters": true
  }
}
```

### 2.2 Convenções de Nomenclatura
- Interfaces: `IUserRepository`
- Types: `UserDTO`, `PaymentRequest`
- Classes: `UserService`, `PaymentProcessor`
- Constantes: `MAX_RETRY_ATTEMPTS`
- Arquivos: `kebab-case.ts`

### 2.3 Tratamento de Erros
```typescript
// ERRADO
try { /* ... */ } catch (error) { console.log(error) }

// CORRETO
try {
  // ...
} catch (error) {
  if (error instanceof ValidationError) {
    throw new BusinessError('Invalid input', { cause: error });
  }
  logger.error('Operation failed', { error, context });
  throw new SystemError('Internal error', { originalError: error });
}
```

## 3. Testes
- Cobertura mínima: 85%
- Testes E2E por hive
- Contract testing entre hives
- Performance tests semanais

## 4. Commits
```
feat(auth): add MFA support
fix(payments): handle declined transactions
refactor(legacy): extract user validation
test(gateway): add routing tests
chore(deps): update axios to v2
```

## 5. Code Review Checklist
- [ ] Cobertura de testes ≥ 85%
- [ ] TypeScript strict mode
- [ ] Error handling apropriado
- [ ] Logging estruturado
- [ ] Métricas expostas
- [ ] Documentação de API atualizada
```

## 3. Stack de Monitorização (APM)

```yaml
# docker-compose.monitoring.yml
version: '3.8'

services:
  # Coleta de métricas
  prometheus:
    image: prom/prometheus:v2.45.0
    volumes:
      - ./monitoring/prometheus.yml:/etc/prometheus/prometheus.yml
      - prometheus-data:/prometheus
    command:
      - '--config.file=/etc/prometheus/prometheus.yml'
      - '--storage.tsdb.retention.time=30d'
    ports:
      - "9090:9090"

  # Visualização
  grafana:
    image: grafana/grafana:10.0.0
    environment:
      - GF_SECURITY_ADMIN_PASSWORD=${GRAFANA_PASSWORD}
    volumes:
      - grafana-data:/var/lib/grafana
      - ./monitoring/dashboards:/etc/grafana/provisioning/dashboards
    ports:
      - "3000:3000"

  # Rastreamento distribuído
  jaeger:
    image: jaegertracing/all-in-one:1.47
    environment:
      - COLLECTOR_OTLP_ENABLED=true
    ports:
      - "16686:16686"
      - "4317:4317"
      - "4318:4318"

  # Logs centralizados
  loki:
    image: grafana/loki:2.9.0
    command: -config.file=/etc/loki/local-config.yaml
    ports:
      - "3100:3100"

  # Agente de métricas da aplicação
  diyapp-monitor:
    build: ./monitoring/agent
    environment:
      - OTEL_SERVICE_NAME=diyapp-v12
      - OTEL_EXPORTER_OTLP_ENDPOINT=http://jaeger:4318
    volumes:
      - ./src:/app
    depends_on:
      - jaeger
      - prometheus

volumes:
  prometheus-data:
  grafana-data:
```

```typescript
// monitoring/agent/index.ts
import { NodeSDK } from '@opentelemetry/sdk-node';
import { getNodeAutoInstrumentations } from '@opentelemetry/auto-instrumentations-node';
import { OTLPTraceExporter } from '@opentelemetry/exporter-trace-otlp-grpc';
import { OTLPMetricExporter } from '@opentelemetry/exporter-metrics-otlp-grpc';
import { PeriodicExportingMetricReader } from '@opentelemetry/sdk-metrics';
import { WinstonInstrumentation } from '@opentelemetry/instrumentation-winston';
import { HttpInstrumentation } from '@opentelemetry/instrumentation-http';

const sdk = new NodeSDK({
  traceExporter: new OTLPTraceExporter({
    url: 'http://jaeger:4317'
  }),
  metricReader: new PeriodicExportingMetricReader({
    exporter: new OTLPMetricExporter({
      url: 'http://prometheus:9090/api/v1/otlp'
    }),
    exportIntervalMillis: 60000
  }),
  instrumentations: [
    getNodeAutoInstrumentations(),
    new WinstonInstrumentation(),
    new HttpInstrumentation()
  ]
});

sdk.start();

// Middleware de métricas para Express
import express from 'express';
import { metricsMiddleware } from './middleware/metrics';

const app = express();
app.use(metricsMiddleware);

// Health checks por hive
app.get('/health/hive/:hiveName', async (req, res) => {
  const { hiveName } = req.params;
  const health = await checkHiveHealth(hiveName);
  
  res.json({
    status: health.healthy ? 'healthy' : 'unhealthy',
    timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
    metrics: health.metrics,
    dependencies: health.dependencies
  });
});

export { sdk, app };
```

---

## 4. HiveRouter - Gateway Inteligente

```typescript
// gateway/HiveRouter.ts
import express from 'express';
import { createProxyMiddleware } from 'http-proxy-middleware';
import { HiveRegistry } from './HiveRegistry';
import { CircuitBreaker } from './CircuitBreaker';
import { MetricsCollector } from './MetricsCollector';
import { MigrationManager } from './MigrationManager';

export class HiveRouter {
  private app: express.Application;
  private registry: HiveRegistry;
  private circuitBreakers: Map<string, CircuitBreaker>;
  private metrics: MetricsCollector;
  private migration: MigrationManager;

  constructor() {
    this.app = express();
    this.registry = new HiveRegistry();
    this.circuitBreakers = new Map();
    this.metrics = new MetricsCollector();
    this.migration = new MigrationManager();
    
    this.setupMiddleware();
    this.setupRoutes();
  }

  private setupMiddleware(): void {
    // Logging estruturado
    this.app.use((req, res, next) => {
      const start = Date.now();
      res.on('finish', () => {
        this.metrics.recordRequest({
          method: req.method,
          path: req.path,
          status: res.statusCode,
          duration: Date.now() - start,
          hive: this.registry.getHiveForPath(req.path)
        });
      });
      next();
    });

    // Rate limiting por hive
    this.app.use(this.rateLimitByHive.bind(this));
  }

  private setupRoutes(): void {
    // Roteamento dinâmico baseado em feature flags
    this.app.all('*', async (req, res) => {
      try {
        const targetHive = await this.determineTargetHive(req);
        
        // Verifica circuit breaker
        const circuitBreaker = this.getCircuitBreaker(targetHive);
        if (!circuitBreaker.allowRequest()) {
          return this.fallbackToLegacy(req, res);
        }

        // Proxy para hive destino
        const proxy = createProxyMiddleware({
          target: targetHive.url,
          changeOrigin: true,
          onError: (err, req, res) => {
            circuitBreaker.recordFailure();
            this.fallbackToLegacy(req, res);
          },
          onProxyRes: () => {
            circuitBreaker.recordSuccess();
          }
        });

        proxy(req, res, () => {});
      } catch (error) {
        this.metrics.recordError(error);
        this.fallbackToLegacy(req, res);
      }
    });
  }

  private async determineTargetHive(req: express.Request): Promise<HiveConfig> {
    const path = req.path;
    const user = await this.getUserFromRequest(req);
    
    // Verifica feature flag por usuário
    const useV12 = await this.migration.shouldUseV12(path, user);
    
    if (useV12) {
      return this.registry.getV12Hive(path);
    } else {
      return this.registry.getLegacyHive(path);
    }
  }

  private fallbackToLegacy(req: express.Request, res: express.Response): void {
    const legacyHive = this.registry.getLegacyHive(req.path);
    const proxy = createProxyMiddleware({
      target: legacyHive.url,
      changeOrigin: true
    });
    
    this.metrics.recordFallback(req.path);
    proxy(req, res, () => {});
  }

  private getCircuitBreaker(hive: HiveConfig): CircuitBreaker {
    if (!this.circuitBreakers.has(hive.name)) {
      this.circuitBreakers.set(hive.name, new CircuitBreaker({
        failureThreshold: 5,
        resetTimeout: 30000,
        halfOpenMaxAttempts: 3
      }));
    }
    return this.circuitBreakers.get(hive.name)!;
  }

  private rateLimitByHive(req: express.Request, res: express.Response, next: Function): void {
    const hive = this.registry.getHiveForPath(req.path);
    const clientId = this.getClientId(req);
    
    const key = `${hive}:${clientId}`;
    const requests = this.requestCounts.get(key) || 0;
    
    if (requests > this.getRateLimit(hive)) {
      res.status(429).json({
        error: 'Rate limit exceeded',
        retryAfter: 60
      });
      return;
    }
    
    this.requestCounts.set(key, requests + 1);
    setTimeout(() => {
      const current = this.requestCounts.get(key) || 0;
      this.requestCounts.set(key, Math.max(0, current - 1));
    }, 60000);
    
    next();
  }

  public start(port: number = 3000): void {
    this.app.listen(port, () => {
      console.log(`HiveRouter listening on port ${port}`);
      this.metrics.startCollection();
    });
  }
}

// Interface para dashboard de monitoramento
this.app.get('/dashboard', (req, res) => {
  res.sendFile(__dirname + '/public/dashboard.html');
});

this.app.get('/api/metrics', (req, res) => {
  res.json({
    hives: this.registry.getAllHives(),
    circuitBreakers: Array.from(this.circuitBreakers.entries()).map(([name, cb]) => ({
      name,
      state: cb.getState(),
      stats: cb.getStats()
    })),
    migration: this.migration.getStatus(),
    metrics: this.metrics.getSummary()
  });
});
```

## 5. Plano de Migração por Fases

```markdown
# Plano de Migração V12 - 6 Meses

## Fase 1: Fundação (Mês 1-2)
### Objetivo: Infraestrutura básica operacional
- [x] Setup HiveRouter com fallback 100% para legado
- [x] Implementar APM completo (Prometheus, Grafana, Jaeger)
- [x] Configurar CI/CD com deploy independente por hive
- [x] Criar hive-legacy como wrapper do sistema atual
- [ ] Testes de carga do gateway

## Fase 2: Primeira Hive (Mês 2-3)
### Objetivo: Migrar autenticação (baixo risco, alto valor)
- [ ] Criar hive-auth com:
  - [ ] Login/Logout V12
  - [ ] MFA
  - [ ] Session management
- [ ] Feature flag: 10% usuários → hive-auth
- [ ] Monitorar 7 dias: erros, performance, UX
- [ ] Aumentar para 50% se métricas OK
- [ ] Migrar 100% após 14 dias estáveis

## Fase 3: Hives Críticas (Mês 3-4)
### Objetivo: Pagamentos e transações
- [ ] hive-payments:
  - [ ] Processamento de cartão
  - [ ] Pix
  - [ ] Estornos
- [ ] hive-orders:
  - [ ] Criação de pedidos
  - [ ] Status tracking
- [ ] Sincronização bidirecional com legado
- [ ] Rollback automático por transação falha

## Fase 4: Domínios Restantes (Mês 4-5)
### Objetivo: Completar migração funcional
- [ ] hive-catalog: Produtos e categorias
- [ ] hive-users: Perfis e preferências
- [ ] hive-notifications: Email, SMS, WhatsApp
- [ ] Contract testing entre todas hives

## Fase 5: Otimização e Descomissionamento (Mês 5-6)
### Objetivo: Remover legado
- [ ] Desativar hive-legacy
- [ ] Otimizar comunicação entre hives
- [ ] Implementar cache distribuído
- [ ] Documentação final da arquitetura
- [ ] Post-mortem e lições aprendidas

## Métricas de Sucesso por Fase:
- Zero downtime não planejado
- Performance: P95 latency ≤ 200ms
- Erros: Error rate < 0.1%
- Cobertura de testes: ≥ 85%
- Rollback time: < 5 minutos por hive
```

// 2. PROVIDER DE DESIGN SYSTEM (CSS Variables)
// ============================================

// providers/DesignSystemProvider.tsx
import React, { createContext, useContext, useEffect } from 'react';
import { colors, spacing, typography, breakpoints, effects } from '../tokens';

interface DesignSystemContextType {
  colors: typeof colors;
  spacing: typeof spacing;
  typography: typeof typography;
  breakpoints: typeof breakpoints;
  effects: typeof effects;
}

const DesignSystemContext = createContext<DesignSystemContextType | null>(null);

export const useDesignSystem = () => {
  const context = useContext(DesignSystemContext);
  if (!context) {
    throw new Error('useDesignSystem must be used within DesignSystemProvider');
  }
  return context;
};

interface DesignSystemProviderProps {
  children: React.ReactNode;
}

export const DesignSystemProvider: React.FC<DesignSystemProviderProps> = ({ children }) => {
  // Injetar CSS Variables globalmente
  useEffect(() => {
    const style = document.createElement('style');
    style.textContent = `
      :root {
        /* Colors */
        ${Object.entries(colors.primary).map(([key, value]) => `--color-primary-${key}: ${value};`).join('\n        ')}
        ${Object.entries(colors.neutral).map(([key, value]) => `--color-neutral-${key}: ${value};`).join('\n        ')}
        ${Object.entries(colors.semantic.success).map(([key, value]) => `--color-semantic-success-${key}: ${value};`).join('\n        ')}
        ${Object.entries(colors.semantic.warning).map(([key, value]) => `--color-semantic-warning-${key}: ${value};`).join('\n        ')}
        ${Object.entries(colors.semantic.error).map(([key, value]) => `--color-semantic-error-${key}: ${value};`).join('\n        ')}
        ${Object.entries(colors.semantic.info).map(([key, value]) => `--color-semantic-info-${key}: ${value};`).join('\n        ')}
        
        /* Text Colors */
        --color-text-primary: ${colors.text.primary};
        --color-text-secondary: ${colors.text.secondary};
        --color-text-tertiary: ${colors.text.tertiary};
        --color-text-inverse: ${colors.text.inverse};
        --color-text-disabled: ${colors.text.disabled};
        
        /* Background Colors */
        --color-background-primary: ${colors.background.primary};
        --color-background-secondary: ${colors.background.secondary};
        --color-background-tertiary: ${colors.background.tertiary};
        --color-background-inverse: ${colors.background.inverse};
        
        /* Border Colors */
        --color-border-light: ${colors.border.light};
        --color-border-medium: ${colors.border.medium};
        --color-border-strong: ${colors.border.strong};
        --color-border-focus: ${colors.border.focus};
        --color-border-error: ${colors.border.error};
        
        /* Spacing */
        ${Object.entries(spacing).map(([key, value]) => `--spacing-${key}: ${value};`).join('\n        ')}
        
        /* Typography */
        --font-family-sans: ${typography.fontFamily.sans};
        --font-family-mono: ${typography.fontFamily.mono};
        ${Object.entries(typography.fontSize).map(([key, value]) => `--font-size-${key}: ${value};`).join('\n        ')}
        ${Object.entries(typography.fontWeight).map(([key, value]) => `--font-weight-${key}: ${value};`).join('\n        ')}
        ${Object.entries(typography.lineHeight).map(([key, value]) => `--line-height-${key}: ${value};`).join('\n        ')}
        
        /* Breakpoints */
        ${Object.entries(breakpoints).map(([key, value]) => `--breakpoint-${key}: ${value};`).join('\n        ')}
        
        /* Effects */
        ${Object.entries(effects.shadow).map(([key, value]) => `--shadow-${key}: ${value};`).join('\n        ')}
        ${Object.entries(effects.borderRadius).map(([key, value]) => `--border-radius-${key}: ${value};`).join('\n        ')}
        ${Object.entries(effects.transition).map(([key, value]) => `--transition-${key}: ${value};`).join('\n        ')}
      }
      
      /* Performance optimizations */
      * {
        box-sizing: border-box;
        min-width: 0;
      }
      
      html {
        font-family: var(--font-family-sans);
        -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased;
        -moz-osx-font-smoothing: grayscale;
        text-size-adjust: 100%;
      }
      
      body {
        margin: 0;
        background-color: var(--color-background-primary);
        color: var(--color-text-primary);
        font-size: var(--font-size-base);
        line-height: var(--line-height-normal);
      }
      
      /* Focus styles for accessibility */
      :focus-visible {
        outline: 2px solid var(--color-border-focus);
        outline-offset: 2px;
      }
    `;
    document.head.appendChild(style);
    
    return () => {
      document.head.removeChild(style);
    };
  }, []);

  const value = {
    colors,
    spacing,
    typography,
    breakpoints,
    effects,
  };

  return (
    <DesignSystemContext.Provider value={value}>
      {children}
    </DesignSystemContext.Provider>
  );
};

// 3. COMPONENTES BASE REFATORADOS (Performance Critical)
// ============================================

// components/Button/Button.tsx
import React, { forwardRef, useMemo } from 'react';

export type ButtonVariant = 'primary' | 'secondary' | 'outline' | 'ghost' | 'danger';
export type ButtonSize = 'xs' | 'sm' | 'md' | 'lg' | 'xl';

interface ButtonProps extends React.ButtonHTMLAttributes<HTMLButtonElement> {
  variant?: ButtonVariant;
  size?: ButtonSize;
  isLoading?: boolean;
  leftIcon?: React.ReactNode;
  rightIcon?: React.ReactNode;
  fullWidth?: boolean;
}

export const Button = forwardRef<HTMLButtonElement, ButtonProps>(({
  children,
  variant = 'primary',
  size = 'md',
  isLoading = false,
  leftIcon,
  rightIcon,
  fullWidth = false,
  disabled,
  className = '',
  onClick,
  ...props
}, ref) => {
  const baseClasses = useMemo(() => {
    return [
      'inline-flex items-center justify-center',
      'font-medium',
      'border',
      'transition-all',
      'focus-visible:outline-2 focus-visible:outline-offset-2',
      'disabled:opacity-50 disabled:cursor-not-allowed',
      fullWidth ? 'w-full' : '',
    ].join(' ');
  }, [fullWidth]);

  const variantClasses = useMemo(() => {
    const classes = {
      primary: [
        'bg-[var(--color-primary-500)]',
        'text-[var(--color-neutral-0)]',
        'border-transparent',
        'hover:bg-[var(--color-primary-600)]',
        'active:bg-[var(--color-primary-700)]',
        'focus-visible:outline-[var(--color-primary-500)]',
      ].join(' '),
      
      secondary: [
        'bg-[var(--color-neutral-100)]',
        'text-[var(--color-text-primary)]',
        'border-[var(--color-border-light)]',
        'hover:bg-[var(--color-neutral-200)]',
        'active:bg-[var(--color-neutral-300)]',
        'focus-visible:outline-[var(--color-primary-500)]',
      ].join(' '),
      
      outline: [
        'bg-transparent',
        'text-[var(--color-text-primary)]',
        'border-[var(--color-border-medium)]',
        'hover:bg-[var(--color-neutral-50)]',
        'active:bg-[var(--color-neutral-100)]',
        'focus-visible:outline-[var(--color-primary-500)]',
      ].join(' '),
      
      ghost: [
        'bg-transparent',
        'text-[var(--color-text-primary)]',
        'border-transparent',
        'hover:bg-[var(--color-neutral-100)]',
        'active:bg-[var(--color-neutral-200)]',
        'focus-visible:outline-[var(--color-primary-500)]',
      ].join(' '),
      
      danger: [
        'bg-[var(--color-semantic-error-500)]',
        'text-[var(--color-neutral-0)]',
        'border-transparent',
        'hover:bg-[var(--color-semantic-error-600)]',
        'active:bg-[var(--color-semantic-error-700)]',
        'focus-visible:outline-[var(--color-semantic-error-500)]',
      ].join(' '),
    };
    
    return classes[variant];
  }, [variant]);

  const sizeClasses = useMemo(() => {
    const classes = {
      xs: [
        'h-6',
        'px-2',
        'text-xs',
        'rounded-sm',
      ].join(' '),
      
      sm: [
        'h-8',
        'px-3',
        'text-sm',
        'rounded',
      ].join(' '),
      
      md: [
        'h-10',
        'px-4',
        'text-base',
        'rounded-md',
      ].join(' '),
      
      lg: [
        'h-12',
        'px-6',
        'text-lg',
        'rounded-lg',
      ].join(' '),
      
      xl: [
        'h-14',
        'px-8',
        'text-xl',
        'rounded-lg',
      ].join(' '),
    };
    
    return classes[size];
  }, [size]);

  const loadingClasses = useMemo(() => {
    return isLoading ? 'relative text-transparent' : '';
  }, [isLoading]);

  const handleClick = (e: React.MouseEvent<HTMLButtonElement>) => {
    if (!isLoading && !disabled && onClick) {
      onClick(e);
    }
  };

  return (
    <button
      ref={ref}
      disabled={disabled || isLoading}
      className={`${baseClasses} ${variantClasses} ${sizeClasses} ${loadingClasses} ${className}`}
      onClick={handleClick}
      aria-busy={isLoading}
      {...props}
    >


### [Sessão Paralela: Backend]
```python
# DIYAPP Evolution - V12 Core
# Dev Backend: Otimização de APIs, Resiliência e Métricas de UX

import asyncio
import json
import time
import gzip
from datetime import datetime, timedelta
from typing import Dict, List, Optional, Any
from dataclasses import dataclass, asdict
from functools import wraps
from contextlib import asynccontextmanager

# Dependencies
from fastapi import FastAPI, HTTPException, Request, Response, Depends, status
from fastapi.middleware.cors import CORSMiddleware
from fastapi.middleware.gzip import GZipMiddleware
from fastapi.responses import JSONResponse
from fastapi.security import HTTPBearer, HTTPAuthorizationCredentials
from pydantic import BaseModel, Field, validator
import redis.asyncio as redis
import aioredis
from prometheus_client import Counter, Histogram, Gauge, generate_latest
from circuitbreaker import circuit
import logging
from logging.handlers import RotatingFileHandler
import os

# ============================================================================
# 1. CONFIGURAÇÃO E OBSERVABILIDADE
# ============================================================================

# Logging estruturado JSON
class StructuredJSONFormatter(logging.Formatter):
    def format(self, record):
        log_data = {
            "timestamp": datetime.utcnow().isoformat(),
            "level": record.levelname,
            "correlation_id": getattr(record, 'correlation_id', 'N/A'),
            "user_id": getattr(record, 'user_id', 'N/A'),
            "endpoint": getattr(record, 'endpoint', 'N/A'),
            "message": record.getMessage(),
            "module": record.module,
            "function": record.funcName,
            "line": record.lineno
        }
        
        # Mascarar dados sensíveis
        if hasattr(record, 'sensitive_data'):
            log_data['sensitive_data'] = '***MASKED***'
            
        return json.dumps(log_data)

# Configurar logger
def setup_logger():
    logger = logging.getLogger("diyapp_backend")
    logger.setLevel(logging.INFO)
    
    # File handler com rotação
    file_handler = RotatingFileHandler(
        "logs/backend.log",
        maxBytes=10485760,  # 10MB
        backupCount=5
    )
    file_handler.setFormatter(StructuredJSONFormatter())
    logger.addHandler(file_handler)
    
    # Console handler para desenvolvimento
    console_handler = logging.StreamHandler()
    console_handler.setFormatter(StructuredJSONFormatter())
    logger.addHandler(console_handler)
    
    return logger

logger = setup_logger()

# Métricas Prometheus
REQUEST_COUNT = Counter(
    'http_requests_total',
    'Total HTTP Requests',
    ['method', 'endpoint', 'status']
)

REQUEST_LATENCY = Histogram(
    'http_request_duration_seconds',
    'HTTP request latency',
    ['method', 'endpoint'],
    buckets=[0.01, 0.05, 0.1, 0.3, 0.5, 1.0, 2.0, 5.0]
)

ACTIVE_REQUESTS = Gauge(
    'http_requests_active',
    'Active HTTP requests'
)

CIRCUIT_BREAKER_STATE = Gauge(
    'circuit_breaker_state',
    'Circuit breaker state (0=closed, 1=open, 2=half-open)',
    ['service']
)

CACHE_HITS = Counter(
    'cache_hits_total',
    'Total cache hits',
    ['cache_layer']
)

CACHE_MISSES = Counter(
    'cache_misses_total',
    'Total cache misses',
    ['cache_layer']
)

# ============================================================================
# 2. MODELOS DE DADOS E VALIDAÇÃO
# ============================================================================

class PaginationParams(BaseModel):
    """Parâmetros de paginação padronizados"""
    page: int = Field(default=1, ge=1, description="Número da página")
    limit: int = Field(default=20, ge=1, le=100, description="Itens por página")
    sort_by: Optional[str] = Field(default="created_at", description="Campo para ordenação")
    sort_order: str = Field(default="desc", regex="^(asc|desc)$")

class UserMetricsRequest(BaseModel):
    """Request para métricas de UX"""
    user_id: str = Field(..., min_length=1)
    start_date: datetime
    end_date: datetime
    
    @validator('end_date')
    def validate_date_range(cls, v, values):
        if 'start_date' in values and v < values['start_date']:
            raise ValueError('end_date must be after start_date')
        if (v - values['start_date']).days > 365:
            raise ValueError('Date range cannot exceed 1 year')
        return v

class HealthCheckResponse(BaseModel):
    """Response de health check"""
    status: str
    timestamp: datetime
    version: str = "v12"
    uptime: float
    dependencies: Dict[str, str]
    metrics: Dict[str, Any]

class UXMetricsResponse(BaseModel):
    """Response de métricas de UX"""
    user_id: str
    period: Dict[str, datetime]
    engagement: Dict[str, float]
    performance: Dict[str, float]
    retention: Dict[str, float]
    recommendations: List[str]

# ============================================================================
# 3. CACHE DISTRIBUÍDO COM REDIS
# ============================================================================

class CacheManager:
    """Gerenciador de cache distribuído com circuit breaker"""
    
    def __init__(self, redis_url: str = "redis://localhost:6379"):
        self.redis_url = redis_url
        self.redis_client = None
        self.circuit_state = "closed"
        
    async def connect(self):
        """Conectar ao Redis com retry e timeout"""
        try:
            self.redis_client = await redis.from_url(
                self.redis_url,
                encoding="utf-8",
                decode_responses=True,
                socket_timeout=2.0,
                socket_connect_timeout=2.0,
                retry_on_timeout=True,
                max_connections=10
            )
            await self.redis_client.ping()
            logger.info("Redis connected successfully")
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Redis connection failed: {e}")
            self.redis_client = None
            raise
    
    @circuit(failure_threshold=5, recovery_timeout=30)
    async def get(self, key: str) -> Optional[str]:
        """Obter valor do cache com circuit breaker"""
        if not self.redis_client:
            return None
            
        try:
            value = await self.redis_client.get(key)
            if value:
                CACHE_HITS.labels(cache_layer="redis").inc()
            else:
                CACHE_MISSES.labels(cache_layer="redis").inc()
            return value
        except Exception as e:
            logger.warning(f"Cache get failed: {e}")
            CIRCUIT_BREAKER_STATE.labels(service="redis").set(1)  # open
            raise
    
    @circuit(failure_threshold=5, recovery_timeout=30)
    async def set(self, key: str, value: str, ttl: int = 300):
        """Definir valor no cache com circuit breaker"""
        if not self.redis_client:
            return
            
        try:
            await self.redis_client.setex(key, ttl, value)
            CIRCUIT_BREAKER_STATE.labels(service="redis").set(0)  # closed
        except Exception as e:
            logger.warning(f"Cache set failed: {e}")
            CIRCUIT_BREAKER_STATE.labels(service="redis").set(1)  # open
            raise
    
    async def delete_pattern(self, pattern: str):
        """Deletar chaves por pattern"""
        if not self.redis_client:
            return
            
        try:
            keys = await self.redis_client.keys(pattern)
            if keys:
                await self.redis_client.delete(*keys)
        except Exception as e:
            logger.warning(f"Cache delete pattern failed: {e}")

# ============================================================================
# 4. MIDDLEWARES E DEPENDÊNCIAS
# ============================================================================

security = HTTPBearer()

async def get_current_user(credentials: HTTPAuthorizationCredentials = Depends(security)):
    """Validação de autenticação"""
    # Implementação real validaria token JWT
    # Esta é uma versão simplificada para exemplo
    token = credentials.credentials
    if not token.startswith("Bearer "):
        raise HTTPException(
            status_code=status.HTTP_401_UNAUTHORIZED,
            detail="Invalid authentication scheme"
        )
    
    # Em produção, validar token JWT
    user_id = token.replace("Bearer ", "").split(".")[0]
    return {"user_id": user_id, "token": token}

def log_request():
    """Decorator para logging estruturado"""
    def decorator(func):
        @wraps(func)
        async def wrapper(*args, **kwargs):
            request = kwargs.get('request')
            user = kwargs.get('current_user', {})
            
            correlation_id = request.headers.get('X-Correlation-ID', 'N/A')
            user_id = user.get('user_id', 'anonymous')
            endpoint = request.url.path
            
            # Adicionar contexto ao logger
            logger.info(
                f"Request started: {request.method} {endpoint}",
                extra={
                    'correlation_id': correlation_id,
                    'user_id': user_id,
                    'endpoint': endpoint
                }
            )
            
            start_time = time.time()
            ACTIVE_REQUESTS.inc()
            
            try:
                response = await func(*args, **kwargs)
                duration = time.time() - start_time
                
                # Registrar métricas
                REQUEST_LATENCY.labels(
                    method=request.method,
                    endpoint=endpoint
                ).observe(duration)
                
                REQUEST_COUNT.labels(
                    method=request.method,
                    endpoint=endpoint,
                    status=response.status_code
                ).inc()
                
                logger.info(
                    f"Request completed: {response.status_code} in {duration:.3f}s",
                    extra={
                        'correlation_id': correlation_id,
                        'user_id': user_id,
                        'endpoint': endpoint,
                        'duration_ms': duration * 1000,
                        'status': response.status_code
                    }
                )
                
                return response
                
            except HTTPException as e:
                duration = time.time() - start_time
                logger.warning(
                    f"Request failed with HTTP {e.status_code}: {e.detail}",
                    extra={
                        'correlation_id': correlation_id,
                        'user_id': user_id,
                        'endpoint': endpoint,
                        'duration_ms': duration * 1000,
                        'status': e.status_code
                    }
                )
                raise
                
            except Exception as e:
                duration = time.time() - start_time
                logger.error(
                    f"Request failed with exception: {str(e)}",
                    extra={
                        'correlation_id': correlation_id,
                        'user_id': user_id,
                        'endpoint': endpoint,
                        'duration_ms': duration * 1000,
                        'status': 500
                    },
                    exc_info=True
                )
                raise HTTPException(
                    status_code=500,
                    detail="Internal server error"
                )
                
            finally:
                ACTIVE_REQUESTS.dec()
                
        return wrapper
    return decorator

def cache_response(ttl: int = 300, key_prefix: str = "cache"):
    """Decorator para cache de response"""
    def decorator(func):
        @wraps(func)
        async def wrapper(*args, **kwargs):
            request = kwargs.get('request')
            cache_manager = kwargs.get('cache_manager')
            
            if not cache_manager or not request:
                return await func(*args, **kwargs)
            
            # Gerar chave de cache baseada nos parâmetros
            cache_key = f"{key_prefix}:{request.url.path}:{request.query_params}"
            
            # Tentar obter do cache
            cached = await cache_manager.get(cache_key)
            if cached:
                return JSONResponse(
                    content=json.loads(cached),
                    headers={"X-Cache": "HIT"}
                )
            
            # Executar função e cachear resultado
            response = await func(*args, **kwargs)
            
            if response.status_code == 200:
                response_body = response.body
                if isinstance(response_body, bytes):
                    response_body = response_body.decode('utf-8')
                
                await cache_manager.set(
                    cache_key,
                    response_body,
                    ttl=ttl
                )
            
            return response
            
        return wrapper
    return decorator

# ============================================================================
# 5. APLICAÇÃO FASTAPI
# ============================================================================

@dataclass
class AppState:
    """Estado da aplicação"""
    startup_time: datetime
    cache_manager: Optional[CacheManager] = None
    db_pool: Optional[Any] = None
    is_healthy: bool = True

app_state = AppState(startup_time=datetime.utcnow())

@asynccontextmanager
async def lifespan(app: FastAPI):
    """Gerenciador de ciclo de vida da aplicação"""
    # Startup
    app_state.cache_manager = CacheManager()
    try:
        await app_state.cache_manager.connect()
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"Failed to connect to cache: {e}")
        app_state.cache_manager = None
    
    yield
    
    # Shutdown
    if app_state.cache_manager and app_state.cache_manager.redis_client:
        await app_state.cache_manager.redis_client.close()

app = FastAPI(
    title="DIYAPP Evolution - V12 Core",
    description="APIs otimizadas com cache, resiliência e métricas de UX",
    version="12.0.0",
    lifespan=lifespan
)

# Middlewares
app.add_middleware(
    CORSMiddleware,
    allow_origins=["*"],  # Em produção, especificar domínios
    allow_credentials=True,
    allow_methods=["*"],
    allow_headers=["*"],
)

app.add_middleware(
    GZipMiddleware,
    minimum_size=1000,  # Comprimir apenas responses > 1KB
)

@app.get("/api/v12/health", response_model=HealthCheckResponse)
async def health_check(request: Request):
    """Health check completo com verificação de dependências"""
    dependencies = {
        "api": "healthy",
        "cache": "healthy" if app_state.cache_manager else "unhealthy",
        "database": "healthy",  # Em produção, testar conexão real
    }
    
    # Verificar cache
    if app_state.cache_manager:
        try:
            await app_state.cache_manager.get("health_check")
            dependencies["cache"] = "healthy"
        except Exception:
            dependencies["cache"] = "unhealthy"
    
    uptime = (datetime.utcnow() - app_state.startup_time).total_seconds()
    
    return HealthCheckResponse(
        status="healthy" if all(v == "healthy" for v in dependencies.values()) else "degraded",
        timestamp=datetime.utcnow(),
        uptime=uptime,
        dependencies=dependencies,
        metrics={
            "active_requests": ACTIVE_REQUESTS._value.get(),
            "cache_hits": CACHE_HITS._metrics[('cache_hits_total', ('redis',))]._value.get(),
            "cache_misses": CACHE_MISSES._metrics[('cache_misses_total', ('redis',))]._value.get()
        }
    )

@app.get("/api/v12/metrics")

    """Endpoint Prometheus para métricas"""
    return Response(
        content=generate_latest(),
        media_type="text/plain"
    )

@app.get("/api/v12/users/{user_id}/ux-metrics", response_model=UXMetricsResponse)
@log_request()
@cache_response(ttl=60, key_prefix="ux_metrics")  # Cache de 1 minuto
async def get_user_ux_metrics(
    user_id: str,
    start_date: datetime,
    end_date: datetime,
    request: Request,
    current_user: dict = Depends(get_current_user),
    cache_manager: CacheManager = Depends(lambda: app_state.cache_manager)
):
    """Obter métricas de UX para um usuário específico"""
    # Verificar autorização
    if current_user.get('user_id') != user_id:
        raise HTTPException(
            status_code=status.HTTP_403_FORBIDDEN,
            detail="Not authorized to access these metrics"
        )
    
    # Validar range de datas
    if end_date < start_date:
        raise HTTPException(
            status_code=status.HTTP_400_BAD_REQUEST,
            detail="end_date must be after start_date"
        )
    
    # Em produção, buscar dados reais do banco
    # Esta é uma implementação de exemplo
    
    # Simular processamento de métricas
    engagement = {
        "daily_active_minutes": 45.5,
        "feature_usage_rate": 0.78,
        "session_count": 12,
        "retention_score": 0.85
    }
    
    performance = {
        "avg_page_load_time": 1.2,
        "api_success_rate": 0.997,
        "error_rate": 0.003,
        "p95_response_time": 245
    }
    
    retention = {
        "day_1_retention": 0.65,
        "day_7_retention": 0.42,
        "day_30_retention": 0.28,
        "churn_risk": 0.15
    }
    
    recommendations = [
        "Consider reducing initial onboarding steps",
        "Feature X has low engagement - consider improvements",
        "Users from segment Y show higher retention"
    ]
    
    return UXMetricsResponse(
        user_id=user_id,
        period={"start": start_date, "end": end_date},
        engagement=engagement,
        performance=performance,
        retention=retention,
        recommendations=recommendations
    )

export const colors = {

    success: {
      light: '#d1fae5',
      base: '#10b981',
      dark: '#065f46'
    },
    warning: {
      light: '#fef3c7',
      base: '#f59e0b',
      dark: '#92400e'
    },
    error: {
      light: '#fee2e2',
      base: '#ef4444',
      dark: '#991b1b'
    },
    info: {
      light: '#dbeafe',
      base: '#3b82f6',
      dark: '#1e40af'
    }
  },
  
  // Background Colors
  background: {
    primary: '#ffffff',
    secondary: '#f8fafc',
    tertiary: '#f1f5f9',
    inverse: '#0f172a'
  },
  
  // Text Colors (WCAG AA compliant)
  text: {
    primary: '#0f172a',
    secondary: '#475569',
    tertiary: '#64748b',
    inverse: '#ffffff',
    disabled: '#94a3b8'
  },
  
  // Border Colors
  border: {
    light: '#e2e8f0',
    base: '#cbd5e1',
    dark: '#94a3b8',
    focus: '#0ea5e9'
  }
};

// Função para verificar contraste WCAG AA
export function getContrastColor(backgroundColor) {
  const luminance = (r, g, b) => {
    const [rs, gs, bs] = [r, g, b].map(c => {
      c = c / 255;
      return c <= 0.03928 ? c / 12.92 : Math.pow((c + 0.055) / 1.055, 2.4);
    });
    return 0.2126 * rs + 0.7152 * gs + 0.0722 * bs;
  };
  
  const hexToRgb = (hex) => {
    const result = /^#?([a-f\d]{2})([a-f\d]{2})([a-f\d]{2})$/i.exec(hex);
    return result ? {
      r: parseInt(result[1], 16),
      g: parseInt(result[2], 16),
      b: parseInt(result[3], 16)
    } : null;
  };
  
  const bgRgb = hexToRgb(backgroundColor);
  if (!bgRgb) return colors.text.primary;
  
  const bgLuminance = luminance(bgRgb.r, bgRgb.g, bgRgb.b);
  return bgLuminance > 0.179 ? colors.text.primary : colors.text.inverse;
}
```

### `src/design-tokens/tokens.js`
```javascript
import { colors } from './colors.js';
import { typography } from './typography.js';
import { spacing, borderRadius } from './spacing.js';
import { elevation } from './elevation.js';

export const designTokens = {
  colors,
  typography,
  spacing,
  borderRadius,
  elevation,
  
  // Breakpoints responsivos
  breakpoints: {
    xs: '320px',
    sm: '640px',
    md: '768px',
    lg: '1024px',
    xl: '1280px',
    '2xl': '1536px'
  },
  
  // Transições e animações
  transition: {
    duration: {
      fastest: '75ms',
      faster: '100ms',
      fast: '150ms',
      normal: '200ms',
      slow: '300ms',
      slower: '500ms',
      slowest: '700ms'
    },
    easing: {
      linear: 'linear',
      ease: 'ease',
      easeIn: 'cubic-bezier(0.4, 0, 1, 1)',
      easeOut: 'cubic-bezier(0, 0, 0.2, 1)',
      easeInOut: 'cubic-bezier(0.4, 0, 0.2, 1)',
      spring: 'cubic-bezier(0.175, 0.885, 0.32, 1.275)'
    }
  }
};

// Export para uso global
export default designTokens;
```

## 2. Componentes Premium com Micro-interações

### `src/components/Button/Button.js`
```javascript
import { designTokens } from '../../design-tokens/tokens.js';

export class Button extends HTMLElement {
  constructor() {
    super();
    this.attachShadow({ mode: 'open' });
    this._variant = this.getAttribute('variant') || 'primary';
    this._size = this.getAttribute('size') || 'medium';
    this._state = this.getAttribute('state') || 'default';
    this._loading = this.hasAttribute('loading');
  }

  static get observedAttributes() {
    return ['variant', 'size', 'state', 'loading', 'disabled'];
  }

  connectedCallback() {
    this.render();
    this.setupEventListeners();
  }

  attributeChangedCallback(name, oldValue, newValue) {
    if (oldValue !== newValue) {
      this[`_${name}`] = newValue;
      this.render();
    }
  }

  get variant() { return this._variant; }
  set variant(value) {
    this.setAttribute('variant', value);
  }

  get size() { return this._size; }
  set size(value) {
    this.setAttribute('size', value);
  }

  get state() { return this._state; }
  set state(value) {
    this.setAttribute('state', value);
  }

  get loading() { return this._loading; }
  set loading(value) {
    if (value) {
      this.setAttribute('loading', '');
    } else {
      this.removeAttribute('loading');
    }
  }

  get disabled() { return this.hasAttribute('disabled'); }
  set disabled(value) {
    if (value) {
      this.setAttribute('disabled', '');
    } else {
      this.removeAttribute('disabled');
    }
  }

  setupEventListeners() {
    this.shadowRoot.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
      if (this.disabled || this.loading) {
        e.preventDefault();
        e.stopPropagation();
        return;
      }
      
      // Ripple effect
      this.createRipple(e);
    });

    // Keyboard navigation
    this.shadowRoot.addEventListener('keydown', (e) => {
      if (e.key === 'Enter' || e.key === ' ') {
        e.preventDefault();
        if (!this.disabled && !this.loading) {
          this.click();
        }
      }
    });
  }

  createRipple(event) {
    const button = this.shadowRoot.querySelector('.button');
    const circle = document.createElement('span');
    const diameter = Math.max(button.clientWidth, button.clientHeight);
    const radius = diameter / 2;

    circle.style.width = circle.style.height = `${diameter}px`;
    circle.style.left = `${event.clientX - button.getBoundingClientRect().left - radius}px`;
    circle.style.top = `${event.clientY - button.getBoundingClientRect().top - radius}px`;
    circle.classList.add('ripple');

    const ripple = button.querySelector('.ripple');
    if (ripple) {
      ripple.remove();
    }

    button.appendChild(circle);
  }

  getStyles() {
    const tokens = designTokens;
    return `
      <style>
        :host {
          display: inline-block;
          --button-primary: ${tokens.colors.primary[600]};
          --button-primary-hover: ${tokens.colors.primary[700]};
          --button-primary-active: ${tokens.colors.primary[800]};
          --button-secondary: ${tokens.colors.neutral[100]};
          --button-secondary-hover: ${tokens.colors.neutral[200]};
          --button-secondary-active: ${tokens.colors.neutral[300]};
          --button-ghost: transparent;
          --button-ghost-hover: ${tokens.colors.neutral[100]};
          --button-ghost-active: ${tokens.colors.neutral[200]};
          --button-danger: ${tokens.colors.semantic.error.base};
          --button-danger-hover: ${tokens.colors.semantic.error.dark};
          --button-danger-active: #7f1d1d;
        }

        .button {
          position: relative;
          display: inline-flex;
          align-items: center;
          justify-content: center;
          gap: ${tokens.spacing[2]};
          font-family: ${tokens.typography.fontFamily.sans};
          font-weight: ${tokens.typography.fontWeight.medium};
          line-height: ${tokens.typography.lineHeight.normal};
          border-radius: ${tokens.borderRadius.base};
          border: 1px solid transparent;
          cursor: pointer;
          transition: all ${tokens.transition.duration.normal} ${tokens.transition.easing.easeOut};
          overflow: hidden;
          user-select: none;
          outline: none;
        }

        /* Variants */
        .button--primary {
          background-color: var(--button-primary);
          color: white;
        }

        .button--secondary {
          background-color: var(--button-secondary);
          color: ${tokens.colors.text.primary};
          border-color: ${tokens.colors.border.base};
        }

        .button--ghost {
          background-color: var(--button-ghost);
          color: ${tokens.colors.text.

### [Sessão Paralela: Tech Leader]

## 2. ADR-001: Estratégia de Refatoração - Modo Hive

**Data:** 2024-01-15
**Status:** Aceita
**Autores:** Tech Lead

**CONTEXTO:**
O sistema atual (DIYAPP V11) possui débito técnico significativo, mas precisa manter 100% de disponibilidade durante a migração. A estratégia tradicional de "big bang rewrite" é muito arriscada.

**DECISÃO:**
Implementar refatoração incremental usando "Modo Hive" - refatoração paralela onde:
1. O sistema legado continua funcionando
2. Novos módulos são desenvolvidos em paralelo
3. Um "Adapter Layer" faz a ponte entre sistemas
4. Feature flags controlam o tráfego gradual

**OPÇÕES CONSIDERADAS:**
- **Opção A: Big Bang Rewrite** - Prós: Arquitetura limpa desde o início. Contras: Risco extremo, downtime prolongado.
- **Opção B: Refatoração Incremental** - Prós: Baixo risco, feedback contínuo. Contras: Complexidade temporária, custo de manutenção dupla.
- **Opção C: Modo Hive (escolhida)** - Prós: Paralelismo máximo, risco controlado, permite A/B testing. Contras: Requer disciplina de equipe, overhead de sincronização.

**CONSEQUÊNCIAS:**
**Positivas:**
- Zero downtime durante migração
- Rollback instantâneo em caso de problemas
- Capacidade de testar novas features em produção gradualmente
- Equipe pode trabalhar em paralelo no legado e no novo

**Negativas:**
- Custo de manutenção dupla durante transição
- Complexidade aumentada temporariamente
- Necessidade de disciplina rigorosa em versionamento

**Riscos:**
- Inconsistência de dados entre sistemas
- Mitigação: Sincronização bidirecional com resolução de conflitos
- Overhead de performance no adapter layer
- Mitigação: Cache estratégico e otimizações

**REVISÃO:** 2024-04-15

## 3. Engineering Standards

```javascript
// docs/engineering-standards.md

# DIYAPP V12 Engineering Standards

## 1. Código
- **Linguagem:** TypeScript 5.0+
- **Style Guide:** Airbnb com modificações
- **Linter:** ESLint com regras customizadas
- **Formatter:** Prettier com configuração padronizada
- **Complexidade Ciclomática:** Máximo 15 por função
- **Tamanho de Função:** Máximo 50 linhas

## 2. Commits
- **Conventional Commits:** `feat:`, `fix:`, `chore:`, `refactor:`, `test:`, `docs:`
- **Scope obrigatório:** `feat(agent): add new validation logic`
- **Body descritivo:** Explicar o "porquê", não apenas o "o que"

## 3. Testes
- **Cobertura mínima:** 80% (90% para core modules)
- **Framework:** Jest + Supertest
- **E2E:** Playwright
- **Test Data Factory:** Faker.js com seeds reproduzíveis

## 4. Segurança
- **Dependências:** Scan semanal com Snyk/Dependabot
- **Secrets:** Nunca em código, usar HashiCorp Vault
- **Input Validation:** Zod schemas para todas as entradas
- **Output Encoding:** Auto-escaping em templates

## 5. Performance
- **Query N+1:** Zero tolerância
- **Response Time:** P95 < 200ms para APIs
- **Memory Leaks:** Testes de carga com autocannon
- **Bundle Size:** Monitoramento contínuo

## 6. Documentação
- **APIs:** OpenAPI 3.0 com exemplos
- **Decisões:** ADRs para tudo que afeta arquitetura
- **Onboarding:** README com setup em 5 minutos
```

## 5. Core Monitoring Module

```typescript
// src/core/monitoring/apm/APMController.ts

import { NodeSDK } from '@opentelemetry/sdk-node';
import { getNodeAutoInstrumentations } from '@opentelemetry/auto-instrumentations-node';
import { OTLPTraceExporter } from '@opentelemetry/exporter-trace-otlp-http';
import { OTLPMetricExporter } from '@opentelemetry/exporter-metrics-otlp-http';
import { PeriodicExportingMetricReader } from '@opentelemetry/sdk-metrics';
import { Resource } from '@opentelemetry/resources';
import { SemanticResourceAttributes } from '@opentelemetry/semantic-conventions';
import { WinstonInstrumentation } from '@opentelemetry/instrumentation-winston';
import { HttpInstrumentation } from '@opentelemetry/instrumentation-http';
import { ExpressInstrumentation } from '@opentelemetry/instrumentation-express';
import { RedisInstrumentation } from '@opentelemetry/instrumentation-redis';
import { PrismaInstrumentation } from '@prisma/instrumentation';

export class APMController {
  private sdk: NodeSDK;
  private static instance: APMController;

  private constructor() {
    const resource = new Resource({
      [SemanticResourceAttributes.SERVICE_NAME]: 'diyapp-v12',
      [SemanticResourceAttributes.SERVICE_VERSION]: '12.0.0',
      [SemanticResourceAttributes.DEPLOYMENT_ENVIRONMENT]: process.env.NODE_ENV || 'development',
    });

    this.sdk = new NodeSDK({
      resource,
      traceExporter: new OTLPTraceExporter({
        url: process.env.OTLP_ENDPOINT || 'http://localhost:4318/v1/traces',
      }),
      metricReader: new PeriodicExportingMetricReader({
        exporter: new OTLPMetricExporter({
          url: process.env.OTLP_METRICS_ENDPOINT || 'http://localhost:4318/v1/metrics',
        }),
        exportIntervalMillis: 60000, // 1 minute
      }),
      instrumentations: [
        getNodeAutoInstrumentations({
          '@opentelemetry/instrumentation-fs': { enabled: false },
        }),
        new HttpInstrumentation(),
        new ExpressInstrumentation(),
        new RedisInstrumentation(),
        new WinstonInstrumentation(),
        new PrismaInstrumentation(),
      ],
    });
  }

  public static getInstance(): APMController {
    if (!APMController.instance) {
      APMController.instance = new APMController();
    }
    return APMController.instance;
  }

  public async start(): Promise<void> {
    try {
      await this.sdk.start();
      console.log('APM monitoring started successfully');
      
      // Register shutdown handler
      process.on('SIGTERM', async () => {
        await this.shutdown();
        process.exit(0);
      });
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Failed to start APM:', error);
      // Don't crash the app if monitoring fails
    }
  }

  public async shutdown(): Promise<void> {
    try {
      await this.sdk.shutdown();
      console.log('APM monitoring stopped');
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Error shutting down APM:', error);
    }
  }

  // Custom business metrics
  public recordAgentExecution(agentId: string, duration: number, success: boolean): void {
    const meter = this.sdk.meterProvider.getMeter('diyapp-business');
    
    const executionCounter = meter.createCounter('agent_executions_total', {
      description: 'Total agent executions',
    });
    
    const durationHistogram = meter.createHistogram('agent_execution_duration_ms', {
      description: 'Agent execution duration in milliseconds',
      unit: 'ms',
    });

    executionCounter.add(1, {
      agent_id: agentId,
      success: success.toString(),
      environment: process.env.NODE_ENV || 'development',
    });

    durationHistogram.record(duration, {
      agent_id: agentId,
    });
  }

  public recordHiveModeOperation(module: string, operation: string, duration: number): void {
    const meter = this.sdk.meterProvider.getMeter('diyapp-hive');
    
    const hiveCounter = meter.createCounter('hive_operations_total', {
      description: 'Total Hive mode operations',
    });
    
    hiveCounter.add(1, {
      module,
      operation,
      environment: process.env.NODE_ENV || 'development',
    });
  }
}
```

## 6. Hive Mode Implementation

```typescript
// src/modules/hive-mode/HiveModeOrchestrator.ts

import { EventEmitter } from 'events';
import { APMController } from '../../core/monitoring/apm/APMController';

export interface HiveModule {
  id: string;
  name: string;
  version: string;
  status: 'active' | 'standby' | 'migrating' | 'failed';
  trafficPercentage: number; // 0-100
  healthCheck: () => Promise<boolean>;
  execute: (input: any) => Promise<any>;
  rollback?: () => Promise<void>;
}

export class HiveModeOrchestrator extends EventEmitter {
  private modules: Map<string, HiveModule> = new Map();
  private apm: APMController;
  private trafficRouter: TrafficRouter;

  constructor() {
    super();
    this.apm = APMController.getInstance();
    this.trafficRouter = new TrafficRouter();
  }

  public registerModule(module: HiveModule): void {
    this.modules.set(module.id, module);
    this.trafficRouter.addRoute(module.id, module.trafficPercentage);
    
    console.log(`Hive module registered: ${module.name} v${module.version}`);
    this.emit('module-registered', module);
  }

  public async migrateTraffic(
    fromModuleId: string,
    toModuleId: string,
    percentage: number
  ): Promise<void> {
    const startTime = Date.now();
    
    try {
      // Validate modules exist
      const fromModule = this.modules.get(fromModuleId);
      const toModule = this.modules.get(toModuleId);
      
      if (!fromModule || !toModule) {
        throw new Error(`Module not found: ${!fromModule ? fromModuleId : toModuleId}`);
      }

      // Update traffic distribution
      this.trafficRouter.updateDistribution(fromModuleId, toModuleId, percentage);
      
      // Update module status
      fromModule.status = percentage === 100 ? 'standby' : 'active';
      toModule.status = percentage === 0 ? 'standby' : 'active';
      
      if (percentage > 0 && percentage < 100) {
        fromModule.status = 'migrating';
        toModule.status = 'migrating';
      }

      console.log(`Traffic migration: ${fromModuleId} -> ${toModuleId} (${percentage}%)`);
      
      this.apm.recordHiveModeOperation(
        'orchestrator',
        'migrate-traffic',
        Date.now() - startTime
      );
      
      this.emit('traffic-migrated', { fromModuleId, toModuleId, percentage });
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Traffic migration failed:', error);
      this.emit('migration-failed', { error, fromModuleId, toModuleId });
      throw error;
    }
  }

  public async execute(moduleType: string, input: any): Promise<any> {
    const startTime = Date.now();
    
    try {
      // Route to appropriate module based on traffic distribution
      const moduleId = this.trafficRouter.route(moduleType);
      const module = this.modules.get(moduleId);
      
      if (!module) {
        throw new Error(`No active module found for type: ${moduleType}`);
      }

      // Health check before execution
      const isHealthy = await module.healthCheck();
      if (!isHealthy) {
        // Fallback to legacy module if available
        const fallbackId = this.findFallbackModule(moduleType, moduleId);
        if (fallbackId) {
          console.warn(`Module ${moduleId} unhealthy, falling back to ${fallbackId}`);
          return this.executeWithFallback(fallbackId, input);
        }
        throw new Error(`Module ${moduleId} is unhealthy and no fallback available`);
      }

      // Execute the module
      const result = await module.execute(input);
      
      this.apm.recordHiveModeOperation(
        moduleType,
        'execute',
        Date.now() - startTime
      );
      
      return result;
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Hive execution failed:', error);
      this.emit('execution-failed', { moduleType, input, error });
      throw error;
    }
  }

  private findFallbackModule(moduleType: string, currentModuleId: string): string | null {
    // Find legacy version of the same module type
    for (const [id, module] of this.modules) {
      if (id !== currentModuleId && 
          module.name === moduleType && 
          module.status === 'active') {
        return id;
      }
    }
    return null;
  }

  private async executeWithFallback(fallbackId: string, input: any): Promise<any> {
    const fallbackModule = this.modules.get(fallbackId);
    if (!fallbackModule) {
      throw new Error(`Fallback module ${fallbackId} not found`);
    }
    
    return fallbackModule.execute(input);
  }

  public getModuleHealth(): Array<{
    id: string;
    name: string;
    status: string;
    trafficPercentage: number;
    lastHealthCheck: Date;
  }> {
    return Array.from(this.modules.values()).map(module => ({
      id: module.id,
      name: module.name,
      status: module.status,
      trafficPercentage: this.trafficRouter.getPercentage(module.id),
      lastHealthCheck: new Date(),
    }));
  }
}

class TrafficRouter {
  private distributions: Map<string, Map<string, number>> = new Map();
  private moduleRoutes: Map<string, string[]> = new Map();

  public addRoute(moduleId: string, percentage: number): void {
    const moduleType

### [Sessão Paralela: Frontend]
```typescript

// Data: 2024-01-15

// ============================================
// 1. TOKENS DO DESIGN SYSTEM

    radius: {
      none: '0',
      sm: '0.125rem',   // 2px
      md: '0.375rem',   // 6px
      lg: '0.5rem',     // 8px
      xl: '0.75rem',    // 12px
      '2xl': '1rem',    // 16px
      full: '9999px',
    },
    
    width: {
      thin: '1px',
      medium: '2px',
      thick: '4px',
    },
  },
  
  // Sombras
  shadows: {
    sm: '0 1px 2px 0 rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.05)',
    md: '0 4px 6px -1px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.1), 0 2px 4px -1px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.06)',
    lg: '0 10px 15px -3px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.1), 0 4px 6px -2px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.05)',
    xl: '0 20px 25px -5px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.1), 0 10px 10px -5px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04)',
  },
  
  // Breakpoints
  breakpoints: {
    sm: '640px',
    md: '768px',
    lg: '1024px',
    xl: '1280px',
    '2xl': '1536px',
  },
  
  // Z-index
  zIndex: {
    hide: -1,
    base: 0,
    docked: 10,
    dropdown: 1000,
    sticky: 1100,
    banner: 1200,
    overlay: 1300,
    modal: 1400,
    popover: 1500,
    skipLink: 1600,
    toast: 1700,
    tooltip: 1800,
  },
} as const;

                        keyof typeof tokens.colors.neutral | 
                        keyof typeof tokens.colors.semantic;

// src/design-system/DesignSystemProvider.tsx
import React, { createContext, useContext, ReactNode } from 'react';
import { Global, css, ThemeProvider } from '@emotion/react';
import { tokens } from './tokens';

// Tema baseado nos tokens
const theme = {
  ...tokens,
  mode: 'light' as const,
};

type Theme = typeof theme;

const DesignSystemContext = createContext<Theme | null>(null);

export const useDesignSystem = () => {
  const context = useContext(DesignSystemContext);
  if (!context) {
    throw new Error('useDesignSystem must be used within DesignSystemProvider');
  }
  return context;
};

interface DesignSystemProviderProps {
  children: ReactNode;
  mode?: 'light' | 'dark';
}

export const DesignSystemProvider: React.FC<DesignSystemProviderProps> = ({
  children,
  mode = 'light',
}) => {
  const currentTheme = {
    ...theme,
    mode,
    colors: {
      ...theme.colors,
      background: {
        ...theme.colors.background,
        default: mode === 'light' 
          ? theme.colors.background.light 
          : theme.colors.background.dark,
        card: mode === 'light'
          ? theme.colors.background.card
          : theme.colors.background.cardDark,
      },
    },
  };

  // Estilos globais usando tokens
  const globalStyles = css`
    :root {
      --color-primary-500: ${tokens.colors.primary[500]};
      --color-neutral-100: ${tokens.colors.neutral[100]};
      --spacing-4: ${tokens.spacing[4]};
      --font-size-base: ${tokens.typography.fontSize.base};
    }

    * {
      box-sizing: border-box;
      margin: 0;
      padding: 0;
    }

    html {
      font-family: ${tokens.typography.fontFamily.sans};
      font-size: 16px;
      line-height: ${tokens.typography.lineHeight.normal};
      -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased;
      -moz-osx-font-smoothing: grayscale;
    }

    body {
      background-color: ${currentTheme.colors.background.default};
      color: ${tokens.colors.neutral[900]};
      transition: background-color 0.2s ease;
    }

    @media (prefers-reduced-motion: reduce) {
      * {
        animation-duration: 0.01ms !important;
        animation-iteration-count: 1 !important;
        transition-duration: 0.01ms !important;
      }
    }

    /* Focus styles para acessibilidade */
    :focus-visible {
      outline: 2px solid ${tokens.colors.primary[500]};
      outline-offset: 2px;
    }

    /* Scrollbar styling */
    ::-webkit-scrollbar {
      width: 8px;
      height: 8px;
    }

    ::-webkit-scrollbar-track {
      background: ${tokens.colors.neutral[100]};
    }

    ::-webkit-scrollbar-thumb {
      background: ${tokens.colors.neutral[400]};
      border-radius: ${tokens.borders.radius.full};
    }

    ::-webkit-scrollbar-thumb:hover {
      background: ${tokens.colors.neutral[500]};
    }
  `;

  return (
    <DesignSystemContext.Provider value={currentTheme}>
      <ThemeProvider theme={currentTheme}>
        <Global styles={globalStyles} />
        {children}
      </ThemeProvider>
    </DesignSystemContext.Provider>
  );
};

// src/components/Button/Button.tsx
import React, { forwardRef, ButtonHTMLAttributes } from 'react';
import styled from '@emotion/styled';
import { useDesignSystem } from '../../design-system/DesignSystemProvider';

export type ButtonVariant = 'primary' | 'secondary' | 'outline' | 'ghost';
export type ButtonSize = 'sm' | 'md' | 'lg';

interface ButtonProps extends ButtonHTMLAttributes<HTMLButtonElement> {
  variant?: ButtonVariant;
  size?: ButtonSize;
  isLoading?: boolean;
  leftIcon?: React.ReactNode;
  rightIcon?: React.ReactNode;
  fullWidth?: boolean;
}

const StyledButton = styled.button<{
  variant: ButtonVariant;
  size: ButtonSize;
  isLoading: boolean;
  fullWidth: boolean;
}>(({ variant, size, isLoading, fullWidth, theme }) => {
  const baseStyles = {
    display: 'inline-flex',
    alignItems: 'center',
    justifyContent: 'center',
    gap: theme.spacing[2],
    fontFamily: theme.typography.fontFamily.sans,
    fontWeight: theme.typography.fontWeight.medium,
    border: 'none',
    borderRadius: theme.borders.radius.md,
    cursor: 'pointer',
    transition: 'all 0.2s ease',
    width: fullWidth ? '100%' : 'auto',
    position: 'relative',
    '&:disabled': {
      cursor: 'not-allowed',
      opacity: 0.5,
    },
    '&:focus-visible': {
      outline: `2px solid ${theme.colors.primary[500]}`,
      outlineOffset: '2px',
    },
  };

  const sizeStyles = {
    sm: {
      padding: `${theme.spacing[1]} ${theme.spacing[3]}`,
      fontSize: theme.typography.fontSize.sm,
      height: '32px',
    },
    md: {
      padding: `${theme.spacing[2]} ${theme.spacing[4]}`,
      fontSize: theme.typography.fontSize.base,
      height: '40px',
    },
    lg: {
      padding: `${theme.spacing[3]} ${theme.spacing[5]}`,
      fontSize: theme.typography.fontSize.lg,
      height: '48px',
    },
  };

  const variantStyles = {
    primary: {
      backgroundColor: theme.colors.primary[600],
      color: 'white',
      '&:hover:not(:disabled)': {
        backgroundColor: theme.colors.primary[700],
      },
      '&:active:not(:disabled)': {
        backgroundColor: theme.colors.primary[800],
      },
    },
    secondary: {
      backgroundColor: theme.colors.neutral[200],
      color: theme.colors.neutral[900],
      '&:hover:not(:disabled)': {
        backgroundColor: theme.colors.neutral[300],
      },
      '&:active:not(:disabled)': {
        backgroundColor: theme.colors.neutral[400],
      },
    },
    outline: {
      backgroundColor: 'transparent',
      color: theme.colors.primary[600],
      border: `1px solid ${theme.colors.primary[600]}`,
      '&:hover:not(:disabled)': {
        backgroundColor: theme.colors.primary[50],
      },
      '&:active:not(:disabled)': {
        backgroundColor: theme.colors.primary[100],
      },
    },
    ghost: {
      backgroundColor: 'transparent',
      color: theme.colors.neutral[700],
      '&:hover:not(:disabled)': {
        backgroundColor: theme.colors.neutral[100],
      },
      '&:active:not(:disabled)': {
        backgroundColor: theme.colors.neutral[200],
      },
    },
  };

  const loadingStyles = isLoading ? {
    color: 'transparent !important',
    '&::after': {
      content: '""',
      position: 'absolute',
      width: '16px',
      height: '16px',
      border: `2px solid ${variant === 'primary' ? 'white' : theme.colors.primary[600]}`,
      borderTopColor: 'transparent',
      borderRadius: '50%',
      animation: 'spin 1s linear infinite',
    },
  } : {};

  return {
    ...baseStyles,
    ...sizeStyles[size],
    ...variantStyles[variant],
    ...loadingStyles,
    '@keyframes spin': {
      '0%': { transform: 'rotate(0deg)' },
      '100%': { transform: 'rotate(360deg)' },
    },
  };
});

export const Button = forwardRef<HTMLButtonElement, ButtonProps>(
  (
    {
      children,
      variant = 'primary',
      size = 'md',
      isLoading = false,
      leftIcon,
      rightIcon,
      fullWidth = false,
      disabled,
      ...props
    },
    ref
  ) => {
    const theme = useDesignSystem();
    
    return (
      <StyledButton
        ref={ref}
        variant={variant}
        size={size}
        isLoading={isLoading}
        fullWidth={fullWidth}
        disabled={disabled || isLoading}
        aria-busy={isLoading}
        {...props}
      >
        {!isLoading && leftIcon && <span aria-hidden="true">{leftIcon}</span>}
        <span>{children}</span>
        {!isLoading && rightIcon && <span aria-hidden="true">{rightIcon}</span>}
      </StyledButton>
    );
  }
);

Button.displayName = 'Button';

// src/components/VirtualList/VirtualList.tsx
import React, { useRef, useCallback, useEffect, useState } from 'react';
import styled from '@emotion/styled';
import { useDesignSystem } from '../../design-system/DesignSystemProvider';

interface VirtualListProps<T> {
  items: T[];
  itemHeight: number;
  renderItem: (item: T, index: number) => React.ReactNode;
  overscan?: number;
  className?: string;
  onEndReached?: () => void;
  endReachedThreshold?: number;
}

const Container = styled.div<{ height: number }>`
  height: ${({ height }) => height}px;
  overflow-y: auto;
  position: relative;
  -webkit-overflow-scrolling: touch;
`;

const InnerContainer = styled.div<{ height: number }>`
  height: ${({ height }) => height}px;
  position: relative;
`;

const ItemContainer = styled.div<{ top: number }>`
  position: absolute;
  top: ${({ top }) => top}px;
  width: 100%;
`;

export function VirtualList<T>({
  items,
  itemHeight,
  renderItem,
  overscan = 3,
  className,
  onEndReached,
  endReachedThreshold = 100,
}: VirtualListProps<T>) {
  const containerRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null);
  const [scrollTop, setScrollTop] = useState(0);
  const [containerHeight, setContainerHeight] = useState(0);
  const theme = useDesignSystem();

  // Calcular itens visíveis
  const totalHeight = items.length * itemHeight;
  const startIndex = Math.max(0, Math.floor(scrollTop / itemHeight) - overscan);
  const endIndex = Math.min(
    items.length - 1,
    Math.floor((scrollTop + containerHeight) / itemHeight) + overscan
  );

  const visibleItems = items.slice(startIndex, endIndex + 1);

  // Observer para detectar fim da lista
  useEffect(() => {
    const container = containerRef.current;
    if (!container || !onEndReached) return;

    const observer = new IntersectionObserver(
      (entries) => {
        if (entries[0].isIntersecting) {
          onEndReached();
        }
      },
      {
        root: container,
        rootMargin: `0px 0px ${endReachedThreshold}px 

### [Sessão Paralela: Backend]
```python
