# src/core/config.py
from pydantic_settings import BaseSettings
from typing import Optional
import os

class Settings(BaseSettings):
    # API
    API_V1_STR: str = "/api/v1"
    API_V2_STR: str = "/api/v2"
    PROJECT_NAME: str = "DIYAPP Evolution V12"
    
    # Database
    POSTGRES_SERVER: str = os.getenv("POSTGRES_SERVER", "localhost")
    POSTGRES_USER: str = os.getenv("POSTGRES_USER", "postgres")
    POSTGRES_PASSWORD: str = os.getenv("POSTGRES_PASSWORD", "")
    POSTGRES_DB: str = os.getenv("POSTGRES_DB", "diyapp")
    DATABASE_URL: Optional[str] = None
    
    # Redis
    REDIS_HOST: str = os.getenv("REDIS_HOST", "localhost")
    REDIS_PORT: int = int(os.getenv("REDIS_PORT", 6379))
    REDIS_PASSWORD: Optional[str] = os.getenv("REDIS_PASSWORD")
    REDIS_DB: int = int(os.getenv("REDIS_DB", 0))
    REDIS_CACHE_TTL: int = int(os.getenv("REDIS_CACHE_TTL", 300))  # 5 minutes
    
    # Security
    SECRET_KEY: str = os.getenv("SECRET_KEY", "your-secret-key-change-in-production")
    ALGORITHM: str = "HS256"
    ACCESS_TOKEN_EXPIRE_MINUTES: int = 30
    
    # Circuit Breaker
    CIRCUIT_BREAKER_FAILURE_THRESHOLD: int = 5
    CIRCUIT_BREAKER_RECOVERY_TIMEOUT: int = 60
    CIRCUIT_BREAKER_EXPECTED_EXCEPTION: tuple = (Exception,)
    
    # Rate Limiting
    RATE_LIMIT_REQUESTS: int = 100
    RATE_LIMIT_PERIOD: int = 60  # seconds
    
    # Compression
    USE_RESPONSE_COMPRESSION: bool = True
    COMPRESSION_MIN_SIZE: int = 1024  # 1KB
    
    class Config:
        env_file = ".env"
        case_sensitive = True
    
    def __init__(self, **kwargs):
        super().__init__(**kwargs)
        if not self.DATABASE_URL:
            self.DATABASE_URL = f"postgresql+asyncpg://{self.POSTGRES_USER}:{self.POSTGRES_PASSWORD}@{self.POSTGRES_SERVER}/{self.POSTGRES_DB}"

settings = Settings()

# src/core/cache.py
import redis.asyncio as redis
from typing import Any, Optional, Union
import json
import pickle
from datetime import timedelta
import logging

logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)

class RedisCache:
    def __init__(self):
        self.redis_client: Optional[redis.Redis] = None
        
    async def connect(self):
        """Connect to Redis with circuit breaker pattern"""
        try:
            self.redis_client = await redis.Redis(
                host=settings.REDIS_HOST,
                port=settings.REDIS_PORT,
                password=settings.REDIS_PASSWORD,
                db=settings.REDIS_DB,
                decode_responses=False,
                socket_connect_timeout=5,
                socket_timeout=5,
                retry_on_timeout=True,
                max_connections=20
            )
            # Test connection
            await self.redis_client.ping()
            logger.info("Redis cache connected successfully")
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Failed to connect to Redis: {e}")
            self.redis_client = None
            raise
    
    async def disconnect(self):
        if self.redis_client:
            await self.redis_client.close()
    
    async def get(self, key: str) -> Optional[Any]:
        """Get value from cache with fallback"""
        if not self.redis_client:
            return None
            
        try:
            data = await self.redis_client.get(key)
            if data:
                try:
                    return pickle.loads(data)
                except:
                    return json.loads(data)
        except Exception as e:
            logger.warning(f"Cache get failed for key {key}: {e}")
        return None
    
    async def set(self, key: str, value: Any, ttl: Optional[int] = None) -> bool:
        """Set value in cache with TTL"""
        if not self.redis_client:
            return False
            
        try:
            if ttl is None:
                ttl = settings.REDIS_CACHE_TTL
            
            # Try pickle first (faster for Python objects), fallback to JSON
            try:
                serialized = pickle.dumps(value)
            except:
                serialized = json.dumps(value).encode('utf-8')
            
            await self.redis_client.setex(key, ttl, serialized)
            return True
        except Exception as e:
            logger.warning(f"Cache set failed for key {key}: {e}")
            return False
    
    async def delete(self, key: str) -> bool:
        """Delete key from cache"""
        if not self.redis_client:
            return False
            
        try:
            await self.redis_client.delete(key)
            return True
        except Exception as e:
            logger.warning(f"Cache delete failed for key {key}: {e}")
            return False
    
    async def delete_pattern(self, pattern: str) -> int:
        """Delete all keys matching pattern"""
        if not self.redis_client:
            return 0
            
        try:
            keys = await self.redis_client.keys(pattern)
            if keys:
                await self.redis_client.delete(*keys)
                return len(keys)
        except Exception as e:
            logger.warning(f"Cache delete pattern failed for {pattern}: {e}")
        return 0
    
    async def increment(self, key: str, amount: int = 1, ttl: Optional[int] = None) -> Optional[int]:
        """Atomic increment with optional TTL"""
        if not self.redis_client:
            return None
            
        try:
            async with self.redis_client.pipeline() as pipe:
                result = await pipe.incrby(key, amount).execute()
                if ttl:
                    await pipe.expire(key, ttl).execute()
                return result[0]
        except Exception as e:
            logger.warning(f"Cache increment failed for key {key}: {e}")
            return None

# Global cache instance
cache = RedisCache()

# src/core/circuit_breaker.py
from circuitbreaker import circuit
import time
import asyncio
from typing import Callable, Any, Dict
import logging
from functools import wraps

logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)

class CircuitBreaker:
    """Enhanced circuit breaker with metrics and fallback"""
    
    _instances: Dict[str, 'CircuitBreaker'] = {}
    
    def __init__(self, name: str, failure_threshold: int = 5, 
                 recovery_timeout: int = 60, expected_exception: tuple = (Exception,)):
        self.name = name
        self.failure_threshold = failure_threshold
        self.recovery_timeout = recovery_timeout
        self.expected_exception = expected_exception
        self.metrics = {
            'total_calls': 0,
            'successful_calls': 0,
            'failed_calls': 0,
            'circuit_opened': 0,
            'last_failure_time': None,
            'state': 'closed'  # closed, open, half-open
        }
    
    @classmethod
    def get_instance(cls, name: str) -> 'CircuitBreaker':
        if name not in cls._instances:
            cls._instances[name] = CircuitBreaker(
                name=name,
                failure_threshold=settings.CIRCUIT_BREAKER_FAILURE_THRESHOLD,
                recovery_timeout=settings.CIRCUIT_BREAKER_RECOVERY_TIMEOUT,
                expected_exception=settings.CIRCUIT_BREAKER_EXPECTED_EXCEPTION
            )
        return cls._instances[name]
    
    def __call__(self, func: Callable) -> Callable:
        """Decorator for circuit breaker"""
        @wraps(func)
        async def async_wrapper(*args, **kwargs):
            self.metrics['total_calls'] += 1
            
            if self.metrics['state'] == 'open':
                # Check if recovery timeout has passed
                if (self.metrics['last_failure_time'] and 
                    time.time() - self.metrics['last_failure_time'] > self.recovery_timeout):
                    self.metrics['state'] = 'half-open'
                else:
                    self.metrics['circuit_opened'] += 1
                    raise CircuitBreakerOpenError(
                        f"Circuit breaker '{self.name}' is OPEN. "
                        f"Failed {self.metrics['failed_calls']} times. "
                        f"Next try in {self.recovery_timeout - (time.time() - self.metrics['last_failure_time']):.0f}s"
                    )
            
            try:
                result = await func(*args, **kwargs)
                self.metrics['successful_calls'] += 1
                
                if self.metrics['state'] == 'half-open':
                    self.metrics['state'] = 'closed'
                    self.metrics['failed_calls'] = 0
                    logger.info(f"Circuit breaker '{self.name}' reset to CLOSED")
                
                return result
                
            except self.expected_exception as e:
                self.metrics['failed_calls'] += 1
                self.metrics['last_failure_time'] = time.time()
                
                if (self.metrics['state'] == 'closed' and 
                    self.metrics['failed_calls'] >= self.failure_threshold):
                    self.metrics['state'] = 'open'
                    self.metrics['circuit_opened'] += 1
                    logger.error(
                        f"Circuit breaker '{self.name}' OPENED. "
                        f"Failure threshold ({self.failure_threshold}) reached. "
                        f"Error: {str(e)}"
                    )
                elif self.metrics['state'] == 'half-open':
                    self.metrics['state'] = 'open'
                    logger.error(f"Circuit breaker '{self.name}' re-OPENED from half-open")
                
                raise
                
        return async_wrapper
    
    def get_metrics(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Get circuit breaker metrics"""
        return {
            **self.metrics,
            'failure_rate': (
                self.metrics['failed_calls'] / self.metrics['total_calls'] 
                if self.metrics['total_calls'] > 0 else 0
            )
        }

class CircuitBreakerOpenError(Exception):
    """Raised when circuit breaker is open"""
    pass

# src/utils/pagination.py
from typing import Generic, TypeVar, List, Optional
from pydantic import BaseModel
from math import ceil

T = TypeVar('T')

class PaginatedResponse(BaseModel, Generic[T]):
    items: List[T]
    total: int
    page: int
    size: int
    pages: int
    has_next: bool
    has_prev: bool
    
    @classmethod
    def create(cls, items: List[T], total: int, page: int, size: int) -> 'PaginatedResponse[T]':
        pages = ceil(total / size) if size > 0 else 0
        return cls(
            items=items,
            total=total,
            page=page,
            size=size,
            pages=pages,
            has_next=page < pages,
            has_prev=page > 1
        )

class PaginationParams(BaseModel):
    page: int = 1
    size: int = 20
    sort_by: Optional[str] = None
    sort_order: str = "asc"  # asc or desc
    
    def validate(self):
        if self.page < 1:
            self.page = 1
        if self.size < 1:
            self.size = 20
        if self.size > 100:
            self.size = 100
        if self.sort_order not in ["asc", "desc"]:
            self.sort_order = "asc"
        return self
    
    @property
    def offset(self) -> int:
        return (self.page - 1) * self.size
    
    @property
    def limit(self) -> int:
        return self.size

# src/utils/compression.py
import brotli
import gzip
from typing import Optional
from fastapi import Response
from fastapi.responses import JSONResponse

class CompressionMiddleware:
    """Middleware for response compression"""
    
    @staticmethod
    def compress_response(data: bytes, accept_encoding: str) -> Optional[bytes]:
        """Compress response based on accept-encoding header"""
        if not data or len(data) < settings.COMPRESSION_MIN_SIZE:
            return None
            
        if 'br' in accept_encoding:
            return brotli.compress(data)
        elif 'gzip' in accept_encoding:
            return gzip.compress(data)
        return None
    
    @staticmethod
    def create_compressed_response(
        content: Any,
        status_code: int = 200,
        headers: Optional[dict] = None,
        accept_encoding: str = ""
    ) -> Response:
        """Create response with compression if applicable"""
        import json
        
        # Convert to JSON if not already bytes
        if not isinstance(content, bytes):
            content_bytes = json.dumps(content).encode('utf-8')
        else:
            content_bytes = content
        
        # Check if compression should be applied
        compressed = None
        encoding = None
        
        if (settings.USE_RESPONSE_COMPRESSION and 
            len(content_bytes) >= settings.COMPRESSION_MIN_SIZE and 
            accept_encoding):
            
            compressed = CompressionMiddleware.compress_response(content_bytes, accept_encoding)
            if compressed and len(compressed) < len(content_bytes):
                content_bytes = compressed
                if 'br' in accept_encoding:
                    encoding = 'br'
                elif 'gzip' in accept_encoding:
                    encoding = 'gzip'
        
        # Create response
        response = Response(
            content=content_bytes,
            status_code=status_code,
            headers=headers or {}
        )
        
        if encoding:
            response.headers['Content-Encoding'] = encoding
            response.headers['Vary'] = 'Accept-Encoding'
        
        response.headers['Content-Length'] = str(len(content_bytes))
        return response

# src/api/v1/endpoints/health.py
from fastapi import APIRouter, Depends, HTTPException
from typing import Dict, Any
import asyncio
import time
from sqlalchemy import text
import logging

from src.core.cache import cache
from src.core.circuit_breaker import CircuitBreaker
from src.core.config import settings

router = APIRouter()
logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)

class HealthCheck:
    def __init__(self):
        self.start_time = time.time()
        self.circuit_breaker = CircuitBreaker.get_instance("health_check")
    
    async def check_database(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Check database connectivity and latency"""
        from src.models.database import async_session
        
        start = time.time()
        try:
            async with async_session() as session:
                # Simple query to check connectivity
                result = await session.execute(text("SELECT 1"))
                result.scalar()
                
                latency = (time.time() - start) * 1000  # ms
                return {
                    "status": "healthy",
                    "latency_ms": round(latency, 2),
                    "database": "postgresql"
                }
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Database health check failed: {e}")
            return {
                "status": "unhealthy",
                "error": str(e),
                "latency_ms": round((time.time() - start) * 1000, 2)
            }
    
    async def check_cache(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Check Redis cache connectivity and latency"""
        start = time.time()
        try:
            if cache.redis_client:
                await cache.redis_client.ping()
                latency = (time.time() - start) * 1000
                return {
                    "status": "healthy",
                    "latency_ms": round(latency, 2),
                    "cache": "redis"
                }
            else:


### [Sessão Paralela: Tech Leader]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V12 Core - Arquitetura de Microsserviços

## Estrutura do Projeto

```

├── .github/

## ADR-001: Arquitetura de Microsserviços

**Data:** 2024-03-15
**Status:** Aceita
**Autores:** Tech Lead

**CONTEXTO:**
DIYAPP precisa evoluir para uma arquitetura escalável que suporte:
1. Desenvolvimento paralelo por múltiplas squads (Modo Hive)
2. Deploy independente de componentes
3. Observabilidade completa
4. Estabilidade 100% autônoma

**DECISÃO:**
Adotar arquitetura baseada em microsserviços com os seguintes componentes:
1. API Gateway (NestJS) - ponto único de entrada
2. Serviços independentes por domínio
3. Comunicação via eventos (RabbitMQ) e REST
4. Containerização com Docker
5. Orquestração com Kubernetes
6. Observabilidade unificada (OpenTelemetry)

**OPÇÕES CONSIDERADAS:**
- **Opção A:** Monolito modular - Prós: Simplicidade inicial. Contras: Acoplamento, deploy único, dificulta desenvolvimento paralelo.
- **Opção B:** Microsserviços completos - Prós: Desacoplamento, deploy independente, escalabilidade. Contras: Complexidade operacional.
- **Opção escolhida:** B - Justificativa: Necessidade de desenvolvimento paralelo (Modo Hive) e estabilidade autônoma.

**CONSEQUÊNCIAS:**
**Positivas:** Desenvolvimento paralelo, resiliência, escalabilidade independente.
**Negativas:** Complexidade aumentada, necessidade de infraestrutura robusta.
**Riscos:** Latência em chamadas entre serviços, consistência eventual.

## Engineering Standards

### 1. Padrões de Código

```typescript
// libs/shared/config/coding-standards.ts
export const CODING_STANDARDS = {
  // Estrutura de pastas por serviço
  SERVICE_STRUCTURE: {
    src: {
      controllers: 'Controladores HTTP',
      services: 'Lógica de negócio',
      repositories: 'Acesso a dados',
      entities: 'Entidades de domínio',
      dto: 'Data Transfer Objects',
      interfaces: 'Contratos de interface',
      middleware: 'Middleware HTTP',
      filters: 'Filtros de exceção',
      guards: 'Guards de autorização',
      interceptors: 'Interceptores',
      config: 'Configurações',
      utils: 'Utilitários'
    }
  },

  // Convenções de nomenclatura
  NAMING_CONVENTIONS: {
    classes: 'PascalCase',
    variables: 'camelCase',
    constants: 'UPPER_SNAKE_CASE',
    interfaces: 'I{PascalCase}',
    files: 'kebab-case',
    tests: '{filename}.spec.ts'
  },

  // Configurações de TypeScript
  TYPESCRIPT: {
    strict: true,
    noImplicitAny: true,
    strictNullChecks: true,
    strictFunctionTypes: true,
    noUnusedLocals: true,
    noUnusedParameters: true
  }
};
```

### 2. Template de Serviço

```typescript
// services/template-service/src/main.ts
import { NestFactory } from '@nestjs/core';
import { AppModule } from './app.module';
import { ValidationPipe } from '@nestjs/common';
import { Logger } from './utils/logger';
import { setupSwagger } from './config/swagger';
import { setupMetrics } from './config/metrics';
import { setupTracing } from './config/tracing';

async function bootstrap() {
  const logger = new Logger('Bootstrap');
  
  try {
    const app = await NestFactory.create(AppModule, {
      logger: ['error', 'warn', 'log', 'debug', 'verbose'],
      bufferLogs: true,
    });

    // Configurações
    app.useGlobalPipes(new ValidationPipe({ transform: true, whitelist: true }));
    app.setGlobalPrefix('api/v1');
    
    // Observabilidade
    setupTracing(app);
    setupMetrics(app);
    
    // Documentação
    if (process.env.NODE_ENV !== 'production') {
      setupSwagger(app);
    }

    // CORS
    app.enableCors({
      origin: process.env.ALLOWED_ORIGINS?.split(',') || '*',
      methods: 'GET,HEAD,PUT,PATCH,POST,DELETE',
      credentials: true,
    });

    const port = process.env.PORT || 3000;
    await app.listen(port);
    
    logger.log(`Service started on port ${port}`);
    logger.log(`Environment: ${process.env.NODE_ENV}`);
    
  } catch (error) {
    logger.error('Failed to start service', error);
    process.exit(1);
  }
}

bootstrap();
```

### 3. Logger Padronizado

```typescript
// libs/shared/utils/logger.ts
import { Injectable, Scope } from '@nestjs/common';
import * as winston from 'winston';
import { OpenTelemetryTransport } from './opentelemetry-transport';

@Injectable({ scope: Scope.TRANSIENT })
export class Logger {
  private context: string;
  private logger: winston.Logger;

  constructor(context?: string) {
    this.context = context || 'Application';
    this.initializeLogger();
  }

  private initializeLogger() {
    const format = winston.format.combine(
      winston.format.timestamp(),
      winston.format.errors({ stack: true }),
      winston.format.json()
    );

    this.logger = winston.createLogger({
      level: process.env.LOG_LEVEL || 'info',
      format,
      defaultMeta: {
        service: process.env.SERVICE_NAME,
        context: this.context,
        environment: process.env.NODE_ENV,
      },
      transports: [
        new winston.transports.Console(),
        new OpenTelemetryTransport(),
      ],
    });
  }

  setContext(context: string) {
    this.context = context;
    this.logger.defaultMeta = { ...this.logger.defaultMeta, context };
  }

  log(message: string, meta?: any) {
    this.logger.info(message, meta);
  }

  error(message: string, trace?: any, meta?: any) {
    this.logger.error(message, { ...meta, trace });
  }

  warn(message: string, meta?: any) {
    this.logger.warn(message, meta);
  }

  debug(message: string, meta?: any) {
    this.logger.debug(message, meta);
  }

  verbose(message: string, meta?: any) {
    this.logger.verbose(message, meta);
  }
}
```

### 4. Configuração OpenTelemetry

```typescript
// libs/shared/config/tracing.ts
import { NestApplication } from '@nestjs/core';
import { NodeSDK } from '@opentelemetry/sdk-node';
import { getNodeAutoInstrumentations } from '@opentelemetry/auto-instrumentations-node';
import { OTLPTraceExporter } from '@opentelemetry/exporter-trace-otlp-grpc';
import { Resource } from '@opentelemetry/resources';
import { SemanticResourceAttributes } from '@opentelemetry/semantic-conventions';
import { BatchSpanProcessor } from '@opentelemetry/sdk-trace-node';
import { WinstonInstrumentation } from '@opentelemetry/instrumentation-winston';

export function setupTracing(app: NestApplication) {
  if (process.env.ENABLE_TRACING !== 'true') return;

  const traceExporter = new OTLPTraceExporter({
    url: process.env.OTLP_ENDPOINT || 'http://jaeger:4317',
  });

  const sdk = new NodeSDK({
    resource: new Resource({
      [SemanticResourceAttributes.SERVICE_NAME]: process.env.SERVICE_NAME,
      [SemanticResourceAttributes.SERVICE_VERSION]: process.env.VERSION || '1.0.0',
      [SemanticResourceAttributes.DEPLOYMENT_ENVIRONMENT]: process.env.NODE_ENV || 'development',
    }),
    spanProcessor: new BatchSpanProcessor(traceExporter),
    instrumentations: [
      getNodeAutoInstrumentations({
        '@opentelemetry/instrumentation-http': {
          enabled: true,
        },
        '@opentelemetry/instrumentation-nestjs-core': {
          enabled: true,
        },
      }),
      new WinstonInstrumentation(),
    ],
  });

  sdk.start();

  // Graceful shutdown
  process.on('SIGTERM', async () => {
    try {
      await sdk.shutdown();
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Error shutting down tracing', error);
    }
  });
}
```

## Docker Configuration

```yaml
# docker/docker-compose.yml
version: '3.8'

services:
  # Banco de dados
  postgres:
    image: postgres:15-alpine
    environment:
      POSTGRES_DB: diyapp
      POSTGRES_USER: ${DB_USER:-diyapp}
      POSTGRES_PASSWORD: ${DB_PASSWORD:-secret}
    volumes:
      - postgres_data:/var/lib/postgresql/data
    networks:
      - diyapp-network
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD-SHELL", "pg_isready -U ${DB_USER:-diyapp}"]
      interval: 10s
      timeout: 5s
      retries: 5

  # Message Broker
  rabbitmq:
    image: rabbitmq:3.12-management-alpine
    environment:
      RABBITMQ_DEFAULT_USER: ${RABBITMQ_USER:-admin}
      RABBITMQ_DEFAULT_PASS: ${RABBITMQ_PASS:-admin}
    ports:
      - "15672:15672" # Management UI
    volumes:
      - rabbitmq_data:/var/lib/rabbitmq
    networks:
      - diyapp-network
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD", "rabbitmq-diagnostics", "ping"]
      interval: 30s
      timeout: 10s
      retries: 5

  # Cache
  redis:
    image: redis:7-alpine
    command: redis-server --appendonly yes
    volumes:
      - redis_data:/data
    networks:
      - diyapp-network
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD", "redis-cli", "ping"]
      interval: 10s
      timeout: 5s
      retries: 5

  # Observabilidade
  jaeger:
    image: jaegertracing/all-in-one:1.48
    environment:
      COLLECTOR_OTLP_ENABLED: true
    ports:
      - "16686:16686" # UI
      - "4317:4317"   # OTLP gRPC
      - "4318:4318"   # OTLP HTTP
    networks:
      - diyapp-network

  prometheus:
    image: prom/prometheus:latest
    volumes:
      - ./infrastructure/monitoring/prometheus/prometheus.yml:/etc/prometheus/prometheus.yml
      - prometheus_data:/prometheus
    command:
      - '--config.file=/etc/prometheus/prometheus.yml'
      - '--storage.tsdb.path=/prometheus'
      - '--web.console.libraries=/etc/prometheus/console_libraries'
      - '--web.console.templates=/etc/prometheus/consoles'
      - '--storage.tsdb.retention.time=200h'
      - '--web.enable-lifecycle'
    ports:
      - "9090:9090"
    networks:
      - diyapp-network

  grafana:
    image: grafana/grafana:latest
    environment:
      GF_SECURITY_ADMIN_PASSWORD: ${GRAFANA_PASSWORD:-admin}
    volumes:
      - grafana_data:/var/lib/grafana
      - ./infrastructure/monitoring/grafana/dashboards:/etc/grafana/provisioning/dashboards
      - ./infrastructure/monitoring/grafana/datasources:/etc/grafana/provisioning/datasources
    ports:
      - "3001:3000"
    networks:
      - diyapp-network
    depends_on:
      prometheus:
        condition: service_healthy

  loki:
    image: grafana/loki:latest
    command: -config.file=/etc/loki/local-config.yaml
    ports:
      - "3100:3100"
    volumes:
      - loki_data:/loki
    networks:
      - diyapp-network

  tempo:
    image: grafana/tempo:latest
    command: -config.file=/etc/tempo.yaml
    volumes:
      - ./infrastructure/monitoring/tempo/tempo.yaml:/etc/tempo.yaml
      - tempo_data:/tmp/tempo
    ports:
      - "3200:3200" # tempo
      - "4317:4317" # otlp grpc
      - "4318:4318" # otlp http
    networks:
      - diyapp-network

volumes:
  postgres_data:
  rabbitmq_data:
  redis_data:
  prometheus_data:
  grafana_data:
  loki_data:
  tempo_data:

networks:
  diyapp-network:
    driver: bridge
```

## CI/CD Pipeline

```yaml
# .github/workflows/ci-pipeline.yml
name: CI Pipeline

on:
  push:
    branches: [main, develop]
  pull_request:
    branches: [main, develop]

jobs:
  quality-gate:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v3
      
      - name: Setup Node.js
        uses: actions/setup-node@v3
        with:
          node-version: '18'
          cache: 'npm'
      
      - name: Install dependencies
        run: npm ci
      
      - name: Lint
        run: npm run lint
      
      - name: Type check
        run: npm run type-check
      
      - name: Unit tests
        run: npm run test:cov
      
      - name: Upload coverage
        uses: codecov/codecov-action@v3
        with:
          file: ./coverage/lcov.info
          flags: unittests
      
      - name: Security scan
        uses: snyk/actions/node@master
        env:
          SNYK_TOKEN: ${{ secrets.SNYK_TOKEN }}
        with:
          args: --severity-threshold=high

  build-services:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    needs: quality-gate
    strategy:
      matrix:
        service: [api-gateway, auth-service, user-service, task-service, notification-service]
    
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v3
      
      - name: Set up Docker Buildx
        uses: docker/setup-buildx-action@v2
      
      - name: Login to DockerHub
        uses: docker/login-action@v2
        with:
          username: ${{ secrets.DOCKER_USERNAME }}
          password: ${{ secrets.DOCKER_PASSWORD }}
      
      - name: Build and push
        uses: docker/build-push-action@v4
        with:
          context: ./services/${{ matrix.service }}
          push: ${{ github.event_name != 'pull_request' }}
          tags: |
            ${{ secrets.DOCKER_USERNAME }}/${{ matrix.service }}:${{ github.sha }}
            ${{ secrets.DOCKER_USERNAME }}/${{ matrix.service }}:latest
          cache-from: type=gha
          cache-to: type=gha,mode=max
```

```yaml
# .github/workflows/cd-pipeline.yml
name: CD Pipeline

on:
  push:
    branches: [main]
  workflow_dispatch:

jobs:
  deploy-staging:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    environment: staging
    
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v3
      
      - name: Configure kubectl
        uses: azure/setup-kubectl@v3
        with:
          version: 'latest'
      
      - name: Deploy to Kubernetes
        run: |
          kubectl apply -f infrastructure/k8s/namespaces/
          kubectl apply -f infrastructure/k8s/configmaps/
          kubectl apply -f infrastructure/k8s/secrets/
          kubectl apply -f infrastructure/k8s/deployments/
          kubectl apply -f infrastructure/k8s/services/
      
      - name: Run integration tests
        run: npm run test:e2e
      
      - name: Health check
        run: |
          ./scripts/health-check.sh

  deploy-production:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    needs: deploy-staging
    environment: production
    
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v3
      
      - name: Blue-green deployment
        run: |
          ./scripts/blue-green-deploy.sh
      
      - name: Smoke tests
        run: |
          ./scripts/smoke-tests.sh
      
      - name: Monitor deployment
        run: |
          ./scripts/monitor-deployment.sh
```

  --shadow-lg: 0 10px 15px -3px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.1), 0 4px 6px -2px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.05);
  --shadow-xl: 0 20px 25px -5px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.1), 0 10px 10px -5px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04);
  --shadow-inner: inset 0 2px 4px 0 rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.06);
  
  /* ===== ANIMAÇÕES ===== */
  --transition-fast: 150ms cubic-bezier(0.4, 0, 0.2, 1);
  --transition-normal: 250ms cubic-bezier(0.4, 0, 0.2, 1);
  --transition-slow: 350ms cubic-bezier(0.4, 0, 0.2, 1);
  
  /* ===== Z-INDEX ===== */
  --z-index-dropdown: 1000;
  --z-index-sticky: 1020;
  --z-index-fixed: 1030;
  --z-index-modal-backdrop: 1040;
  --z-index-modal: 1050;
  --z-index-popover: 1060;
  --z-index-tooltip: 1070;
  
  /* ===== LAYOUT ===== */
  --container-max-width: 1280px;
  --sidebar-width: 280px;
  --header-height: 64px;
  
  /* ===== ACESSIBILIDADE ===== */
  /* Contraste verificado - todos acima de 4.5:1 para AA */
  --focus-ring-color: var(--color-primary-500);
  --focus-ring-width: 3px;
  --focus-ring-offset: 2px;
}

### [Sessão Paralela: Backend]
```python
# ============================================
# DIYAPP Evolution - V12 Core
# Dev Backend: Serviços Core Refatorados
# ============================================

# Estrutura do projeto:
# /src
#   /api_gateway
#   /auth_service
#   /task_service
#   /shared
# /tests
# /migrations
# /docs
# /runbooks
# index.html (dashboard de monitoramento)

# ============================================
# 1. API GATEWAY
# ============================================

# src/api_gateway/main.py
import asyncio
import json
import logging
from datetime import datetime
from typing import Dict, Any, Optional
from fastapi import FastAPI, Request, Response, HTTPException, Depends
from fastapi.middleware.cors import CORSMiddleware
from fastapi.responses import JSONResponse
from pydantic import BaseModel, ValidationError
import httpx
from circuitbreaker import circuit
from prometheus_client import Counter, Histogram, generate_latest
import redis.asyncio as redis
from uuid import uuid4
import os

# Configuração de logging estruturado
logging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO)
logger = logging.getLogger("api_gateway")

# Métricas Prometheus
REQUEST_COUNT = Counter('http_requests_total', 'Total HTTP Requests', ['method', 'endpoint', 'status'])
REQUEST_LATENCY = Histogram('http_request_duration_seconds', 'HTTP request latency', ['method', 'endpoint'])

app = FastAPI(title="DIYAPP API Gateway", version="1.0.0")

# CORS
app.add_middleware(
    CORSMiddleware,
    allow_origins=os.getenv("ALLOWED_ORIGINS", "*").split(","),
    allow_credentials=True,
    allow_methods=["*"],
    allow_headers=["*"],
)

# Redis para rate limiting e circuit breaker state
redis_client = None

async def get_redis():
    global redis_client
    if redis_client is None:
        redis_client = redis.from_url(
            os.getenv("REDIS_URL", "redis://localhost:6379"),
            decode_responses=True
        )
    return redis_client

# Circuit breaker configuration
def circuit_failure_callback(func, args, kwargs, exception, elapsed):
    logger.error({
        "level": "error",
        "service": "circuit_breaker",
        "function": func.__name__,
        "exception": str(exception),
        "elapsed_ms": elapsed * 1000
    })

# Rate limiting middleware
async def rate_limit_middleware(request: Request, call_next):
    correlation_id = request.headers.get("X-Correlation-ID", str(uuid4()))
    
    # Log structured
    logger.info({
        "level": "info",
        "correlation_id": correlation_id,
        "user_id": request.headers.get("X-User-ID"),
        "endpoint": f"{request.method} {request.url.path}",
        "ip": request.client.host if request.client else None
    })
    
    # Rate limiting (10 requests per minute per IP)
    redis_conn = await get_redis()
    key = f"rate_limit:{request.client.host}:{request.url.path}"
    current = await redis_conn.incr(key)
    
    if current == 1:
        await redis_conn.expire(key, 60)
    
    if current > 10:
        logger.warning({
            "level": "warning",
            "correlation_id": correlation_id,
            "message": "Rate limit exceeded",
            "ip": request.client.host,
            "endpoint": request.url.path
        })
        return JSONResponse(
            status_code=429,
            content={"error": "Too many requests", "retry_after": 60}
        )
    
    # Process request with metrics
    start_time = datetime.now()
    
    try:
        response = await call_next(request)
        duration = (datetime.now() - start_time).total_seconds()
        
        REQUEST_COUNT.labels(
            method=request.method,
            endpoint=request.url.path,
            status=response.status_code
        ).inc()
        
        REQUEST_LATENCY.labels(
            method=request.method,
            endpoint=request.url.path
        ).observe(duration)
        
        # Add correlation ID to response
        response.headers["X-Correlation-ID"] = correlation_id
        
        logger.info({
            "level": "info",
            "correlation_id": correlation_id,
            "duration_ms": duration * 1000,
            "status": response.status_code,
            "endpoint": f"{request.method} {request.url.path}"
        })
        
        return response
        
    except Exception as e:
        duration = (datetime.now() - start_time).total_seconds()
        logger.error({
            "level": "error",
            "correlation_id": correlation_id,
            "error": str(e),
            "duration_ms": duration * 1000,
            "endpoint": f"{request.method} {request.url.path}",
            "stack_trace": None  # Never log full stack trace in production
        })
        
        REQUEST_COUNT.labels(
            method=request.method,
            endpoint=request.url.path,
            status=500
        ).inc()
        
        return JSONResponse(
            status_code=500,
            content={"error": "Internal server error"},
            headers={"X-Correlation-ID": correlation_id}
        )

app.middleware("http")(rate_limit_middleware)

# Service discovery and routing
SERVICES = {
    "auth": os.getenv("AUTH_SERVICE_URL", "http://localhost:8001"),
    "tasks": os.getenv("TASK_SERVICE_URL", "http://localhost:8002"),
}

# Circuit breaker for external services
@circuit(
    failure_threshold=5,
    recovery_timeout=30,
    expected_exception=httpx.HTTPStatusError,
    fallback_function=lambda: {"error": "Service temporarily unavailable"},
    name="external_service"
)
async def call_service(
    service_name: str,
    method: str,
    path: str,
    data: Optional[Dict] = None,
    headers: Optional[Dict] = None,
    timeout: float = 5.0
) -> Dict[str, Any]:
    """Call external service with circuit breaker and retry logic"""
    service_url = SERVICES.get(service_name)
    if not service_url:
        raise HTTPException(status_code=502, detail=f"Service {service_name} not configured")
    
    async with httpx.AsyncClient(timeout=timeout) as client:
        url = f"{service_url}{path}"
        
        # Add correlation ID if not present
        headers = headers or {}
        if "X-Correlation-ID" not in headers:
            headers["X-Correlation-ID"] = str(uuid4())
        
        # Retry logic with exponential backoff
        max_retries = 3
        for attempt in range(max_retries):
            try:
                if method == "GET":
                    response = await client.get(url, headers=headers)
                elif method == "POST":
                    response = await client.post(url, json=data, headers=headers)
                elif method == "PUT":
                    response = await client.put(url, json=data, headers=headers)
                elif method == "DELETE":
                    response = await client.delete(url, headers=headers)
                else:
                    raise ValueError(f"Unsupported method: {method}")
                
                response.raise_for_status()
                return response.json()
                
            except (httpx.TimeoutException, httpx.ConnectError) as e:
                if attempt == max_retries - 1:
                    logger.error({
                        "level": "error",
                        "service": service_name,
                        "error": f"Service timeout after {max_retries} attempts",
                        "url": url
                    })
                    raise
                await asyncio.sleep(2 ** attempt)  # Exponential backoff
                continue
                
            except httpx.HTTPStatusError as e:
                # Don't retry on client errors (4xx)
                if 400 <= e.response.status_code < 500:
                    raise HTTPException(
                        status_code=e.response.status_code,
                        detail=e.response.json().get("detail", "Client error")
                    )
                raise

# Authentication middleware
async def verify_token(request: Request):
    """Verify JWT token before routing to services"""
    auth_header = request.headers.get("Authorization")
    
    if not auth_header or not auth_header.startswith("Bearer "):
        raise HTTPException(status_code=401, detail="Missing or invalid authorization header")
    
    token = auth_header.split(" ")[1]
    
    # Call auth service to validate token
    try:
        user_data = await call_service(
            "auth",
            "POST",
            "/auth/verify",
            data={"token": token},
            timeout=2.0
        )
        request.state.user = user_data
    except HTTPException:
        raise
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error({
            "level": "error",
            "message": "Auth service unavailable",
            "error": str(e)
        })
        raise HTTPException(status_code=503, detail="Authentication service unavailable")

# Routes
@app.get("/health")
async def health_check():
    """Health check endpoint"""
    services_status = {}
    
    for service_name, url in SERVICES.items():
        try:
            async with httpx.AsyncClient(timeout=1.0) as client:
                response = await client.get(f"{url}/health")
                services_status[service_name] = response.status_code == 200
        except Exception:
            services_status[service_name] = False
    
    return {
        "status": "healthy",
        "timestamp": datetime.now().isoformat(),
        "services": services_status
    }

@app.get("/metrics")
async def metrics():
    """Prometheus metrics endpoint"""
    return Response(content=generate_latest(), media_type="text/plain")

# Task service routes (protected)
@app.get("/api/v1/tasks")
async def get_tasks(request: Request, user=Depends(verify_token)):
    """Get user tasks"""
    return await call_service(
        "tasks",
        "GET",
        "/api/v1/tasks",
        headers={"X-User-ID": str(request.state.user["id"])}
    )

@app.post("/api/v1/tasks")
async def create_task(request: Request, user=Depends(verify_token)):
    """Create new task"""
    data = await request.json()
    return await call_service(
        "tasks",
        "POST",
        "/api/v1/tasks",
        data=data,
        headers={"X-User-ID": str(request.state.user["id"])}
    )

# ============================================
# 2. AUTHENTICATION SERVICE
# ============================================

# src/auth_service/main.py
import asyncio
import jwt
import bcrypt
from datetime import datetime, timedelta
from typing import Optional, Dict, Any
from fastapi import FastAPI, HTTPException, Depends
from fastapi.security import OAuth2PasswordBearer, OAuth2PasswordRequestForm
from pydantic import BaseModel, EmailStr, validator
import asyncpg
from contextlib import asynccontextmanager
import os

# Models
class UserCreate(BaseModel):
    email: EmailStr
    password: str
    name: str
    
    @validator('password')
    def validate_password(cls, v):
        if len(v) < 8:
            raise ValueError('Password must be at least 8 characters')
        return v

class UserLogin(BaseModel):
    email: EmailStr
    password: str

class Token(BaseModel):
    access_token: str
    token_type: str
    expires_in: int
    refresh_token: str

class TokenData(BaseModel):
    user_id: int
    email: str

# Database connection pool
pool = None

@asynccontextmanager
async def lifespan(app: FastAPI):
    # Startup
    global pool
    pool = await asyncpg.create_pool(
        dsn=os.getenv("DATABASE_URL", "postgresql://user:password@localhost/diyapp"),
        min_size=5,
        max_size=20
    )
    
    # Run migrations
    await run_migrations()
    
    yield
    
    # Shutdown
    await pool.close()

app = FastAPI(title="DIYAPP Auth Service", version="1.0.0", lifespan=lifespan)

oauth2_scheme = OAuth2PasswordBearer(tokenUrl="/auth/login")

# JWT Configuration
JWT_SECRET = os.getenv("JWT_SECRET", "your-secret-key-change-in-production")
JWT_ALGORITHM = "HS256"
ACCESS_TOKEN_EXPIRE_MINUTES = 30
REFRESH_TOKEN_EXPIRE_DAYS = 7

# Password hashing
def hash_password(password: str) -> str:
    salt = bcrypt.gensalt()
    return bcrypt.hashpw(password.encode(), salt).decode()

def verify_password(plain_password: str, hashed_password: str) -> bool:
    return bcrypt.checkpw(plain_password.encode(), hashed_password.encode())

# JWT functions
def create_access_token(data: Dict[str, Any], expires_delta: Optional[timedelta] = None) -> str:
    to_encode = data.copy()
    if expires_delta:
        expire = datetime.utcnow() + expires_delta
    else:
        expire = datetime.utcnow() + timedelta(minutes=ACCESS_TOKEN_EXPIRE_MINUTES)
    
    to_encode.update({"exp": expire, "type": "access"})
    return jwt.encode(to_encode, JWT_SECRET, algorithm=JWT_ALGORITHM)

def create_refresh_token(data: Dict[str, Any]) -> str:
    to_encode = data.copy()
    expire = datetime.utcnow() + timedelta(days=REFRESH_TOKEN_EXPIRE_DAYS)
    to_encode.update({"exp": expire, "type": "refresh"})
    return jwt.encode(to_encode, JWT_SECRET, algorithm=JWT_ALGORITHM)

async def verify_token(token: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:
    try:
        payload = jwt.decode(token, JWT_SECRET, algorithms=[JWT_ALGORITHM])
        
        # Check token type
        if payload.get("type") not in ["access", "refresh"]:
            raise HTTPException(status_code=401, detail="Invalid token type")
        
        # Check if token is blacklisted
        async with pool.acquire() as conn:
            blacklisted = await conn.fetchval(
                "SELECT 1 FROM token_blacklist WHERE token = $1",
                token
            )
            if blacklisted:
                raise HTTPException(status_code=401, detail="Token revoked")
        
        return payload
    except jwt.ExpiredSignatureError:
        raise HTTPException(status_code=401, detail="Token expired")
    except jwt.InvalidTokenError:
        raise HTTPException(status_code=401, detail="Invalid token")

# Database operations with prepared statements
async def create_user(email: str, password: str, name: str) -> int:
    async with pool.acquire() as conn:
        # Check if user exists
        existing = await conn.fetchval(
            "SELECT id FROM users WHERE email = $1",
            email
        )
        if existing:
            raise HTTPException(status_code=409, detail="Email already registered")
        
        # Create user with parameterized query
        user_id = await conn.fetchval(
            "INSERT INTO users (email, password_hash, name, created_at) VALUES ($1, $2, $3, $4) RETURNING id",
            email,
            hash_password(password),
            name,
            datetime.utcnow()
        )
        return user_id

async def authenticate_user(email: str, password: str) -> Optional[Dict[str, Any]]:
    async with pool.acquire() as conn:
        # Parameterized query - NO string concatenation
        user = await conn.fetchrow(
            "SELECT id, email, password_hash, name FROM users WHERE email = $1",
            email
        )
        
        if not user or not verify_password(password, user["password_hash"]):
            return None
        
        return {
            "id": user["id"],
            "email": user["email"],
            "name": user["name"]
        }

# Routes
@app.post("/auth/register")
async def register(user_data: UserCreate):
    """Register new user"""
    try:
        user_id = await create_user(
            user_data.email,
            user_data.password,
            user_data.name
        )
        
        # Create tokens
        token_data = {"user_id": user_id, "email": user_data.email}
        access_token = create_access_token(token_data)
        refresh_token = create_refresh_token(token_data)
        
        # Store refresh token
        async with pool.acquire() as conn:
            await conn.execute(
                "INSERT INTO refresh_tokens (user_id, token, expires_at) VALUES ($1, $2, $3)",
                user_id,
                refresh_token,
                datetime.utcnow() + timedelta(days=REFRESH_TOKEN_EXPIRE_DAYS)
            )
        
        return Token(
            access_token=access_token,
            token_type="bearer",
            expires_in=ACCESS_TOKEN_EXPIRE_MINUTES * 60,
            refresh_token=refresh_token
        )
        
    except HTTPException:
        raise
    except Exception as e:
        # Never expose internal errors
        raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail="Registration failed")

@app.post("/auth/login")
async def login(form_data: OAuth2PasswordRequestForm = Depends()):
    """Login user"""
    user = await authenticate_user(form_data.username, form_data.password)
    
    if not user:
        raise HTTPException(status_code=401, detail="Invalid credentials")
    
    # Create tokens
    token_data = {"user_id": user["id"], "email": user["email"]}
    access_token = create_access_token(token_data)
    refresh_token = create_refresh_token(token_data)
    
    # Store refresh token
    async with pool.acquire() as conn:
        await conn.execute(
            "INSERT INTO refresh_tokens (user_id, token, expires_at) VALUES ($1, $2, $3)",
            user["id"],
            refresh_token,
            datetime.utcnow() + timedelta(days=REFRESH_TOKEN_EXPIRE_DAYS)
        )
    
    return Token(
        access_token=access_token,
        token_type="bearer",
        expires_in=ACCESS_TOKEN_EXPIRE_MINUTES * 60,
        refresh_token=refresh_token
    )

@app.post("/auth/verify")
async def verify(token_data: Dict[str, str]):
    """Verify JWT token"""
    token = token_data.get("token")
    if not token:
        raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail="Token required")
    
    payload =

```typescript
// src/types/index.ts
export interface User {
  id: string;
  name: string;
  email: string;
  avatar?: string;
  role: 'admin' | 'user' | 'viewer';
  lastActive: Date;
}

export interface DashboardMetric {
  id: string;
  title: string;
  value: number | string;
  change: number;
  trend: 'up' | 'down' | 'stable';
  format?: 'number' | 'currency' | 'percentage';
}

export interface Notification {
  id: string;
  type: 'info' | 'success' | 'warning' | 'error';
  title: string;
  message: string;
  timestamp: Date;
  read: boolean;
}

export interface WebSocketMessage {
  type: 'notification' | 'metric_update' | 'system_alert' | 'user_activity';
  payload: any;
  timestamp: string;
}

export interface AppState {
  user: User | null;
  notifications: Notification[];
  metrics: DashboardMetric[];
  isLoading: boolean;
  error: string | null;
  lastUpdate: Date | null;
}
```

```typescript
// src/stores/useAppStore.ts
import { create } from 'zustand';
import { persist } from 'zustand/middleware';
import { AppState, User, Notification, DashboardMetric } from '@/types';

interface AppStore extends AppState {
  setUser: (user: User | null) => void;
  addNotification: (notification: Omit<Notification, 'id' | 'timestamp' | 'read'>) => void;
  markNotificationAsRead: (id: string) => void;
  clearNotifications: () => void;
  updateMetrics: (metrics: DashboardMetric[]) => void;
  setLoading: (isLoading: boolean) => void;
  setError: (error: string | null) => void;
  updateLastUpdate: () => void;
  reset: () => void;
}

const initialState: AppState = {
  user: null,
  notifications: [],
  metrics: [],
  isLoading: false,
  error: null,
  lastUpdate: null,
};

export const useAppStore = create<AppStore>()(
  persist(
    (set, get) => ({
      ...initialState,
      
      setUser: (user) => set({ user }),
      
      addNotification: (notification) => {
        const newNotification: Notification = {
          ...notification,
          id: crypto.randomUUID(),
          timestamp: new Date(),
          read: false,
        };
        
        set((state) => ({
          notifications: [newNotification, ...state.notifications].slice(0, 50), // Keep last 50
        }));
      },
      
      markNotificationAsRead: (id) =>
        set((state) => ({
          notifications: state.notifications.map((n) =>
            n.id === id ? { ...n, read: true } : n
          ),
        })),
      
      clearNotifications: () => set({ notifications: [] }),
      
      updateMetrics: (metrics) => set({ metrics, lastUpdate: new Date() }),
      
      setLoading: (isLoading) => set({ isLoading }),
      
      setError: (error) => set({ error }),
      
      updateLastUpdate: () => set({ lastUpdate: new Date() }),
      
      reset: () => set(initialState),
    }),
    {
      name: 'diyapp-store',
      partialize: (state) => ({
        user: state.user,
        notifications: state.notifications,
      }),
    }
  )
);
```

```typescript
// src/hooks/useWebSocket.ts
import { useEffect, useRef, useCallback } from 'react';
import { io, Socket } from 'socket.io-client';
import { useAppStore } from '@/stores/useAppStore';
import { WebSocketMessage } from '@/types';

const WS_URL = import.meta.env.VITE_WS_URL || 'ws://localhost:3000';

export const useWebSocket = () => {
  const socketRef = useRef<Socket | null>(null);
  const { addNotification, updateMetrics } = useAppStore();

  const connect = useCallback(() => {
    if (socketRef.current?.connected) return;

    socketRef.current = io(WS_URL, {
      transports: ['websocket'],
      reconnection: true,
      reconnectionAttempts: 5,
      reconnectionDelay: 1000,
    });

    socketRef.current.on('connect', () => {
      console.log('WebSocket connected');
      addNotification({
        type: 'success',
        title: 'Connection Established',
        message: 'Real-time updates are now active',
      });
    });

    socketRef.current.on('message', (message: WebSocketMessage) => {
      switch (message.type) {
        case 'notification':
          addNotification(message.payload);
          break;
        case 'metric_update':
          updateMetrics(message.payload);
          break;
        case 'system_alert':
          addNotification({
            type: 'warning',
            title: 'System Alert',
            message: message.payload.message,
          });
          break;
        case 'user_activity':
          // Handle user activity updates
          break;
      }
    });

    socketRef.current.on('disconnect', (reason) => {
      console.log('WebSocket disconnected:', reason);
      if (reason === 'io server disconnect') {
        // Server initiated disconnect, try to reconnect
        socketRef.current?.connect();
      }
    });

    socketRef.current.on('connect_error', (error) => {
      console.error('WebSocket connection error:', error);
      addNotification({
        type: 'error',
        title: 'Connection Error',
        message: 'Failed to establish real-time connection',
      });
    });
  }, [addNotification, updateMetrics]);

  const disconnect = useCallback(() => {
    if (socketRef.current) {
      socketRef.current.disconnect();
      socketRef.current = null;
    }
  }, []);

  const send = useCallback((type: string, payload: any) => {
    if (socketRef.current?.connected) {
      socketRef.current.emit('message', { type, payload, timestamp: new Date().toISOString() });
    }
  }, []);

  useEffect(() => {
    connect();

    return () => {
      disconnect();
    };
  }, [connect, disconnect]);

  return { send, disconnect, reconnect: connect };
};
```

                  <span className="absolute -top-1 -right-1 h-5 w-5 bg-error-500 text-white text

## 1. Configuração do Data Warehouse (BigQuery)

### `scripts/setup_warehouse.sql`

```sql
-- DIYAPP Telemetry Warehouse Setup
-- Data Engineer: Senior Squad

-- Schema para dados raw (bronze)
CREATE SCHEMA IF NOT EXISTS `diyapp-prod.telemetry_raw`
OPTIONS(
  description = 'Dados brutos de telemetria - nunca deletar',
  location = 'us-central1'
);

-- Schema para dados staging (silver)
CREATE SCHEMA IF NOT EXISTS `diyapp-prod.telemetry_staging`
OPTIONS(
  description = 'Dados limpos e padronizados',
  location = 'us-central1'
);

-- Schema para dados marts (gold)
CREATE SCHEMA IF NOT EXISTS `diyapp-prod.telemetry_marts`
OPTIONS(
  description = 'Dados prontos para consumo por squads',
  location = 'us-central1'
);

-- Tabelas raw
CREATE OR REPLACE TABLE `diyapp-prod.telemetry_raw.web_vitals` (
  event_id STRING NOT NULL,
  session_id STRING NOT NULL,
  user_id STRING,
  page_url STRING,
  metric_name STRING,
  metric_value FLOAT64,
  rating STRING,
  device_type STRING,
  browser STRING,
  country_code STRING,
  event_timestamp TIMESTAMP,
  received_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP(),
  _source_file STRING,
  _load_timestamp TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP()
)
PARTITION BY DATE(event_timestamp)
CLUSTER BY session_id, metric_name
OPTIONS(
  description = 'Dados brutos de Core Web Vitals',
  require_partition_filter = true
);

CREATE OR REPLACE TABLE `diyapp-prod.telemetry_raw.page_events` (
  event_id STRING NOT NULL,
  session_id STRING NOT NULL,
  user_id STRING,
  page_url STRING,
  event_type STRING,
  event_name STRING,
  element_id STRING,
  metadata JSON,
  device_type STRING,
  browser STRING,
  country_code STRING,
  event_timestamp TIMESTAMP,
  received_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP(),
  _source_file STRING,
  _load_timestamp TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP()
)
PARTITION BY DATE(event_timestamp)
CLUSTER BY session_id, event_type
OPTIONS(
  description = 'Dados brutos de eventos de página',
  require_partition_filter = true
);

CREATE OR REPLACE TABLE `diyapp-prod.telemetry_raw.error_logs` (
  error_id STRING NOT NULL,
  session_id STRING,
  user_id STRING,
  page_url STRING,
  error_type STRING,
  error_message STRING,
  stack_trace STRING,
  severity STRING,
  component STRING,
  browser_info STRING,
  device_info STRING,
  event_timestamp TIMESTAMP,
  received_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP(),
  _source_file STRING,
  _load_timestamp TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP()
)
PARTITION BY DATE(event_timestamp)
CLUSTER BY error_type, severity
OPTIONS(
  description = 'Dados brutos de erros da aplicação',
  require_partition_filter = true
);

CREATE OR REPLACE TABLE `diyapp-prod.telemetry_raw.user_sessions` (
  session_id STRING NOT NULL,
  user_id STRING,
  device_id STRING,
  start_time TIMESTAMP,
  end_time TIMESTAMP,
  page_count INT64,
  duration_seconds INT64,
  country_code STRING,
  browser STRING,
  os STRING,
  screen_resolution STRING,
  is_new_user BOOL,
  event_timestamp TIMESTAMP,
  received_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP(),
  _source_file STRING,
  _load_timestamp TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP()
)
PARTITION BY DATE(start_time)
CLUSTER BY user_id, country_code
OPTIONS(
  description = 'Dados brutos de sessões de usuário',
  require_partition_filter = true
);

-- Políticas de retenção (7 dias para raw, 30 dias para staging, 90 dias para marts)
ALTER TABLE `diyapp-prod.telemetry_raw.web_vitals`
SET OPTIONS (partition_expiration_days = 7);

ALTER TABLE `diyapp-prod.telemetry_staging.*`
SET OPTIONS (partition_expiration_days = 30);

ALTER TABLE `diyapp-prod.telemetry_marts.*`
SET OPTIONS (partition_expiration_days = 90);
```

sources:
  - name: telemetry_raw
    description: "Dados brutos de telemetria da DIYAPP"
    database: diyapp-prod
    schema: telemetry_raw
    tables:
      - name: web_vitals
        description: "Core Web Vitals brutos"
        loaded_at_field: _load_timestamp
        freshness:
          warn_after: {count: 1, period: hour}
          error_after: {count: 2, period: hour}
        columns:
          - name: event_id
            tests:
              - unique
              - not_null
          - name: session_id
            tests:
              - not_null
          - name: metric_name
            tests:
              - accepted_values:
                  values: ['CLS', 'FID', 'LCP', 'FCP', 'TTFB']
          - name: rating
            tests:
              - accepted_values:
                  values: ['good', 'needs-improvement', 'poor']
          
      - name: page_events
        description: "Eventos de página brutos"
        loaded_at_field: _load_timestamp
        freshness:
          warn_after: {count: 1, period: hour}
          error_after: {count: 2, period: hour}
          
      - name: error_logs
        description: "Logs de erro brutos"
        loaded_at_field: _load_timestamp
        freshness:
          warn_after: {count: 30, period: minute}
          error_after: {count: 1, period: hour}
          
      - name: user_sessions
        description: "Sessões de usuário brutas"
        loaded_at_field: _load_timestamp
        freshness:
          warn_after: {count: 1, period: hour}
          error_after: {count: 3, period: hour}
```

          - not_null

          - not_null

          - not_null
      - name: rating

          - not_null

          - not_null

### `dbt/models/staging/stg_web_vitals.sql`

```sql
{{
    config(
        materialized='view',
        schema='telemetry_staging',
        tags=['staging', 'web_vitals']
    )
}}

WITH raw_data AS (
    SELECT
        event_id,
        session_id,
        COALESCE(user_id, 'anonymous') AS user_id,
        page_url,
        metric_name,
        -- Normaliza valores outliers
        CASE 
            WHEN metric_value < 0 THEN 0
            WHEN metric_value > 10000 THEN 10000
            ELSE metric_value
        END AS metric_value,
        rating,
        COALESCE(device_type, 'unknown') AS device_type,
        COALESCE(browser, 'unknown') AS browser,
        COALESCE(country_code, 'unknown') AS country_code,
        TIMESTAMP_TRUNC(event_timestamp, SECOND) AS event_timestamp,
        DATE(event_timestamp) AS event_date,
        received_at
    FROM {{ source('telemetry_raw', 'web_vitals') }}
    WHERE event_timestamp IS NOT NULL
      AND metric_name IS NOT NULL
      AND DATE(event_timestamp) >= DATE_SUB(CURRENT_DATE(), INTERVAL 7 DAY)
)

SELECT
    event_id,
    session_id,
    user_id,
    page_url,
    metric_name,
    metric_value,
    rating,
    device_type,
    browser,
    country_code,
    event_timestamp,
    event_date,
    received_at,
    -- Classificação de performance
    CASE 
        WHEN metric_name = 'LCP' AND metric_value <= 2500 THEN 'good'
        WHEN metric_name = 'LCP' AND metric_value <= 4000 THEN 'needs-improvement'
        WHEN metric_name = 'LCP' AND metric_value > 4000 THEN 'poor'
        WHEN metric_name = 'FID' AND metric_value <= 100 THEN 'good'
        WHEN metric_name = 'FID' AND metric_value <= 300 THEN 'needs-improvement'
        WHEN metric_name = 'FID' AND metric_value > 300 THEN 'poor'
        WHEN metric_name = 'CLS' AND metric_value <= 0.1 THEN 'good'
        WHEN metric_name = 'CLS' AND metric_value <= 0.25 THEN 'needs-improvement'
        WHEN metric_name = 'CLS' AND metric_value > 0.25 THEN 'poor'
        ELSE rating
    END AS performance_rating
FROM raw_data
```

### `dbt/models/staging/stg_error_logs.sql`

```sql
{{
    config(
        materialized='view',
        schema='telemetry_staging',
        tags=['staging', 'error_logs']
    )
}}

WITH raw_data AS (
    SELECT
        error_id,
        session_id,
        COALESCE(user_id, 'anonymous') AS user_id,
        page_url,
        error_type,
        -- Limita tamanho da mensagem de erro
        SUBSTR(error_message, 1, 1000) AS error_message,
        SUBSTR(stack_trace, 1, 5000) AS stack_trace,
        COALESCE(severity, 'error') AS severity,
        COALESCE(component, 'unknown') AS component,
        browser_info,
        device_info,
        TIMESTAMP_TRUNC(event_timestamp, SECOND) AS event_timestamp,
        DATE(event_timestamp) AS event_date,
        received_at
    FROM {{ source('telemetry_raw', 'error_logs') }}
    WHERE event_timestamp IS NOT NULL
      AND error_type IS NOT NULL
      AND DATE(event_timestamp) >= DATE_SUB(CURRENT_DATE(), INTERVAL 7 DAY)
)

SELECT
    error_id,
    session_id,
    user_id,
    page_url,
    error_type,
    error_message,
    stack_trace,
    severity,
    component,
    browser_info,
    device_info,
    event_timestamp,
    event_date,
    received_at,
    -- Categorização de erros
    CASE 
        WHEN error_type LIKE '%Timeout%' THEN 'timeout'
        WHEN error_type LIKE '%Network%' THEN 'network'
        WHEN error_type LIKE '%Syntax%' THEN 'syntax'
        WHEN error_type LIKE '%TypeError%' THEN 'type_error'
        WHEN error_type LIKE '%ReferenceError%' THEN 'reference_error'
        WHEN error_type LIKE '%RangeError%' THEN 'range_error'
        ELSE 'other'
    END AS error_category
FROM raw_data
```

### `dbt/models/marts/mart_product/daily_active_users.sql`

```sql


### [Sessão Paralela: Tech Leader]
```yaml
# DIYAPP Evolution - V12 Core Architecture Specification
# Arquitetura de Microsserviços, Containers, CI/CD e Observabilidade
# Tech Lead: Squad Autônoma de IA

# ============================================================================
# ARQUITETURA DE MICROSSERVIÇOS
# ============================================================================

# 1. ESTRUTURA DE REPOSITÓRIOS
# ----------------------------
# ADR-001: Monorepo com Workspaces vs Multi-repo
# Status: Aceita
# Data: 2024-01-15
# Decisão: Monorepo com workspaces (pnpm/turborepo) para:
# - Compartilhamento de código fácil (tipos, utils, configurações)
# - CI/CD simplificado
# - Refatoração cross-service mais segura
# - Versionamento consistente

# Estrutura do monorepo:
diyapp-v12-core/
├── packages/
│   ├── shared/                    # Código compartilhado
│   │   ├── types/                 # TypeScript types/interfaces
│   │   ├── utils/                 # Utilitários comuns
│   │   ├── config/                # Configurações compartilhadas
│   │   └── schemas/               # Validações Zod/Joi
│   ├── api-gateway/              # Gateway principal
│   ├── auth-service/             # Autenticação/autorização
│   ├── llm-orchestrator/         # Orquestração de modelos LLM
│   ├── workflow-engine/          # Motor de fluxos de trabalho
│   ├── data-pipeline/            # Processamento de dados
│   ├── monitoring-service/       # Coleta de métricas
│   └── notification-service/     # Notificações (WhatsApp, email)
├── apps/
│   └── dashboard/                # Frontend dashboard
├── docker-compose.yml           # Desenvolvimento local
├── turbo.json                   # Turborepo pipeline
├── package.json                 # Root package.json
└── README.md

# ============================================================================
# 2. PADRÕES DE CONTAINERS/DOCKER
# ============================================================================

# ADR-002: Multi-stage Docker builds vs Single-stage
# Status: Aceita
# Data: 2024-01-15
# Decisão: Multi-stage builds para:
# - Imagens menores em produção
# - Segurança (sem ferramentas de build em produção)
# - Cache de dependências otimizado

# Template Dockerfile para serviços Node.js:
# Arquivo: packages/[service-name]/Dockerfile
FROM node:18-alpine AS builder
WORKDIR /app
COPY package.json pnpm-lock.yaml ./
RUN npm install -g pnpm && pnpm install --frozen-lockfile
COPY . .
RUN pnpm run build

FROM node:18-alpine AS production
WORKDIR /app
ENV NODE_ENV=production
COPY --from=builder /app/dist ./dist
COPY --from=builder /app/node_modules ./node_modules
COPY package.json ./
USER node
EXPOSE 3000
CMD ["node", "dist/index.js"]

# Template docker-compose para desenvolvimento:
# Arquivo: docker-compose.yml
version: '3.8'
services:
  postgres:
    image: postgres:15-alpine
    environment:
      POSTGRES_DB: diyapp
      POSTGRES_USER: diyapp
      POSTGRES_PASSWORD: ${DB_PASSWORD}
    volumes:
      - postgres_data:/var/lib/postgresql/data
    ports:
      - "5432:5432"
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD-SHELL", "pg_isready -U diyapp"]
      interval: 10s
      timeout: 5s
      retries: 5

  redis:
    image: redis:7-alpine
    ports:
      - "6379:6379"
    command: redis-server --appendonly yes
    volumes:
      - redis_data:/data

  api-gateway:
    build:
      context: .
      dockerfile: packages/api-gateway/Dockerfile.dev
    ports:
      - "3000:3000"
    environment:
      - NODE_ENV=development
      - DATABASE_URL=postgresql://diyapp:${DB_PASSWORD}@postgres:5432/diyapp
      - REDIS_URL=redis://redis:6379
    depends_on:
      postgres:
        condition: service_healthy
      redis:
        condition: service_started
    volumes:
      - ./packages/api-gateway:/app
      - /app/node_modules

  # Outros serviços seguem padrão similar...

volumes:
  postgres_data:
  redis_data:

# ============================================================================
# 3. PADRÕES DE CÓDIGO E ARQUITETURA
# ============================================================================

# Engineering Standards Document
# Arquivo: ENGINEERING_STANDARDS.md

# 3.1 Estrutura de Serviço (Clean Architecture adaptada)
packages/auth-service/
├── src/
│   ├── domain/                  # Entidades e regras de negócio
│   │   ├── entities/
│   │   │   └── user.entity.ts
│   │   ├── repositories/        # Interfaces de repositório
│   │   │   └── user.repository.ts
│   │   └── use-cases/          # Casos de uso
│   │       └── authenticate-user.use-case.ts
│   ├── application/             # Aplicação (services, DTOs)
│   │   ├── services/
│   │   ├── dtos/
│   │   └── mappers/
│   ├── infrastructure/          # Implementações concretas
│   │   ├── database/
│   │   │   └── prisma/
│   │   ├── http/
│   │   │   └── controllers/
│   │   └── messaging/
│   ├── shared/                  # Utilitários do serviço
│   └── index.ts                 # Ponto de entrada
├── tests/
│   ├── unit/
│   ├── integration/
│   └── e2e/
├── Dockerfile
├── Dockerfile.dev
└── package.json

# 3.2 Padrões de Código TypeScript
# Arquivo: packages/shared/config/typescript/base.json
{
  "compilerOptions": {
    "target": "ES2022",
    "module": "commonjs",
    "lib": ["ES2022"],
    "outDir": "./dist",
    "rootDir": "./src",
    "strict": true,
    "esModuleInterop": true,
    "skipLibCheck": true,
    "forceConsistentCasingInFileNames": true,
    "resolveJsonModule": true,
    "declaration": true,
    "declarationMap": true,
    "sourceMap": true,
    "noUnusedLocals": true,
    "noUnusedParameters": true,
    "noImplicitReturns": true,
    "noFallthroughCasesInSwitch": true,
    "moduleResolution": "node",
    "allowSyntheticDefaultImports": true,
    "experimentalDecorators": true,
    "emitDecoratorMetadata": true
  },
  "exclude": ["node_modules", "dist", "**/*.test.ts", "**/*.spec.ts"]
}

# 3.3 ESLint Config
# Arquivo: packages/shared/config/eslint/base.js
module.exports = {
  parser: '@typescript-eslint/parser',
  plugins: ['@typescript-eslint', 'import', 'prettier'],
  extends: [
    'eslint:recommended',
    'plugin:@typescript-eslint/recommended',

    'prettier'
  ],
  rules: {
    '@typescript-eslint/explicit-function-return-type': 'error',
    '@typescript-eslint/no-explicit-any': 'error',
    '@typescript-eslint/no-unused-vars': ['error', { 'argsIgnorePattern': '^_' }],
    'import/order': ['error', {
      'groups': ['builtin', 'external', 'internal', 'parent', 'sibling', 'index'],
      'newlines-between': 'always',
      'alphabetize': { 'order': 'asc' }
    }],
    'no-console': ['warn', { allow: ['warn', 'error', 'info'] }]
  }
};

{

  "trailingComma": "es5",
  "singleQuote": true,
  "printWidth": 100,
  "tabWidth": 2,
  "useTabs": false,
  "bracketSpacing": true,
  "arrowParens": "avoid"
}

# ============================================================================
# 4. CI/CD PIPELINE
# ============================================================================

# ADR-003: GitHub Actions vs GitLab CI vs Jenkins
# Status: Aceita
# Data: 2024-01-15
# Decisão: GitHub Actions para:
# - Integração nativa com GitHub
# - Marketplace de actions rico
# - Custo zero para open source
# - Suporte a matriz de builds

# Arquivo: .github/workflows/ci-cd.yml
name: CI/CD Pipeline

on:
  push:
    branches: [main, develop]
  pull_request:
    branches: [main]

env:
  REGISTRY: ghcr.io
  IMAGE_NAME: ${{ github.repository }}

jobs:
  # Job 1: Validação de Código
  validate:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v3
      
      - name: Setup Node.js
        uses: actions/setup-node@v3
        with:
          node-version: '18'
          cache: 'pnpm'
          
      - name: Install dependencies
        run: npm install -g pnpm && pnpm install --frozen-lockfile
        
      - name: Type check
        run: pnpm run type-check
        
      - name: Lint
        run: pnpm run lint
        
      - name: Test
        run: pnpm run test
        
      - name: Build
        run: pnpm run build

  # Job 2: Testes de Integração
  integration-tests:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    needs: validate
    services:
      postgres:
        image: postgres:15-alpine
        env:
          POSTGRES_PASSWORD: testpassword
        options: >-
          --health-cmd pg_isready
          --health-interval 10s
          --health-timeout 5s
          --health-retries 5
        ports:
          - 5432:5432
          
      redis:
        image: redis:7-alpine
        options: >-
          --health-cmd "redis-cli ping"
          --health-interval 10s
          --health-timeout 5s
          --health-retries 5
        ports:
          - 6379:6379
          
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v3
      - uses: actions/setup-node@v3
        with:
          node-version: '18'
          
      - run: npm install -g pnpm && pnpm install
      - run: pnpm run test:integration
        env:
          DATABASE_URL: postgresql://postgres:testpassword@localhost:5432/postgres
          REDIS_URL: redis://localhost:6379

  # Job 3: Build e Push de Containers
  build-and-push:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    needs: integration-tests
    if: github.event_name == 'push' && github.ref == 'refs/heads/main'
    
    permissions:
      contents: read
      packages: write
      
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v3
      
      - name: Log in to Container Registry
        uses: docker/login-action@v2
        with:
          registry: ${{ env.REGISTRY }}
          username: ${{ github.actor }}
          password: ${{ secrets.GITHUB_TOKEN }}
          
      - name: Extract metadata
        id: meta
        uses: docker/metadata-action@v4
        with:
          images: ${{ env.REGISTRY }}/${{ env.IMAGE_NAME }}
          tags: |
            type=sha,prefix={{branch}}-
            type=ref,event=branch
            type=ref,event=pr
            type=semver,pattern={{version}}
            type=semver,pattern={{major}}.{{minor}}
            
      - name: Build and push Docker images
        uses: docker/build-push-action@v4
        with:
          context: .
          push: true
          tags: ${{ steps.meta.outputs.tags }}
          labels: ${{ steps.meta.outputs.labels }}
          cache-from: type=gha
          cache-to: type=gha,mode=max

  # Job 4: Deploy para Staging
  deploy-staging:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    needs: build-and-push
    if: github.event_name == 'push' && github.ref == 'refs/heads/develop'
    
    steps:
      - name: Deploy to Staging
        uses: appleboy/ssh-action@v0.1.5
        with:
          host: ${{ secrets.STAGING_HOST }}
          username: ${{ secrets.STAGING_USER }}
          key: ${{ secrets.STAGING_SSH_KEY }}
          script: |
            cd /opt/diyapp-staging
            docker-compose pull
            docker-compose up -d --remove-orphans
            docker system prune -f

  # Job 5: Deploy para Produção (manual approval)
  deploy-production:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    needs: build-and-push
    if: github.event_name == 'push' && github.ref == 'refs/heads/main'
    
    environment: production
    permissions:
      deployments: write
      
    steps:
      - name: Wait for manual approval
        uses: trstringer/manual-approval@v1
        with:
          secret: ${{ github.token }}
          approvers: ${{ secrets.PRODUCTION_APPROVERS }}
          minimum-approvals: 2
          
      - name: Deploy to Production
        uses: appleboy/ssh-action@v0.1.5
        with:
          host: ${{ secrets.PRODUCTION_HOST }}
          username: ${{ secrets.PRODUCTION_USER }}
          key: ${{ secrets.PRODUCTION_SSH_KEY }}
          script: |
            cd /opt/diyapp-production
            docker-compose pull
            docker-compose up -d --remove-orphans
            docker system prune -f
            
      - name: Create deployment status
        uses: actions/github-script@v6
        with:
          script: |
            github.rest.repos.createDeployment({
              owner: context.repo.owner,
              repo: context.repo.repo,
              ref: context.sha,
              environment: 'production',
              auto_merge: false,
              required_contexts: []
            })

# ============================================================================
# 5. OBSERVABILIDADE (Logs, Traces, Métricas)
# ============================================================================

# ADR-004: OpenTelemetry vs Vendor-specific
# Status: Aceita
# Data: 2024-01-15
# Decisão: OpenTelemetry para:
# - Vendor-agnostic
# - Padrão CNCF
# - Instrumentação automática
# - Exportadores múltiplos

# 5.1 Configuração OpenTelemetry
# Arquivo: packages/shared/observability/otel-config.ts
import { NodeSDK } from '@opentelemetry/sdk-node';
import { getNodeAutoInstrumentations } from '@opentelemetry/auto-instrumentations-node';
import { OTLPTraceExporter } from '@opentelemetry/exporter-trace-otlp-http';
import { OTLPMetricExporter } from '@opentelemetry/exporter-metrics-otlp-http';
import { PeriodicExportingMetricReader } from '@opentelemetry/sdk-metrics';
import { Resource } from '@opentelemetry/resources';
import { SemanticResourceAttributes } from '@opentelemetry/semantic-conventions';
import { WinstonInstrumentation } from '@opentelemetry/instrumentation-winston';
import { PgInstrumentation } from '@opentelemetry/instrumentation-pg';
import { RedisInstrumentation } from '@opentelemetry/instrumentation-redis';

export function initializeTelemetry(serviceName: string) {
  const sdk = new NodeSDK({
    resource: new Resource({
      [SemanticResourceAttributes.SERVICE_NAME]: serviceName,
      [SemanticResourceAttributes.SERVICE_VERSION]: process.env.npm_package_version || '1.0.0',
      'deployment.environment': process.env.NODE_ENV || 'development',
    }),
    traceExporter: new OTLPTraceExporter({
      url: process.env.OTEL_EXPORTER_OTLP_ENDPOINT || 'http://localhost:4318/v1/traces',
    }),
    metricReader: new PeriodicExportingMetricReader({
      exporter: new OTLPMetricExporter({
        url: process.env.OTEL_EXPORTER_OTLP_ENDPOINT || 'http://localhost:4318/v1/metrics',
      }),
      exportIntervalMillis: 60000, // 1 minuto
    }),
    instrumentations: [
      getNodeAutoInstrumentations({
        '@opentelemetry/instrumentation-http': {
          ignoreIncomingPaths: ['/health', '/metrics'],
        },
      }),
      new WinstonInstrumentation(),
      new PgInstrumentation(),
      new RedisInstrumentation(),
    ],
  });

  sdk.start();
  return sdk;
}

  level: process.env.LOG_LEVEL || 'info',
  format

# DIYAPP Evolution - V12 Core - Serviços Refatorados

## Estrutura do Projeto

```

├── src/
│   ├── api-gateway/
│   ├── auth-service/

│   └── index.js
