**.env.example**
```env
# Server
NODE_ENV=development
PORT=3000
API_GATEWAY_PORT=8080
AUTH_SERVICE_PORT=3001
TASK_SERVICE_PORT=3002

# Database
POSTGRES_HOST=localhost
POSTGRES_PORT=5432
POSTGRES_DB=diyapp_v12
POSTGRES_USER=diyapp_user
POSTGRES_PASSWORD=secure_password_here

# Redis
REDIS_HOST=localhost
REDIS_PORT=6379
REDIS_PASSWORD=

# JWT
JWT_SECRET=your_super_secret_jwt_key_change_in_production
JWT_EXPIRES_IN=24h
REFRESH_TOKEN_SECRET=your_refresh_token_secret
REFRESH_TOKEN_EXPIRES_IN=7d

# OAuth2 (example for Google)
GOOGLE_CLIENT_ID=your_google_client_id
GOOGLE_CLIENT_SECRET=your_google_client_secret
GOOGLE_CALLBACK_URL=http://localhost:8080/auth/google/callback

# Circuit Breaker
CIRCUIT_BREAKER_TIMEOUT=5000
CIRCUIT_BREAKER_THRESHOLD=5
CIRCUIT_BREAKER_RESET_TIMEOUT=30000

# Rate Limiting
RATE_LIMIT_WINDOW_MS=900000
RATE_LIMIT_MAX_REQUESTS=100

# External Services (example)
EXTERNAL_API_BASE_URL=https://api.example.com
EXTERNAL_API_TIMEOUT=10000
```

## 2. API Gateway com Resiliência

**src/api-gateway/index.js**
```javascript
const express = require('express');
const helmet = require('helmet');
const cors = require('cors');
const rateLimit = require('express-rate-limit');
const compression = require('compression');
const winston = require('winston');
const CircuitBreaker = require('circuit-breaker-js');
const axios = require('axios');
const NodeCache = require('node-cache');

// Logger configuration
const logger = winston.createLogger({
  level: process.env.NODE_ENV === 'production' ? 'info' : 'debug',
  format: winston.format.combine(
    winston.format.timestamp(),
    winston.format.json()
  ),
  transports: [
    new winston.transports.File({ filename: 'logs/error.log', level: 'error' }),
    new winston.transports.File({ filename: 'logs/combined.log' }),
    new winston.transports.Console({
      format: winston.format.combine(
        winston.format.colorize(),
        winston.format.simple()
      )
    })
  ]
});

// Cache configuration (5 minutes TTL)
const cache = new NodeCache({ stdTTL: 300, checkperiod: 60 });

// Circuit breaker configuration
const createCircuitBreaker = (serviceName) => {
  return new CircuitBreaker({
    timeoutDuration: parseInt(process.env.CIRCUIT_BREAKER_TIMEOUT) || 5000,
    errorThreshold: parseInt(process.env.CIRCUIT_BREAKER_THRESHOLD) || 5,
    resetTimeout: parseInt(process.env.CIRCUIT_BREAKER_RESET_TIMEOUT) || 30000,
    onStateChange: (from, to) => {
      logger.warn(`Circuit breaker for ${serviceName} changed from ${from} to ${to}`);
    }
  });
};

// Service configurations
const services = {
  auth: {
    baseUrl: `http://localhost:${process.env.AUTH_SERVICE_PORT || 3001}`,
    circuitBreaker: createCircuitBreaker('auth-service'),
    timeout: 10000
  },
  tasks: {
    baseUrl: `http://localhost:${process.env.TASK_SERVICE_PORT || 3002}`,
    circuitBreaker: createCircuitBreaker('task-service'),
    timeout: 15000
  }
};

// HTTP client with retry logic
const createHttpClient = (serviceConfig) => {
  const client = axios.create({
    baseURL: serviceConfig.baseUrl,
    timeout: serviceConfig.timeout,
    headers: {
      'Content-Type': 'application/json',
      'User-Agent': 'DIYAPP-API-Gateway/12.0'
    }
  });

  // Request interceptor for logging
  client.interceptors.request.use(
    (config) => {
      const correlationId = config.headers['x-correlation-id'] || 
        config.headers['X-Correlation-ID'] || 
        `corr-${Date.now()}-${Math.random().toString(36).substr(2, 9)}`;
      
      config.headers['x-correlation-id'] = correlationId;
      config.metadata = { startTime: Date.now(), correlationId };
      
      logger.info({
        correlationId,
        service: config.baseURL,
        method: config.method.toUpperCase(),
        url: config.url,
        message: 'Outgoing request'
      });
      
      return config;
    },
    (error) => {
      logger.error({
        message: 'Request interceptor error',
        error: error.message
      });
      return Promise.reject(error);
    }
  );

  // Response interceptor with retry logic
  client.interceptors.response.use(
    (response) => {
      const duration = Date.now() - response.config.metadata.startTime;
      logger.info({
        correlationId: response.config.metadata.correlationId,
        service: response.config.baseURL,
        method: response.config.method.toUpperCase(),
        url: response.config.url,
        status: response.status,
        duration,
        message: 'Request completed'
      });
      return response;
    },
    async (error) => {
      const config = error.config;
      
      // Don't retry on 4xx errors (except 429)
      if (error.response && error.response.status < 500 && error.response.status !== 429) {
        return Promise.reject(error);
      }
      
      // Implement retry with exponential backoff
      config.retryCount = config.retryCount || 0;
      const maxRetries = 3;
      
      if (config.retryCount >= maxRetries) {
        logger.error({
          correlationId: config.metadata?.correlationId,
          service: config.baseURL,
          method: config.method.toUpperCase(),
          url: config.url,
          retryCount: config.retryCount,
          error: error.message,
          message: 'Max retries exceeded'
        });
        return Promise.reject(error);
      }
      
      config.retryCount += 1;
      const delay = Math.pow(2, config.retryCount) * 1000 + Math.random() * 1000; // Exponential backoff with jitter
      
      logger.warn({
        correlationId: config.metadata?.correlationId,
        service: config.baseURL,
        method: config.method.toUpperCase(),
        url: config.url,
        retryCount: config.retryCount,
        delay,
        error: error.message,
        message: 'Retrying request'
      });
      
      await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, delay));
      return client(config);
    }
  );

  return client;
};

// Create HTTP clients for each service
Object.keys(services).forEach(serviceName => {
  services[serviceName].client = createHttpClient(services[serviceName]);
});

// Proxy middleware with circuit breaker and caching
const createProxyMiddleware = (serviceName, pathPrefix = '') => {
  return async (req, res, next) => {
    const service = services[serviceName];
    const correlationId = req.headers['x-correlation-id'] || 
      `corr-${Date.now()}-${Math.random().toString(36).substr(2, 9)}`;
    
    // Add correlation ID to response headers
    res.setHeader('x-correlation-id', correlationId);
    
    // Log incoming request
    logger.info({
      correlationId,
      service: serviceName,
      method: req.method,
      url: req.originalUrl,
      ip: req.ip,
      userAgent: req.get('User-Agent'),
      message: 'Incoming request'
    });
    
    // Check cache for GET requests
    if (req.method === 'GET') {
      const cacheKey = `${serviceName}:${req.originalUrl}`;
      const cachedResponse = cache.get(cacheKey);
      
      if (cachedResponse) {
        logger.debug({
          correlationId,
          cacheKey,
          message: 'Cache hit'
        });
        
        // Add cache headers
        res.setHeader('x-cache', 'HIT');
        res.setHeader('x-cache-ttl', cache.getTtl(cacheKey) - Date.now());
        
        return res.json(cachedResponse);
      }
    }
    
    // Prepare request options
    const requestOptions = {
      method: req.method,
      url: `${pathPrefix}${req.path}`,
      headers: {
        ...req.headers,
        'x-correlation-id': correlationId,
        'x-forwarded-for': req.ip,
        'x-original-url': req.originalUrl
      },
      params: req.query,
      data: req.body
    };
    
    // Remove hop-by-hop headers
    const hopByHopHeaders = [
      'connection', 'keep-alive', 'proxy-authenticate',
      'proxy-authorization', 'te', 'trailers', 'transfer-encoding', 'upgrade'
    ];
    
    hopByHopHeaders.forEach(header => {
      delete requestOptions.headers[header];
    });
    
    // Execute request with circuit breaker
    try {
      const result = await new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
        service.circuitBreaker.run(async (success, fail) => {
          try {
            const response = await service.client(requestOptions);
            
            // Cache successful GET responses
            if (req.method === 'GET' && response.status === 200) {
              const cacheKey = `${serviceName}:${req.originalUrl}`;
              cache.set(cacheKey, response.data);
              
              // Add cache headers
              res.setHeader('x-cache', 'MISS');
              res.setHeader('x-cache-ttl', 300);
            }
            
            success(response);
          } catch (error) {
            fail(error);
          }
        }, (error) => {
          reject(error);
        });
      });
      
      // Forward response
      res.status(result.status)
         .set(result.headers)
         .send(result.data);
      
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error({
        correlationId,
        service: serviceName,
        method: req.method,
        url: req.originalUrl,
        error: error.message,
        stack: process.env.NODE_ENV === 'development' ? error.stack : undefined,
        message: 'Proxy request failed'
      });
      
      // Circuit breaker fallback
      if (service.circuitBreaker.isOpen()) {
        res.status(503).json({
          error: 'Service temporarily unavailable',
          message: `The ${serviceName} service is currently unavailable. Please try again later.`,
          correlationId,
          timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
        });
      } else if (error.response) {
        // Forward error from service
        res.status(error.response.status)
           .set(error.response.headers)
           .json(error.response.data);
      } else if (error.code === 'ECONNREFUSED') {
        res.status(502).json({
          error: 'Bad Gateway',
          message: `Unable to connect to ${serviceName} service`,
          correlationId,
          timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
        });
      } else if (error.code === 'ETIMEDOUT') {
        res.status(504).json({
          error: 'Gateway Timeout',
          message: `The ${serviceName} service took too long to respond`,
          correlationId,
          timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
        });
      } else {
        res.status(500).json({
          error: 'Internal Server Error',
          message: 'An unexpected error occurred',
          correlationId,
          timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
        });
      }
    }
  };
};

// Create Express app
const app = express();

// Security middleware
app.use(helmet({
  contentSecurityPolicy: {
    directives: {
      defaultSrc: ["'self'"],
      styleSrc: ["'self'", "'unsafe-inline'"],
      scriptSrc: ["'self'"],
      imgSrc: ["'self'", "data:", "https:"]
    }
  }
}));

// CORS configuration
app.use(cors({
  origin: process.env.CORS_ORIGIN || 'http://localhost:3000',
  credentials: true,
  methods: ['GET', 'POST', 'PUT', 'DELETE', 'PATCH', 'OPTIONS'],
  allowedHeaders: ['Content-Type', 'Authorization', 'x-correlation-id']
}));

// Rate limiting
const limiter = rateLimit({
  windowMs: parseInt(process.env.RATE_LIMIT_WINDOW_MS) || 15 * 60 * 1000,
  max: parseInt(process.env.RATE_LIMIT_MAX_REQUESTS) || 100,
  message: {
    error: 'Too many requests',
    message: 'Please try again later.'
  },
  standardHeaders: true,
  legacyHeaders: false,
  keyGenerator: (req) => req.ip,
  skip: (req) => req.ip === '127.0.0.1' // Skip localhost in development
});

app.use(limiter);

// Body parsing
app.use(express.json({ limit: '10mb' }));
app.use(express.urlencoded({ extended: true, limit: '10mb' }));

// Compression
app.use(compression());

// Request logging middleware
app.use((req, res, next) => {
  const correlationId = req.headers['x-correlation-id'] || 
    `corr-${Date.now()}-${Math.random().toString(36).substr(2, 9)}`;
  
  req.correlationId = correlationId;
  res.setHeader('x-correlation-id', correlationId);
  
  // Log request start
  logger.info({
    correlationId,
    method: req.method,
    url: req.originalUrl,
    ip: req.ip,
    userAgent: req.get('User-Agent'),
    message: 'Request started'
  });
  
  // Log response completion
  const originalEnd = res.end;
  res.end = function(chunk, encoding) {
    const duration = Date.now() - req._startTime || Date.now();
    
    logger.info({
      correlationId,
      method: req.method,
      url: req.originalUrl,
      status: res.statusCode,
      duration,
      message: 'Request completed'
    });
    
    originalEnd.call(this, chunk, encoding);
  };
  
  req._startTime = Date.now();
  next();
});

// Health check endpoint
app.get('/health', (req, res) => {
  const health = {
    status: 'healthy',
    timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
    uptime: process.uptime(),
    services: {}
  };
  
  // Check service health
  Object.keys(services).forEach(async (serviceName) => {
    const service = services[serviceName];
    try {
      const response = await service.client.get('/health', { timeout: 5000 });
      health.services[serviceName] = {
        status: 'healthy',
        latency: response.duration
      };
    } catch (error) {
      health.services[serviceName] = {
        status: 'unhealthy',
        error: error.message
      };
    }
  });
  
  res.json(health);
});

// Metrics endpoint
app.get('/metrics', (req, res) => {
  const metrics = {
    timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
    cache: {
      stats: cache.get

### [Sessão Paralela: Frontend]

```typescript
// src/types/index.ts
export interface User {
  id: string
  name: string
  email: string
  role: 'admin' | 'user' | 'viewer'
  avatar?: string
  lastActive: string
}

export interface DashboardMetric {
  id: string
  title: string
  value: number | string
  change: number
  trend: 'up' | 'down' | 'stable'
  format?: 'number' | 'percent' | 'currency'
  icon: string
}

export interface Notification {
  id: string
  type: 'info' | 'success' | 'warning' | 'error'
  title: string
  message: string
  timestamp: string
  read: boolean
  action?: {
    label: string
    onClick: () => void
  }
}

export interface WebSocketMessage {
  type: 'notification' | 'metric_update' | 'user_activity' | 'system_alert'
  payload: any
  timestamp: string
}

export interface AppState {
  user: User | null
  notifications: Notification[]
  metrics: DashboardMetric[]
  sidebarCollapsed: boolean
  theme: 'light' | 'dark'
  isLoading: boolean
  error: string | null
}
```

```typescript
// src/stores/useAppStore.ts
import { create } from 'zustand'
import { persist } from 'zustand/middleware'
import { AppState, User, Notification, DashboardMetric } from '@/types'

interface AppStore extends AppState {
  setUser: (user: User | null) => void
  addNotification: (notification: Omit<Notification, 'id' | 'timestamp' | 'read'>) => void
  markNotificationAsRead: (id: string) => void
  clearNotifications: () => void
  updateMetrics: (metrics: DashboardMetric[]) => void
  toggleSidebar: () => void
  toggleTheme: () => void
  setLoading: (isLoading: boolean) => void
  setError: (error: string | null) => void
}

export const useAppStore = create<AppStore>()(
  persist(
    (set, get) => ({
      user: null,
      notifications: [],
      metrics: [],
      sidebarCollapsed: false,
      theme: 'light',
      isLoading: false,
      error: null,

      setUser: (user) => set({ user }),

      addNotification: (notification) =>
        set((state) => ({
          notifications: [
            {
              ...notification,
              id: Date.now().toString(),
              timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
              read: false,
            },
            ...state.notifications,
          ].slice(0, 50), // Keep last 50 notifications
        })),

      markNotificationAsRead: (id) =>
        set((state) => ({
          notifications: state.notifications.map((n) =>
            n.id === id ? { ...n, read: true } : n
          ),
        })),

      clearNotifications: () => set({ notifications: [] }),

      updateMetrics: (metrics) => set({ metrics }),

      toggleSidebar: () =>
        set((state) => ({ sidebarCollapsed: !state.sidebarCollapsed })),

      toggleTheme: () =>
        set((state) => ({ theme: state.theme === 'light' ? 'dark' : 'light' })),

      setLoading: (isLoading) => set({ isLoading }),

      setError: (error) => set({ error }),
    }),
    {
      name: 'diyapp-storage',
      partialize: (state) => ({
        user: state.user,
        theme: state.theme,
        sidebarCollapsed: state.sidebarCollapsed,
      }),
    }
  )
)
```

```typescript
// src/hooks/useWebSocket.ts
import { useEffect, useRef, useCallback } from 'react'
import { io, Socket } from 'socket.io-client'
import { useAppStore } from '@/stores/useAppStore'
import { WebSocketMessage } from '@/types'

const WS_URL = import.meta.env.VITE_WS_URL || 'ws://localhost:3001'

export const useWebSocket = () => {
  const socketRef = useRef<Socket | null>(null)
  const { addNotification, updateMetrics, setError } = useAppStore()

  const connect = useCallback(() => {
    if (socketRef.current?.connected) return

    socketRef.current = io(WS_URL, {
      transports: ['websocket'],
      reconnection: true,
      reconnectionAttempts: 5,
      reconnectionDelay: 1000,
    })

    socketRef.current.on('connect', () => {
      console.log('WebSocket connected')
      setError(null)
    })

    socketRef.current.on('message', (message: WebSocketMessage) => {
      switch (message.type) {
        case 'notification':
          addNotification({
            type: message.payload.type,
            title: message.payload.title,
            message: message.payload.message,
          })
          break
        case 'metric_update':
          updateMetrics(message.payload)
          break
        case 'system_alert':
          setError(message.payload.message)
          break
      }
    })

    socketRef.current.on('disconnect', () => {
      console.log('WebSocket disconnected')
    })

    socketRef.current.on('connect_error', (error) => {
      console.error('WebSocket connection error:', error)
      setError('Connection lost. Attempting to reconnect...')
    })
  }, [addNotification, updateMetrics, setError])

  const disconnect = useCallback(() => {
    if (socketRef.current) {
      socketRef.current.disconnect()
      socketRef.current = null
    }
  }, [])

  const sendMessage = useCallback((type: string, payload: any) => {
    if (socketRef.current?.connected) {
      socketRef.current.emit('message', { type, payload })
    }
  }, [])

  useEffect(() => {
    connect()

    return () => {
      disconnect()
    }
  }, [connect, disconnect])

  return { sendMessage, isConnected: socketRef.current?.connected || false }
}
```

```typescript
// src/components/Layout/AppLayout.tsx
import React, { Suspense } from 'react'
import { Outlet } from 'react-router-dom'
import { Sidebar } from './Sidebar'
import { Header } from './Header'
import { LoadingSpinner } from '@/components/UI/LoadingSpinner'
import { ErrorBoundary } from '@/components/UI/ErrorBoundary'
import { useAppStore } from '@/stores/useAppStore'

export const AppLayout: React.FC = () => {
  const { sidebarCollapsed, theme } = useAppStore()

  React.useEffect(() => {
    document.documentElement.classList.toggle('dark', theme === 'dark')
  }, [theme])

  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen bg-surface-light dark:bg-surface-dark transition-colors duration-200">
      <Header />
      <div className="flex">
        <Sidebar />
        <main
          className={`flex-1 transition-all duration-200 ${
            sidebarCollapsed ? 'ml-16' : 'ml-64'
          } p-6`}
        >
          <ErrorBoundary>
            <Suspense fallback={<LoadingSpinner fullScreen />}>
              <Outlet />
            </Suspense>
          </ErrorBoundary>
        </main>
      </div>
    </div>
  )
}
```

```typescript
// src/components/Layout/Sidebar.tsx
import React from 'react'
import { NavLink } from 'react-router-dom'
import { useAppStore } from '@/stores/useAppStore'
import {
  HomeIcon,
  ChartBarIcon,
  UsersIcon,
  CogIcon,
  BellIcon,
  DocumentTextIcon,
  ArrowLeftIcon,
  ArrowRightIcon,
} from '@heroicons/react/24/outline'

const navItems = [
  { path: '/', label: 'Dashboard', icon: HomeIcon },
  { path: '/analytics', label: 'Analytics', icon: ChartBarIcon },
  { path: '/users', label: 'Users', icon: UsersIcon },
  { path: '/documents', label: 'Documents', icon: DocumentTextIcon },
  { path: '/notifications', label: 'Notifications', icon: BellIcon },
  { path: '/settings', label: 'Settings', icon: CogIcon },
]

export const Sidebar: React.FC = () => {
  const { sidebarCollapsed, toggleSidebar } = useAppStore()

  return (
    <aside
      className={`fixed left-0 top-0 h-screen bg-white dark:bg-gray-900 border-r border-gray-200 dark:border-gray-800 transition-all duration-200 z-40 ${
        sidebarCollapsed ? 'w-16' : 'w-64'
      }`}
    >
      <div className="flex flex-col h-full">
        <div className="p-4 border-b border-gray-200 dark:border-gray-800">
          <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
            {!sidebarCollapsed && (
              <h1 className="text-xl font-bold text-gray-900 dark:text-white">
                DIYAPP V12
              </h1>
            )}
            <button
              onClick={toggleSidebar}
              className="p-2 rounded-lg hover:bg-gray-100 dark:hover:bg-gray-800 transition-colors"
              aria-label={sidebarCollapsed ? 'Expand sidebar' : 'Collapse sidebar'}
            >
              {sidebarCollapsed ? (
                <ArrowRightIcon className="w-5 h-5 text-gray-600 dark:text-gray-400" />
              ) : (
                <ArrowLeftIcon className="w-5 h-5 text-gray-600 dark:text-gray-400" />
              )}
            </button>
          </div>
        </div>

        <nav className="flex-1 p-4 space-y-2">
          {navItems.map((item) => (
            <NavLink
              key={item.path}
              to={item.path}
              className={({ isActive }) =>
                `flex items-center p-3 rounded-lg transition-colors ${
                  isActive
                    ? 'bg-primary-100 dark:bg-primary-900 text-primary-700 dark:text-primary-300'
                    : 'text-gray-700 dark:text-gray-300 hover:bg-gray-100 dark:hover:bg-gray-800'
                } ${sidebarCollapsed ? 'justify-center' : ''}`
              }
            >
              <item.icon className="w-5 h-5" />
              {!sidebarCollapsed && (
                <span className="ml-3 font-medium">{item.label}</span>
              )}
            </NavLink>
          ))}
        </nav>

        <div className="p-4 border-t border-gray-200 dark:border-gray-800">
          <div className={`flex items-center ${sidebarCollapsed ? 'justify-center' : ''}`}>
            <div className="w-8 h-8 rounded-full bg-primary-500 flex items-center justify-center text-white font-bold">
              U
            </div>
            {!sidebarCollapsed && (
              <div className="ml-3">
                <p className="text-sm font-medium text-gray-900 dark:text-white">
                  User Name
                </p>
                <p className="text-xs text-gray-500 dark:text-gray-400">Admin</p>
              </div>
            )}
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    </aside>
  )
}
```

## 1. Configuração do Data Warehouse (BigQuery)

### `scripts/setup_warehouse.sql`

```sql
-- Criar dataset para dados brutos
CREATE SCHEMA IF NOT EXISTS `diyapp_telemetry.raw`
OPTIONS(
  description = 'Dados brutos de telemetria da DIYAPP V12',
  location = 'us-central1',
  default_table_expiration_days = 90
);

-- Criar dataset para dados processados
CREATE SCHEMA IF NOT EXISTS `diyapp_telemetry.staging`
OPTIONS(
  description = 'Dados de staging da DIYAPP V12',
  location = 'us-central1',
  default_table_expiration_days = 30
);

-- Criar dataset para dados de consumo
CREATE SCHEMA IF NOT EXISTS `diyapp_telemetry.marts`
OPTIONS(
  description = 'Dados de consumo da DIYAPP V12',
  location = 'us-central1',
  default_table_expiration_days = 365
);

-- Tabelas raw
CREATE OR REPLACE TABLE `diyapp_telemetry.raw.web_vitals` (
  event_id STRING,
  session_id STRING,
  user_id STRING,
  page_url STRING,
  metric_name STRING,
  metric_value FLOAT64,
  rating STRING,
  device_type STRING,
  browser STRING,
  country_code STRING,
  event_timestamp TIMESTAMP,
  ingestion_timestamp TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP()
)
PARTITION BY DATE(event_timestamp)
CLUSTER BY session_id, metric_name
OPTIONS(
  description = 'Dados brutos de Core Web Vitals'
);

CREATE OR REPLACE TABLE `diyapp_telemetry.raw.user_events` (
  event_id STRING,
  session_id STRING,
  user_id STRING,
  event_type STRING,
  event_name STRING,
  feature_name STRING,
  element_id STRING,
  page_url STRING,
  referrer_url STRING,
  utm_source STRING,
  utm_medium STRING,
  utm_campaign STRING,
  device_info JSON,
  geo_info JSON,
  event_properties JSON,
  event_timestamp TIMESTAMP,
  ingestion_timestamp TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP()
)
PARTITION BY DATE(event_timestamp)
CLUSTER BY session_id, event_type, feature_name
OPTIONS(
  description = 'Dados brutos de eventos de usuário'
);

CREATE OR REPLACE TABLE `diyapp_telemetry.raw.error_logs` (
  error_id STRING,
  session_id STRING,
  user_id STRING,
  error_type STRING,
  error_message STRING,
  stack_trace STRING,
  component_name STRING,
  feature_name STRING,
  page_url STRING,
  http_status_code INT64,
  request_id STRING,
  device_info JSON,
  browser_info JSON,
  error_context JSON,
  event_timestamp TIMESTAMP,
  ingestion_timestamp TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP()
)
PARTITION BY DATE(event_timestamp)
CLUSTER BY error_type, component_name
OPTIONS(
  description = 'Dados brutos de logs de erro'
);

CREATE OR REPLACE TABLE `diyapp_telemetry.raw.performance_metrics` (
  metric_id STRING,
  session_id STRING,
  user_id STRING,
  metric_type STRING,
  metric_name STRING,
  metric_value FLOAT64,
  unit STRING,
  component_name STRING,
  operation_name STRING,
  duration_ms FLOAT64,
  success BOOL,
  tags JSON,
  metadata JSON,
  event_timestamp TIMESTAMP,
  ingestion_timestamp TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP()
)
PARTITION BY DATE(event_timestamp)
CLUSTER BY metric_type, component_name
OPTIONS(
  description = 'Dados brutos de métricas de performance'
);
```

snapshot-paths: ["snapshots"]

  - "target"
  - "dbt_packages"

models:
  diyapp_telemetry:
    materialized: table
    staging:
      materialized: view
      +schema: staging
    marts:
      materialized: table
      +schema: marts
      product:
        materialized: table
        +tags: ["product", "pm"]
      ai:
        materialized: table
        +tags: ["ai", "llm"]
      ops:
        materialized: table
        +tags: ["ops", "sre"]

seeds:
  diyapp_telemetry:
    +schema: raw
    country_codes:
      +column_types:
        country_code: varchar(2)
        country_name: varchar(100)
    device_types:
      +column_types:
        device_type: varchar(50)
        device_category: varchar(50)

```yaml
version: 2

sources:
  - name: raw
    database: diyapp_telemetry
    schema: raw
    tables:
      - name: web_vitals
        description: "Dados brutos de Core Web Vitals"
        loaded_at_field: ingestion_timestamp
        freshness:
          warn_after: {count: 1, period: hour}
          error_after: {count: 2, period: hour}
        
      - name: user_events
        description: "Dados brutos de eventos de usuário"
        loaded_at_field: ingestion_timestamp
        freshness:
          warn_after: {count: 1, period: hour}
          error_after: {count: 2, period: hour}
        
      - name: error_logs
        description: "Dados brutos de logs de erro"
        loaded_at_field: ingestion_timestamp
        freshness:
          warn_after: {count: 1, period: hour}
          error_after: {count: 2, period: hour}
        
      - name: performance_metrics
        description: "Dados brutos de métricas de performance"
        loaded_at_field: ingestion_timestamp
        freshness:
          warn_after: {count: 1, period: hour}
          error_after: {count: 2, period: hour}
```

models:
  - name: stg_web_vitals

          - not_null

          - not_null

        tests:

          - not_null

        description: "ID da sessão do usuário"
        tests:
          - not_null
      
      - name: user_id
        description: "ID do usuário (anonimizado)"
      
      - name: event_type
        description: "Tipo de evento (click, pageview, etc)"
        tests:
          - not_null
      
      - name: feature_name
        description: "Nome da feature relacionada"
      
      - name: page_url_path
        description: "Caminho da URL (sem domínio)"
      
      - name: utm_source
        description: "UTM source"
      
      - name: device_category
        description: "Categoria do dispositivo (mobile, desktop, tablet)"
        tests:
          - accepted_values:
              values: ['mobile', 'desktop', 'tablet', 'unknown']

        description: "Data do evento"

### `dbt/models/staging/stg_web_vitals.sql`

```sql
{{
    config(
        materialized='view',
        schema='staging'
    )
}}

WITH raw_data AS (
    SELECT
        event_id,
        session_id,
        -- Anonimizar user_id mantendo consistência
        MD5(user_id) as user_id,
        page_url,
        metric_name,
        metric_value,
        rating,
        -- Padronizar device_type
        CASE 
            WHEN LOWER(device_type) LIKE '%mobile%' THEN 'mobile'
            WHEN LOWER(device_type) LIKE '%tablet%' THEN 'tablet'
            WHEN LOWER(device_type) LIKE '%desktop%' THEN 'desktop'
            ELSE 'unknown'
        END as device_type,
        -- Extrair navegador principal
        REGEXP_EXTRACT(browser, r'^([^/]+)') as browser,
        -- Validar country_code
        CASE 
            WHEN LENGTH(country_code) = 2 AND country_code REGEXP '^[A-Z]{2}$' 
            THEN UPPER(country_code)
            ELSE 'XX'
        END as country_code,
        TIMESTAMP(event_timestamp) as event_timestamp,
        DATE(event_timestamp) as event_date
    FROM {{ source('raw', 'web_vitals') }}
    WHERE event_timestamp IS NOT NULL
      AND metric_name IS NOT NULL
      AND metric_value IS NOT NULL
      AND session_id IS NOT NULL
)

SELECT
    event_id,
    session_id,
    user_id,
    page_url,
    metric_name,
    metric_value,
    rating,
    device_type,
    browser,
    country_code,
    event_timestamp,
    event_date
FROM raw_data
```

### `dbt/models/staging/stg_user_events.sql`

```sql
{{
    config(
        materialized='view',
        schema='staging'
    )
}}

WITH raw_data AS (
    SELECT
        event_id,
        session_id,
        -- Anonimizar user_id
        MD5(user_id) as user_id,
        event_type,
        event_name,
        feature_name,
        -- Extrair caminho da URL
        REGEXP_EXTRACT(page_url, r'://[^/]+(/[^?#]*)') as page_url_path,
        -- Parsear UTM parameters
        utm_source,
        utm_medium,
        utm_campaign,
        -- Extrair device category do JSON
        JSON_VALUE(device_info, '$.category') as device_category,
        -- Extrair country do JSON
        JSON_VALUE(geo_info, '$.country_code') as country_code,
        -- Extrair screen resolution
        JSON_VALUE(device_info, '$.screen_resolution') as screen_resolution,
        TIMESTAMP(event_timestamp) as event_timestamp,
        DATE(event_timestamp) as event_date
    FROM {{ source('raw', 'user_events') }}
    WHERE event_timestamp IS NOT NULL
      AND event_type IS NOT NULL
      AND session_id IS NOT NULL
)

SELECT
    event_id,
    session_id,
    user_id,
    event_type,
    event_name,
    feature_name,
    page_url_path,
    utm_source,
    utm_medium,
    utm_campaign,
    COALESCE(device_category, 'unknown') as device_category,
    COALESCE(country_code, 'XX') as country_code,
    screen_resolution,
    event_timestamp,
    event_date
FROM raw_data
```

### `dbt/models/staging/stg_error_logs.sql`

```sql
{{
    config(
        materialized='view',
        schema='staging'
    )
}}

WITH raw_data AS (
    SELECT
        error_id,
        session_id,
        -- Anonimizar user_id
        MD5(user_id) as user_id,
        error_type,
        -- Limitar tamanho da mensagem de erro
        SUBSTR(error_message, 1, 500) as error_message,
        -- Mascarar dados sensíveis no stack trace
        REGEXP_REPLACE(
            stack_trace, 
            r'(password|token|key|secret)=[^&\s]+', 
            '$1=***'
        ) as stack_trace_masked,
        component_name,
        feature_name,
        page_url,
        http_status_code,
        request_id,
        -- Extrair browser info
        JSON_VALUE(browser_info, '$.name') as browser_name,
        JSON_VALUE(browser_info, '$.version') as browser_version,
        TIMESTAMP(event_timestamp) as event_timestamp,
        DATE(event_timestamp) as event_date
    FROM {{ source('raw', 'error_logs') }}
    WHERE event_timestamp IS NOT NULL
      AND error_type IS NOT NULL
)

SELECT
    error_id,
    session_id,
    user_id,
    error_type,
    error_message,
    stack_trace_masked,
    component_name,
    feature_name,
    page_url,
    http_status_code,
    request_id,
    browser_name,
    browser_version,
    event_timestamp,
    event_date
FROM raw_data
```

# DIYAPP Evolution - V12 Core Architecture Specification
# Arquitetura de Microsserviços, Containers, CI/CD e Observabilidade

## 1. ESTRUTURA DE MICROSSERVIÇOS

## 2. ADR-001: ARQUITETURA DE MICROSSERVIÇOS

```markdown
# ADR-001: Arquitetura Baseada em Microsserviços com Kubernetes

Data: 2024-01-15
Status: Aceita
Autores: Tech Lead + Especialista Infra

CONTEXTO:
O DIYAPP precisa evoluir para uma arquitetura que suporte:
- Escalabilidade independente por componente
- Deploy contínuo sem downtime
- Isolamento de falhas
- Time de desenvolvimento paralelo (Modo Hive)

DECISÃO:
Adotar arquitetura de microsserviços com:
1. Kubernetes como orquestrador de containers
2. API Gateway como ponto único de entrada
3. Service Mesh (Istio) para comunicação entre serviços
4. Banco de dados por serviço (Database per Service)
5. Mensageria assíncrona (RabbitMQ) para eventos

OPÇÕES CONSIDERADAS:
- Opção A: Monolito modularizado
  Prós: Simplicidade inicial, transações ACID fáceis
  Contras: Escalabilidade limitada, acoplamento alto

- Opção B: Microsserviços com Kubernetes
  Prós: Escalabilidade independente, deploy contínuo, isolamento de falhas
  Contras: Complexidade operacional, necessidade de observabilidade robusta

- Opção escolhida: B - Justificativa: Alinha com requisitos de autonomia e escalabilidade

CONSEQUÊNCIAS:
Positivas:
- Cada squad pode desenvolver/deployar independentemente
- Escalabilidade granular por serviço
- Tecnologias heterogêneas possíveis

Negativas:
- Complexidade de deploy e monitoramento aumentada
- Necessidade de padrões rigorosos de comunicação
- Overhead de rede entre serviços

Riscos:
- Latência em chamadas entre serviços
- Gerenciamento de transações distribuídas
- Mitigação: Circuit breakers, retry policies, sagas

REVISÃO: 2024-04-15
```

## 3. PADRÕES DE CÓDIGO E ENGENHARIA

```javascript
// shared/libs/logger/index.js
const winston = require('winston');
const { v4: uuidv4 } = require('uuid');

class StructuredLogger {
  constructor(serviceName) {
    this.service = serviceName;
    this.correlationId = uuidv4();
    
    this.logger = winston.createLogger({
      level: process.env.LOG_LEVEL || 'info',
      format: winston.format.combine(
        winston.format.timestamp(),
        winston.format.json()
      ),
      defaultMeta: {
        service: this.service,
        correlationId: this.correlationId,
        environment: process.env.NODE_ENV
      },
      transports: [
        new winston.transports.Console(),
        new winston.transports.File({ 
          filename: `logs/${serviceName}-error.log`, 
          level: 'error' 
        }),
        new winston.transports.File({ 
          filename: `logs/${serviceName}-combined.log` 
        })
      ]
    });
  }

  info(message, metadata = {}) {
    this.logger.info(message, metadata);
  }

  error(message, error, metadata = {}) {
    this.logger.error(message, { 
      ...metadata, 
      error: {
        message: error.message,
        stack: error.stack,
        code: error.code
      }
    });
  }

  warn(message, metadata = {}) {
    this.logger.warn(message, metadata);
  }

  debug(message, metadata = {}) {
    this.logger.debug(message, metadata);
  }

  withCorrelation(correlationId) {
    this.correlationId = correlationId;
    return this;
  }
}

module.exports = StructuredLogger;
```

```javascript
// shared/libs/metrics/index.js
const client = require('prom-client');

class MetricsCollector {
  constructor() {
    this.register = new client.Registry();
    
    // Métricas padrão do Node.js
    client.collectDefaultMetrics({ register: this.register });
    
    // Métricas customizadas
    this.httpRequestDuration = new client.Histogram({
      name: 'http_request_duration_seconds',
      help: 'Duration of HTTP requests in seconds',
      labelNames: ['method', 'route', 'status_code', 'service'],
      buckets: [0.1, 0.5, 1, 2, 5]
    });

    this.serviceErrors = new client.Counter({
      name: 'service_errors_total',
      help: 'Total number of service errors',
      labelNames: ['service', 'error_type']
    });

    this.activeConnections = new client.Gauge({
      name: 'active_connections',
      help: 'Number of active connections',
      labelNames: ['service']
    });

    this.register.registerMetric(this.httpRequestDuration);
    this.register.registerMetric(this.serviceErrors);
    this.register.registerMetric(this.activeConnections);
  }

  observeRequest(method, route, statusCode, duration, service) {
    this.httpRequestDuration.observe(
      { method, route, status_code: statusCode, service },
      duration
    );
  }

  incrementError(service, errorType) {
    this.serviceErrors.inc({ service, error_type: errorType });
  }

  setConnections(service, count) {
    this.activeConnections.set({ service }, count);
  }

  async getMetrics() {
    return await this.register.metrics();
  }
}

module.exports = MetricsCollector;
```

## 4. DOCKERFILE PADRÃO PARA SERVIÇOS NODE.JS

```dockerfile
# services/user-service/Dockerfile
FROM node:18-alpine AS builder

WORKDIR /app

# Instala dependências de build
RUN apk add --no-cache python3 make g++

# Copia package files
COPY package*.json ./
COPY shared/libs/ ./shared/libs/

# Instala dependências
RUN npm ci --only=production

# Copia código fonte
COPY src/ ./src/
COPY tests/ ./tests/

# Usuário não-root para segurança
FROM node:18-alpine

WORKDIR /app

# Cria usuário não-root
RUN addgroup -g 1001 -S nodejs && \
    adduser -S nodejs -u 1001

# Copia dependências do builder
COPY --from=builder --chown=nodejs:nodejs /app/node_modules ./node_modules
COPY --from=builder --chown=nodejs:nodejs /app/src ./src
COPY --from=builder --chown=nodejs:nodejs /app/shared ./shared

# Configurações de saúde
HEALTHCHECK --interval=30s --timeout=3s --start-period=5s --retries=3 \
  CMD node src/health-check.js || exit 1

# Troca para usuário não-root
USER nodejs

# Expõe porta
EXPOSE 3000

# Comando de inicialização
CMD ["node", "src/server.js"]
```

## 5. DOCKER-COMPOSE PARA DESENVOLVIMENTO

```yaml
# infrastructure/docker-compose.yml
version: '3.8'

services:
  # Banco de dados
  postgres:
    image: postgres:15-alpine
    environment:
      POSTGRES_DB: diyapp
      POSTGRES_USER: diyapp_user
      POSTGRES_PASSWORD: ${DB_PASSWORD}
    volumes:
      - postgres_data:/var/lib/postgresql/data
    ports:
      - "5432:5432"
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD-SHELL", "pg_isready -U diyapp_user"]
      interval: 10s
      timeout: 5s
      retries: 5

  # Mensageria
  rabbitmq:
    image: rabbitmq:3.11-management-alpine
    environment:
      RABBITMQ_DEFAULT_USER: ${RABBITMQ_USER}
      RABBITMQ_DEFAULT_PASS: ${RABBITMQ_PASSWORD}
    ports:
      - "5672:5672"
      - "15672:15672"
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD", "rabbitmq-diagnostics", "ping"]
      interval: 30s
      timeout: 10s
      retries: 5

  # Cache
  redis:
    image: redis:7-alpine
    command: redis-server --requirepass ${REDIS_PASSWORD}
    ports:
      - "6379:6379"
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD", "redis-cli", "ping"]
      interval: 10s
      timeout: 5s
      retries: 5

  # Observabilidade
  prometheus:
    image: prom/prometheus:latest
    volumes:
      - ./infrastructure/monitoring/prometheus/prometheus.yml:/etc/prometheus/prometheus.yml
      - prometheus_data:/prometheus
    ports:
      - "9090:9090"
    command:
      - '--config.file=/etc/prometheus/prometheus.yml'
      - '--storage.tsdb.path=/prometheus'
      - '--web.console.libraries=/etc/prometheus/console_libraries'
      - '--web.console.templates=/etc/prometheus/consoles'
      - '--storage.tsdb.retention.time=200h'
      - '--web.enable-lifecycle'

  grafana:
    image: grafana/grafana:latest
    environment:
      GF_SECURITY_ADMIN_PASSWORD: ${GRAFANA_PASSWORD}
    volumes:
      - grafana_data:/var/lib/grafana
      - ./infrastructure/monitoring/grafana/dashboards:/etc/grafana/provisioning/dashboards
      - ./infrastructure/monitoring/grafana/datasources:/etc/grafana/provisioning/datasources
    ports:
      - "3001:3000"
    depends_on:
      prometheus:
        condition: service_healthy

  loki:
    image: grafana/loki:latest
    ports:
      - "3100:3100"
    command: -config.file=/etc/loki/local-config.yaml

  # Serviços DIYAPP
  api-gateway:
    build:
      context: ../services/api-gateway
      dockerfile: Dockerfile.dev
    environment:
      NODE_ENV: development
      PORT: 3000
      JWT_SECRET: ${JWT_SECRET}
      RABBITMQ_URL: amqp://rabbitmq:5672
      REDIS_URL: redis://redis:6379
    ports:
      - "3000:3000"
    depends_on:
      rabbitmq:
        condition: service_healthy
      redis:
        condition: service_healthy
    volumes:
      - ../services/api-gateway/src:/app/src
      - ../shared:/app/shared

  user-service:
    build:
      context: ../services/user-service
      dockerfile: Dockerfile.dev
    environment:
      NODE_ENV: development
      PORT: 3001
      DB_URL: postgresql://diyapp_user:${DB_PASSWORD}@postgres:5432/diyapp
      RABBITMQ_URL: amqp://rabbitmq:5672
    ports:
      - "3001:3001"
    depends_on:
      postgres:
        condition: service_healthy
      rabbitmq:
        condition: service_healthy
    volumes:
      - ../services/user-service/src:/app/src
      - ../shared:/app/shared

volumes:
  postgres_data:
  prometheus_data:
  grafana_data:
```

## 6. CI/CD PIPELINE (GITHUB ACTIONS)

```yaml
# .github/workflows/ci-pipeline.yml
name: CI Pipeline

on:
  push:
    branches: [ main, develop ]
  pull_request:
    branches: [ main ]

jobs:
  lint-and-test:
    name: Lint and Test
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    strategy:
      matrix:
        service: [api-gateway, user-service, task-service, notification-service, ai-orchestrator]
    
    steps:
    - name: Checkout code
      uses: actions/checkout@v3

    - name: Setup Node.js
      uses: actions/setup-node@v3
      with:
        node-version: '18'
        cache: 'npm'
        cache-dependency-path: services/${{ matrix.service }}/package-lock.json

    - name: Install dependencies
      run: |
        cd services/${{ matrix.service }}
        npm ci

    - name: Lint
      run: |
        cd services/${{ matrix.service }}
        npm run lint

    - name: Run tests
      run: |
        cd services/${{ matrix.service }}
        npm test -- --coverage
      
    - name: Upload coverage
      uses: codecov/codecov-action@v3
      with:
        file: services/${{ matrix.service }}/coverage/lcov.info
        flags: ${{ matrix.service }}

  security-scan:
    name: Security Scan
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    needs: lint-and-test
    
    steps:
    - name: Checkout code
      uses: actions/checkout@v3

    - name: Run Snyk to check for vulnerabilities
      uses: snyk/actions/node@master
      env:
        SNYK_TOKEN: ${{ secrets.SNYK_TOKEN }}
      with:
        args: --all-projects --severity-threshold=high

    - name: Run Trivy vulnerability scanner
      uses: aquasecurity/trivy-action@master
      with:
        scan-type: 'fs'
        scan-ref: '.'
        format: 'sarif'
        output: 'trivy-results.sarif'

    - name: Upload Trivy scan results to GitHub Security tab
      uses: github/codeql-action/upload-sarif@v2
      with:
        sarif_file: 'trivy-results.sarif'

  build-and-push:
    name: Build and Push Docker Images
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    needs: [lint-and-test, security-scan]
    if: github.event_name == 'push' && github.ref == 'refs/heads/main'
    
    steps:
    - name: Checkout code
      uses: actions/checkout@v3

    - name: Set up Docker Buildx
      uses: docker/setup-buildx-action@v2

    - name: Login to DockerHub
      uses: docker/login-action@v2
      with:
        username: ${{ secrets.DOCKER_USERNAME }}
        password: ${{ secrets.DOCKER_PASSWORD }}

    - name: Build and push
      uses: docker/build-push-action@v4
      with:
        context: .
        file: ./services/api-gateway/Dockerfile
        push: true
        tags: |
          ${{ secrets.DOCKER_USERNAME }}/diyapp-api-gateway:latest
          ${{ secrets.DOCKER_USERNAME }}/diyapp-api-gateway:${{ github.sha }}
        cache-from: type=gha
        cache-to: type=gha,mode=max
```

```yaml
# .github/workflows/cd-pipeline.yml
name: CD Pipeline

on:
  workflow_run:
    workflows: ["CI Pipeline"]
    branches: [main]
    types:
      - completed

jobs:
  deploy-staging:
    name: Deploy to Staging
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    if: ${{ github.event.workflow_run.conclusion == 'success' }}
    
    steps:
    - name: Checkout code
      uses: actions/checkout@v3

    - name: Configure

        }
        
        /* Progress Steps */
        .progress-steps {
            display: flex;
            justify-content: space-between;
            position: relative;
            margin-bottom: var(--spacing-8);
        }
        
        .progress-steps::before {
            content: '';
            position: absolute;
            top: 50%;
            left: 0;
            right: 0;
            height: 2px;
            background-color: var(--color-gray-300);
            transform: translateY(-50%);
            z-index: 1;
        }
        
        .progress-bar {
            position: absolute;
            top: 50%;
            left: 0;
            height: 2px;
            background-color: var(--color-primary-600);
            transform: translateY(-50%);
            z-index: 2;
            transition: width var(--transition-normal);
        }
        
        .step {
            position: relative;
            z-index: 3;
            display: flex;
            flex-direction: column;
            align-items: center;
            width: 6rem;
        }
        
        .step-circle {
            width: 2.5rem;
            height: 2.5rem;
            border-radius: var(--radius-full);
            background-color: white;
            border: 2px solid var(--color-gray-300);
            display: flex;
            align-items: center;
            justify-content: center;
            font-weight: var(--font-weight-semibold);
            color: var(--color-gray-500);
            margin-bottom: var(--spacing-2);
            transition: all var(--transition-normal);
        }
        
        .step.active .step-circle {
            border-color: var(--color-primary-600);
            background-color: var(--color-primary-600);
            color: white;
        }
        
        .step.completed .step-circle {
            border-color: var(--color-primary-600);
            background-color: var(--color-primary-600);
            color: white;
        }


### [Sessão Paralela: Backend]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V12 Core - Serviços Refatorados

## Estrutura do Projeto

```
diyapp-v12-core/
├── src/
│   ├── api-gateway/
│   ├── auth-service/
│   ├── task-service/
│   ├── shared/
│   └── index.js
├── public/
│   └── index.html
├── package.json
├── docker-compose.yml
├── .env.example
└── README.md

## 2. API Gateway Refatorado

**src/api-gateway/index.js**
```javascript
const express = require('express');
const helmet = require('helmet');
const cors = require('cors');
const rateLimit = require('express-rate-limit');
const compression = require('compression');
const winston = require('winston');
const axios = require('axios');
const CircuitBreaker = require('circuit-breaker-js');
const { createProxyMiddleware } = require('http-proxy-middleware');

class APIGateway {
  constructor() {
    this.app = express();
    this.port = process.env.API_GATEWAY_PORT || 3000;
    this.services = {
      auth: process.env.AUTH_SERVICE_URL || 'http://localhost:3001',
      tasks: process.env.TASKS_SERVICE_URL || 'http://localhost:3002'
    };
    
    this.logger = this.setupLogger();
    this.circuitBreakers = new Map();
    this.setupMiddleware();
    this.setupProxies();
    this.setupHealthChecks();
    this.setupErrorHandling();
  }

  setupLogger() {
    return winston.createLogger({
      level: process.env.LOG_LEVEL || 'info',
      format: winston.format.combine(
        winston.format.timestamp(),
        winston.format.json()
      ),
      transports: [
        new winston.transports.File({ filename: 'logs/api-gateway-error.log', level: 'error' }),
        new winston.transports.File({ filename: 'logs/api-gateway-combined.log' }),
        new winston.transports.Console({
          format: winston.format.simple()
        })
      ]
    });
  }

  setupMiddleware() {
    // Security middleware
    this.app.use(helmet());
    this.app.use(cors({
      origin: process.env.CORS_ORIGIN || '*',
      credentials: true
    }));
    
    // Rate limiting
    const limiter = rateLimit({
      windowMs: 15 * 60 * 1000, // 15 minutes
      max: 100, // Limit each IP to 100 requests per windowMs
      message: 'Too many requests from this IP, please try again later.',
      standardHeaders: true,
      legacyHeaders: false
    });
    this.app.use('/api/', limiter);
    
    // Compression
    this.app.use(compression());
    
    // Request logging
    this.app.use((req, res, next) => {
      const correlationId = req.headers['x-correlation-id'] || require('uuid').v4();
      req.correlationId = correlationId;
      res.setHeader('x-correlation-id', correlationId);
      
      this.logger.info({
        correlationId,
        method: req.method,
        url: req.url,
        userAgent: req.get('user-agent'),
        ip: req.ip
      });
      
      const start = Date.now();
      res.on('finish', () => {
        const duration = Date.now() - start;
        this.logger.info({
          correlationId,
          statusCode: res.statusCode,
          durationMs: duration,
          contentLength: res.get('content-length')
        });
      });
      
      next();
    });
    
    // Body parsing
    this.app.use(express.json({ limit: '10mb' }));
    this.app.use(express.urlencoded({ extended: true, limit: '10mb' }));
  }

  getCircuitBreaker(serviceName) {
    if (!this.circuitBreakers.has(serviceName)) {
      const breaker = new CircuitBreaker({
        timeoutDuration: 5000,
        errorThreshold: 50,
        volumeThreshold: 10,
        onCircuitOpen: () => {
          this.logger.warn(`Circuit breaker opened for ${serviceName}`);
        },
        onCircuitClose: () => {
          this.logger.info(`Circuit breaker closed for ${serviceName}`);
        }
      });
      this.circuitBreakers.set(serviceName, breaker);
    }
    return this.circuitBreakers.get(serviceName);
  }

  async callWithRetry(serviceName, url, config, retries = 3) {
    const breaker = this.getCircuitBreaker(serviceName);
    
    return breaker.run(async () => {
      for (let attempt = 1; attempt <= retries; attempt++) {
        try {
          const response = await axios({
            ...config,
            url,
            timeout: 10000,
            headers: {
              ...config.headers,
              'x-correlation-id': config.headers?.['x-correlation-id'] || require('uuid').v4()
            }
          });
          
          if (response.status >= 500) {
            throw new Error(`Service ${serviceName} returned ${response.status}`);
          }
          
          return response;
        } catch (error) {
          if (attempt === retries) {
            this.logger.error({
              service: serviceName,
              url,
              attempt,
              error: error.message,
              correlationId: config.headers?.['x-correlation-id']
            });
            throw error;
          }
          
          // Exponential backoff with jitter
          const delay = Math.min(1000 * Math.pow(2, attempt - 1) + Math.random() * 100, 10000);
          await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, delay));
          
          this.logger.warn({
            service: serviceName,
            url,
            attempt,
            retryInMs: delay,
            error: error.message
          });
        }
      }
    }, () => {
      // Fallback function when circuit is open
      return {
        status: 503,
        data: {
          error: 'Service temporarily unavailable',
          service: serviceName,
          timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
        }
      };
    });
  }

  setupProxies() {
    // Auth service proxy
    this.app.use('/api/v1/auth', async (req, res) => {
      try {
        const response = await this.callWithRetry('auth', `${this.services.auth}${req.url}`, {
          method: req.method,
          headers: {
            ...req.headers,
            'x-correlation-id': req.correlationId
          },
          data: req.body,
          params: req.query
        });
        
        res.status(response.status).json(response.data);
      } catch (error) {
        this.logger.error({
          correlationId: req.correlationId,
          error: error.message,
          stack: error.stack
        });
        
        res.status(500).json({
          error: 'Internal server error',
          correlationId: req.correlationId,
          timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
        });
      }
    });

    // Tasks service proxy
    this.app.use('/api/v1/tasks', async (req, res) => {
      try {
        // Validate authentication
        const authHeader = req.headers.authorization;
        if (!authHeader) {
          return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Authentication required' });
        }

        const response = await this.callWithRetry('tasks', `${this.services.tasks}${req.url}`, {
          method: req.method,
          headers: {
            ...req.headers,
            'x-correlation-id': req.correlationId
          },
          data: req.body,
          params: req.query
        });
        
        res.status(response.status).json(response.data);
      } catch (error) {
        this.logger.error({
          correlationId: req.correlationId,
          error: error.message,
          stack: error.stack
        });
        
        if (error.response) {
          res.status(error.response.status).json(error.response.data);
        } else {
          res.status(500).json({
            error: 'Internal server error',
            correlationId: req.correlationId,
            timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
          });
        }
      }
    });
  }

  setupHealthChecks() {
    this.app.get('/health', (req, res) => {
      res.json({
        status: 'healthy',
        timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
        uptime: process.uptime(),
        services: Object.keys(this.services).reduce((acc, service) => {
          acc[service] = this.circuitBreakers.get(service)?.isOpen() ? 'degraded' : 'healthy';
          return acc;
        }, {})
      });
    });

    this.app.get('/metrics', (req, res) => {
      const metrics = {
        requests: {
          total: this.requestCount || 0
        },
        circuit_breakers: Array.from(this.circuitBreakers.entries()).map(([service, breaker]) => ({
          service,
          state: breaker.isOpen() ? 'open' : 'closed',
          failure_count: breaker.stats.failures,
          success_count: breaker.stats.successes
        }))
      };
      res.json(metrics);
    });
  }

  setupErrorHandling() {
    // 404 handler
    this.app.use((req, res) => {
      res.status(404).json({
        error: 'Not found',
        path: req.url,
        method: req.method,
        correlationId: req.correlationId
      });
    });

    // Global error handler
    this.app.use((error, req, res, next) => {
      this.logger.error({
        correlationId: req.correlationId,
        error: error.message,
        stack: error.stack,
        url: req.url,
        method: req.method
      });

      res.status(error.status || 500).json({
        error: 'Internal server error',
        correlationId: req.correlationId,
        timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
      });
    });
  }

  start() {
    return new Promise((resolve) => {
      this.server = this.app.listen(this.port, () => {
        this.logger.info(`API Gateway running on port ${this.port}`);
        resolve();
      });
    });
  }

  async stop() {
    return new Promise((resolve) => {
      if (this.server) {
        this.server.close(() => {
          this.logger.info('API Gateway stopped');
          resolve();
        });
      } else {
        resolve();
      }
    });
  }
}

module.exports = APIGateway;
```

## 3. Serviço de Autenticação JWT/OAuth2

**src/auth-service/index.js**
```javascript
const express = require('express');
const jwt = require('jsonwebtoken');
const bcrypt = require('bcrypt');
const { Sequelize, DataTypes } = require('sequelize');
const winston = require('winston');
const Joi = require('joi');
const crypto = require('crypto');

class AuthService {
  constructor() {
    this.app = express();
    this.port = process.env.AUTH_SERVICE_PORT || 3001;
    this.jwtSecret = process.env.JWT_SECRET || crypto.randomBytes(64).toString('hex');
    this.jwtExpiry = process.env.JWT_EXPIRY || '24h';
    this.refreshTokenExpiry = process.env.REFRESH_TOKEN_EXPIRY || '7d';
    
    this.logger = this.setupLogger();
    this.db = this.setupDatabase();
    this.setupModels();
    this.setupMiddleware();
    this.setupRoutes();
    this.setupErrorHandling();
  }

  setupLogger() {
    return winston.createLogger({
      level: process.env.LOG_LEVEL || 'info',
      format: winston.format.combine(
        winston.format.timestamp(),
        winston.format.json()
      ),
      transports: [
        new winston.transports.File({ filename: 'logs/auth-service-error.log', level: 'error' }),
        new winston.transports.File({ filename: 'logs/auth-service-combined.log' }),
        new winston.transports.Console({
          format: winston.format.simple()
        })
      ]
    });
  }

  setupDatabase() {
    const sequelize = new Sequelize({
      dialect: 'sqlite',
      storage: process.env.DB_PATH || './data/auth.db',
      logging: (msg) => this.logger.debug(msg)
    });

    sequelize.authenticate()
      .then(() => this.logger.info('Database connected'))
      .catch(err => {
        this.logger.error('Database connection failed:', err);
        process.exit(1);
      });

    return sequelize;
  }

  setupModels() {
    this.User = this.db.define('User', {
      id: {
        type: DataTypes.UUID,
        defaultValue: DataTypes.UUIDV4,
        primaryKey: true
      },
      email: {
        type: DataTypes.STRING,
        allowNull: false,
        unique: true,
        validate: {
          isEmail: true
        }
      },
      passwordHash: {
        type: DataTypes.STRING,
        allowNull: false
      },
      name: {
        type: DataTypes.STRING,
        allowNull: false
      },
      role: {
        type: DataTypes.ENUM('user', 'admin', 'moderator'),
        defaultValue: 'user'
      },
      isActive: {
        type: DataTypes.BOOLEAN,
        defaultValue: true
      },
      lastLogin: {
        type: DataTypes.DATE
      },
      metadata: {
        type: DataTypes.JSON,
        defaultValue: {}
      }
    }, {
      indexes: [
        { fields: ['email'] },
        { fields: ['role'] },
        { fields: ['isActive'] }
      ]
    });

    this.RefreshToken = this.db.define('RefreshToken', {
      id: {
        type: DataTypes.UUID,
        defaultValue: DataTypes.UUIDV4,
        primaryKey: true
      },
      token: {
        type: DataTypes.STRING,
        allowNull: false,
        unique: true
      },
      userId: {
        type: DataTypes.UUID,
        allowNull: false
      },
      expiresAt: {
        type: DataTypes.DATE,
        allowNull: false
      },
      userAgent: {
        type: DataTypes.STRING
      },
      ipAddress: {
        type: DataTypes.STRING
      },
      isRevoked: {
        type: DataTypes.BOOLEAN,
        defaultValue: false
      }
    }, {
      indexes: [
        { fields: ['token'] },
        { fields: ['userId'] },
        { fields: ['expiresAt'] }
      ]
    });

    // Associations
    this.User.hasMany(this.RefreshToken, { foreignKey: 'userId' });
    this.RefreshToken.belongsTo(this.User, { foreignKey: 'userId' });
  }

  setupMiddleware() {
    this.app.use(express.json());
    
    // Request logging
    this.app.use((req, res, next) => {
      const correlationId = req.headers['x-correlation-id'] || require('uuid').v4();
      req.correlationId = correlationId;
      
      this.logger.info({
        correlationId,
        service: 'auth',
        method: req.method,
        endpoint: req.url,
        userAgent: req.get('user-agent'),
        ip: req.ip
      });
      
      next();
    });
  }

  setupRoutes() {
    // Validation schemas
    const registerSchema = Joi.object({
      email: Joi.string().email().required(),
      password: Joi.string().min(8).required(),
      name: Joi.string().min(2).required(),
      metadata: Joi.object().optional()
    });

    const loginSchema = Joi.object({
      email: Joi.string().email().required(),
      password: Joi.string().required()
    });

    const refreshSchema = Joi.object({
      refreshToken: Joi.string().required()
    });

    // Register endpoint
    this.app.post('/api/v1/auth/register', async (req, res) => {
      try {
        const { error, value } = registerSchema.validate(req.body);
        if (error) {
          return res.status(400).json({
            error: 'Validation failed',
            details: error.d

### [Sessão Paralela: Frontend]

```tsx
// src/design-system/tokens.ts
export const tokens = {
  colors: {
    primary: {
      50: '#eff6ff',
      100: '#dbeafe',
      200: '#bfdbfe',
      300: '#93c5fd',
      400: '#60a5fa',
      500: '#3b82f6',
      600: '#2563eb',
      700: '#1d4ed8',
      800: '#1e40af',
      900: '#1e3a8a',
    },
    secondary: {
      50: '#f8fafc',
      100: '#f1f5f9',
      200: '#e2e8f0',
      300: '#cbd5e1',
      400: '#94a3b8',
      500: '#64748b',
      600: '#475569',
      700: '#334155',
      800: '#1e293b',
      900: '#0f172a',
    },
    success: '#22c55e',
    warning: '#eab308',
    error: '#ef4444',
    surface: {
      light: '#ffffff',
      dark: '#0f172a',
      card: '#f8fafc',
    }
  },
  spacing: {
    xs: '0.5rem',
    sm: '1rem',
    md: '1.5rem',
    lg: '2rem',
    xl: '3rem',
    '2xl': '4rem',
  },
  typography: {
    fontFamily: {
      sans: 'system-ui, -apple-system, sans-serif',
      mono: 'monospace',
    },
    fontSize: {
      xs: '0.75rem',
      sm: '0.875rem',
      base: '1rem',
      lg: '1.125rem',
      xl: '1.25rem',
      '2xl': '1.5rem',
      '3xl': '1.875rem',
      '4xl': '2.25rem',
    },
    fontWeight: {
      normal: '400',
      medium: '500',
      semibold: '600',
      bold: '700',
    },
  },
  borderRadius: {
    sm: '0.25rem',
    md: '0.5rem',
    lg: '0.75rem',
    xl: '1rem',
    full: '9999px',
  },
  shadows: {
    sm: '0 1px 2px 0 rgb(0 0 0 / 0.05)',
    md: '0 4px 6px -1px rgb(0 0 0 / 0.1)',
    lg: '0 10px 15px -3px rgb(0 0 0 / 0.1)',
  },
  zIndex: {
    dropdown: 1000,
    modal: 2000,
    toast: 3000,
  },
} as const;

export type ColorToken = keyof typeof tokens.colors;
export type SpacingToken = keyof typeof tokens.spacing;
export type TypographyToken = keyof typeof tokens.typography.fontSize;
```

```tsx
// src/store/useAppStore.ts
import { create } from 'zustand';
import { persist } from 'zustand/middleware';
import { io, Socket } from 'socket.io-client';

export interface User {
  id: string;
  name: string;
  email: string;
  avatar?: string;
  role: 'admin' | 'user' | 'viewer';
}

export interface DashboardModule {
  id: string;
  name: string;
  description: string;
  icon: string;
  component: string;
  enabled: boolean;
  order: number;
}

export interface RealTimeEvent {
  id: string;
  type: 'notification' | 'data_update' | 'system_alert';
  title: string;
  message: string;
  timestamp: Date;
  read: boolean;
}

interface AppState {
  // User state
  user: User | null;
  isAuthenticated: boolean;
  
  // Dashboard state
  modules: DashboardModule[];
  activeModule: string;
  sidebarCollapsed: boolean;
  
  // Real-time state
  socket: Socket | null;
  realTimeEvents: RealTimeEvent[];
  connectionStatus: 'connected' | 'connecting' | 'disconnected' | 'error';
  
  // Actions
  setUser: (user: User | null) => void;
  setModules: (modules: DashboardModule[]) => void;
  setActiveModule: (moduleId: string) => void;
  toggleSidebar: () => void;
  
  // Real-time actions
  connectSocket: (url: string) => void;
  disconnectSocket: () => void;
  addRealTimeEvent: (event: Omit<RealTimeEvent, 'id' | 'timestamp' | 'read'>) => void;
  markEventAsRead: (eventId: string) => void;
  clearEvents: () => void;
}

export const useAppStore = create<AppState>()(
  persist(
    (set, get) => ({
      // Initial state
      user: null,
      isAuthenticated: false,
      modules: [],
      activeModule: 'overview',
      sidebarCollapsed: false,
      socket: null,
      realTimeEvents: [],
      connectionStatus: 'disconnected',

      // User actions
      setUser: (user) => set({ 
        user, 
        isAuthenticated: !!user 
      }),

      // Dashboard actions
      setModules: (modules) => set({ modules }),
      setActiveModule: (moduleId) => set({ activeModule: moduleId }),
      toggleSidebar: () => set((state) => ({ 
        sidebarCollapsed: !state.sidebarCollapsed 
      })),

      // Real-time actions
      connectSocket: (url: string) => {
        const socket = io(url, {
          transports: ['websocket'],
          reconnection: true,
          reconnectionAttempts: 5,
          reconnectionDelay: 1000,
        });

        socket.on('connect', () => {
          set({ connectionStatus: 'connected' });
          console.log('WebSocket connected');
        });

        socket.on('disconnect', () => {
          set({ connectionStatus: 'disconnected' });
        });

        socket.on('connect_error', (error) => {
          set({ connectionStatus: 'error' });
          console.error('WebSocket connection error:', error);
        });

        socket.on('notification', (data: any) => {
          get().addRealTimeEvent({
            type: 'notification',
            title: data.title,
            message: data.message,
          });
        });

        socket.on('data_update', (data: any) => {
          get().addRealTimeEvent({
            type: 'data_update',
            title: 'Data Updated',
            message: data.message,
          });
        });

        set({ socket, connectionStatus: 'connecting' });
      },

      disconnectSocket: () => {
        const { socket } = get();
        if (socket) {
          socket.disconnect();
          set({ socket: null, connectionStatus: 'disconnected' });
        }
      },

      addRealTimeEvent: (event) => set((state) => ({
        realTimeEvents: [
          {
            ...event,
            id: Date.now().toString(),
            timestamp: new Date(),
            read: false,
          },
          ...state.realTimeEvents.slice(0, 49), // Keep last 50 events
        ],
      })),

      markEventAsRead: (eventId) => set((state) => ({
        realTimeEvents: state.realTimeEvents.map((event) =>
          event.id === eventId ? { ...event, read: true } : event
        ),
      })),

      clearEvents: () => set({ realTimeEvents: [] }),
    }),
    {
      name: 'diyapp-storage',
      partialize: (state) => ({
        user: state.user,
        modules: state.modules,
        activeModule: state.activeModule,
        sidebarCollapsed: state.sidebarCollapsed,
      }),
    }
  )
);
```

```tsx
// src/components/layout/Sidebar.tsx
import React from 'react';
import { NavLink } from 'react-router-dom';
import { useAppStore, DashboardModule } from '../../store/useAppStore';
import { tokens } from '../../design-system/tokens';
import clsx from 'clsx';

interface SidebarProps {
  modules: DashboardModule[];
}

export const Sidebar: React.FC<SidebarProps> = ({ modules }) => {
  const { sidebarCollapsed, toggleSidebar } = useAppStore();

  return (
    <aside
      className={clsx(
        'flex flex-col h-full transition-all duration-300',
        'bg-surface-card border-r border-secondary-200',
        sidebarCollapsed ? 'w-20' : 'w-64'
      )}
      style={{
        backgroundColor: tokens.colors.surface.card,
        borderColor: tokens.colors.secondary[200],
      }}
      aria-label="Main navigation"
    >
      {/* Logo */}
      <div className="flex items-center justify-between p-4 border-b border-secondary-200">
        {!sidebarCollapsed && (
          <div className="flex items-center space-x-3">
            <div 
              className="w-8 h-8 rounded-lg"
              style={{ backgroundColor: tokens.colors.primary[600] }}
              aria-hidden="true"
            />
            <h1 
              className="text-xl font-bold truncate"
              style={{ color: tokens.colors.secondary[900] }}
            >
              DIYAPP V12
            </h1>
          </div>
        )}
        {sidebarCollapsed && (
          <div 
            className="w-8 h-8 rounded-lg mx-auto"
            style={{ backgroundColor: tokens.colors.primary[600] }}
            aria-label="DIYAPP Logo"
          />
        )}
        <button
          onClick={toggleSidebar}
          className={clsx(
            'p-2 rounded-lg hover:bg-secondary-100 transition-colors',
            'focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-primary-500'
          )}
          aria-label={sidebarCollapsed ? 'Expand sidebar' : 'Collapse sidebar'}
          style={{
            color: tokens.colors.secondary[600],
          }}
        >
          {sidebarCollapsed ? '→' : '←'}
        </button>
      </div>

      {/* Navigation */}
      <nav className="flex-1 p-4 overflow-y-auto">
        <ul className="space-y-2">
          {modules
            .filter((module) => module.enabled)
            .sort((a, b) => a.order - b.order)
            .map((module) => (
              <li key={module.id}>
                <NavLink
                  to={`/dashboard/${module.id}`}
                  className={({ isActive }) =>
                    clsx(
                      'flex items-center rounded-lg px-3 py-2.5 transition-all',
                      'hover:bg-primary-50 focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-primary-500',
                      isActive
                        ? 'bg-primary-50 text-primary-700'
                        : 'text-secondary-700 hover:text-primary-600'
                    )
                  }
                  style={({ isActive }) => ({
                    backgroundColor: isActive ? tokens.colors.primary[50] : 'transparent',
                    color: isActive ? tokens.colors.primary[700] : tokens.colors.secondary[700],
                  })}
                >
                  <span 
                    className="text-lg mr-3"
                    style={{ color: 'inherit' }}
                    aria-hidden="true"
                  >
                    {module.icon}
                  </span>
                  {!sidebarCollapsed && (
                    <span className="truncate font-medium">{module.name}</span>
                  )}
                </NavLink>
              </li>
            ))}
        </ul>
      </nav>

      {/* Connection Status */}
      <div className="p-4 border-t border-secondary-200">
        <div className="flex items-center justify-center">
          <div className="flex items-center space-x-2">
            <div 
              className="w-2 h-2 rounded-full animate-pulse"
              style={{ backgroundColor: tokens.colors.success }}
              aria-hidden="true"
            />
            {!sidebarCollapsed && (
              <span 
                className="text-sm"
                style={{ color: tokens.colors.secondary[600] }}
              >
                Connected
              </span>

## 1. Esquema do Data Warehouse (BigQuery/Snowflake)

### 1.1 Arquivo: `dbt/models/raw/raw__app_events.sql`
```sql
{{ config(
    materialized='incremental',
    unique_key='event_id',
    partition_by={
      "field": "event_timestamp",
      "data_type": "timestamp",
      "granularity": "day"
    },
    cluster_by = ["event_type", "user_id"]
) }}

SELECT
  event_id,
  user_id,
  session_id,
  event_type,
  event_name,
  event_properties,
  page_url,
  referrer_url,
  user_agent,
  device_type,
  browser,
  os,
  screen_resolution,
  ip_address,
  country_code,
  region,
  city,
  event_timestamp,
  ingested_at
FROM {{ source('app_telemetry', 'app_events') }}

{% if is_incremental() %}
WHERE event_timestamp > (SELECT MAX(event_timestamp) FROM {{ this }})
{% endif %}
```

### 1.2 Arquivo: `dbt/models/raw/raw__performance_metrics.sql`
```sql
{{ config(
    materialized='incremental',
    unique_key='metric_id',
    partition_by={
      "field": "metric_timestamp",
      "data_type": "timestamp",
      "granularity": "hour"
    },
    cluster_by = ["metric_name", "page_url"]
) }}

SELECT
  metric_id,
  session_id,
  page_url,
  metric_name,
  metric_value,
  metric_unit,
  -- Core Web Vitals
  lcp,
  fid,
  cls,
  inp,
  ttfb,
  fcp,
  -- Resource timing
  dom_content_loaded,
  window_load,
  first_paint,
  -- Custom metrics
  custom_metrics,
  metric_timestamp,
  ingested_at
FROM {{ source('app_telemetry', 'performance_metrics') }}

{% if is_incremental() %}
WHERE metric_timestamp > (SELECT MAX(metric_timestamp) FROM {{ this }})
{% endif %}
```

FROM {{ source('app_telemetry', 'error_logs') }}

{{ config(
